et lieve le keur qui est endroit la mice, ou li coutes dou malaide vient devers senestre, et soit li elevations dont tu lieves le keur selonc la keur, selonc la longesce dou cors, et li cautere soient selonc la largesce dou cors.	And raise the heart that is at the mouse, where the cost of the patient comes towards the left, and let the elevation be according to the height of the body, and the width of the cautery should be according to the breadth of the body.
Aprés i boute les II ners enflamez tant que li keurs soit perciez de l’autre part, et puis trai fuers le cautere, et ensi en i avra IIII.	Afterwards, thrust the two flaming edges so that the heart is pierced from the other side, then pull out the cautery, and thus there will be four.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize a tot le cautere a III ners.	And if you wish, cauterize with all three edges of the cautery.
Aprés le cure quant il a geteit porriture par lonc tens, et ce vaut mues que li autre des cures devant dites.	After this treatment, if it has thrown off corruption over a long period of time, then it is better than the other treatments mentioned earlier.
de ydropisie	of dropsy
Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	A fire cautery is not suitable for a dropsical person, except in the manner called "ascites.
Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis;	When you treat according to the methods that we have mentioned in divisions, and your treatment does not help, then it is necessary for you to make four cauteries around the neck, one on the stomach, one on the liver, one at the mouse, and two behind the back on the spine, and one near the breast;
et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur.	And let the cautery be placed close to the spearhead of the heart.
Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere;	Afterwards, leave the cautery open for some time to expel corruption, and do not neglect the patient's care after the cautery.
et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les II ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	And healing would hasten, and both intentions would be together with God’s help.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit;	The form of the cautery for the belly is the one we have shown before.
et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	And that for the back be olive-shaped, as it is depicted here.
de l’enfleure des piez	Edema of the feet
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire;	When the feet of one suffering from dropsy are swollen and filled with yellow water, you must cauterize on the back of the foot between the little toe and the ring toe.
et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	And lift your hand with the cautery without turning it.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	And do not enter too deeply at first; thus one would avoid causing injury like that caused by the aw within the citrine, and let the cauterization be done according to this form:
Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire;	Then make two cauteries on each leg at the point of the shinbone.
et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe;	And let the cautery be long, one below the knee in front and the other behind, in the middle of the leg.
et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse;	And let fire cauteries remain on longer without being cleaned until they are discharged.
aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	After treating other wounds as we have described.
de la menoison	Of the dislocation
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures;	When an attack of colic comes from coldness and dampness, so that the retaining and digestive powers in the stomach and intestines are weakened, and cannot be cured by ordinary remedies;
et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule;	And you see the patient suffering greatly and having strong virtue, then make a large cautery on the stomach according to what was spoken of previously in the cautery for the stomach, using the circular cautery.
et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	And four small cauteries around the navel like one cautery on each side of the spine, and two cauteries on the hips.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et .i. cautere sus chaicun yle, et .ij. petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	"And if you see the moistures abundant and the patient suffering, make them a cautery on the point, and one cautery on each side, and two small cauteries on the stomach near the large one, for the treatment is beneficial when there is good aid."
de la cure des emorroydes	"Of the Cure of Hemorrhoids"
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres:	When hemorrhoids are on the anus, one or more, and are old and consist of thick corrupt cold and moist humors, and have been treated by division as we have said without success, then apply cauteries:
III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois;	III upon the spine of the back, that which is all deflected below toward the shoulder-blade little by little in a triangle shape, and [apply] the cautery beneath the armpit II times;
et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile;	and if you think that its stomach is cooled, and the flesh does not cook, and one sees the face swell, then apply one great cautery to the stomach as it is stated before, and another to the liver, and another to the spleen at all cautery points
et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	and let the cautery remain on for a long time.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	Afterwards, heal the place until it is clean.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	"Of the Fleshy Growth Called 'Thelul'"
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit;	When you cut into fat tissue, heat the cautery that resembles a razor, and then place it all ablaze upon that cut fat.
et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort;	and let your hand remain there until the cautery reaches the opening of the vein, where the blood flows out
fai ceu une fois ou II, et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit;	do this once or twice, and if there is much fat tissue, cauterize each one as we have said
aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez;	afterwards, use ointments to aid in healing until they are clean.
et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	And if you cauterize with a large cautery on alcatraz, it will have greater help.
de plaie mal curee	"Of a Wound Poorly Treated"
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When the patient cannot bear cutting or opening,
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	When a fistula occurs and becomes inflamed and filled with rottenness and corrupted moisture, you should probe it gently with the tip of your finger, ensuring that you know the full depth of the opening.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing;	And after heating the cautery which resembles a razor, put it into the fistula according to the quantity that the tent entered there, and begin again with the cautery until those corrupt and rotten bodies are burned, once or twice or three times, depending on what is needed.
et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	And beware of burning the nerves that are nearby, and the large veins.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans;	If the fistula goes to the body of the bladder and the intestines, then beware of these places, and do not perform this operation except in a fleshy area, and think that it is not persistent.
aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement;	Then heal the place until it is clean, and if the place is healed, and the matter has been removed for a long time, then know that the place is entirely healthy.
et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font;	And if the matter is not removed, know that the place is wounded, and the bone at the front is rotting.
et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	And so like one of those we will mention later.
de la maladie des reins	Of the disease of the kidneys
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit;	When pain from cold comes to the kidneys, and from great flatulence, and she does not menstruate, then you must perform a fire cautery on her kidneys on both sides with the clavicle cautery that we have mentioned before.
et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra III cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	And if we cauterize it in the middle, it will have three cauteries in a row, and this will provide greater relief.
de la vessie	Of the bladder
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et I a destre et I a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce;	When the bladder is weak and flaccid from cold and moisture so that the patient retains urine, then perform cautery on the front part of the bladder where the pubic hair begins, one on the right side and one on the left side, with each cautery being as long as a barleycorn.
et li fais I cautere defuers le dos, ou II se tu en as besoing;	And perform one cautery at the back if necessary.
et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	And let the clavicle cautery be according to the shape mentioned before.
de la marris	Of the marrow
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde;	When the womb is cold and moist, preventing conception due to this reason, and the menstrual flow is corrupt with delayed periods,
et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor:	and when they come, great pain is felt:
adonques covient il c’on li faice III cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et II cauteres defuers le dos;	then it is necessary that one performs three cauteries around the bladder, as we have said regarding the cautery of the bladder, and two cauteries behind the back:
et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	and the cautery should be performed with a hot iron, as we have said.
de la hainche	Of the hair
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble;	When viscous moisture descends to the hip joint, and for this reason it moves from its place, and the sign is that one thigh appears longer than the other when measured together;
et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle;	and the location of the joint's separation is found, then you must cauterize the patient around the hip joint with one circular cautery, and seal around the joint as it turns, so that the joint is inside the circle;
et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	and let the cautery be like those used to cauterize the stomach.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai III cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs;	And if this cautery is not available, then perform three large olive-shaped cauteries, and let the cautery be as deep as all the others;
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and let him rest until he is healed
de la dolor de la hainche	Of the pain in the hair
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene:	When pain comes to the small of the back due to coldness and dampness, and the patient has been treated with what we have mentioned in the division but is not cured, and the disease is chronic:
adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	Then you must purge the patient of thick humors using fetid pills or similar good pills.
Aprés li fai cautere;	Afterward apply a cautery;
et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres:	and the manner of the cautery is in two ways:
c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	namely, hot remedies together with fire cautery.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz:	Fire cautery has many ways, one of which is this:
que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire;	such that you cauterize the small of the back with three triangular cauteries according to this shape, and they should be deeply and widely made, and there should be the width of two fingers between each cautery, and the cauteries should be olive-shaped.
aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	Sometimes one cauterizes in the middle upon the top of the small of the back, for which there are four cauteries according to this shape:
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche;	And if you wish, cauterize it with the circular cautery which we have mentioned previously for the dislocation of the hip joint.
mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	but do it in such a way that the circle contains the entire hip joint, and all the spokes of the heart are burned
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	And this is the manner in which it is done for sciatica, when the pain holds at the hip and does not reach the thigh or the leg.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc;	And if it extends to the thigh and leg, apply two cauteries where the patient feels pain, and one cautery above the ankle on the left side
et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur;	and let the cauteries be ellipsoidal, and let the thickness of the heart be burned.
et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	and if the patient feels that pain extends to two fingers' width from the foot or further, cauterize where they feel pain three times or four with a cautery called "points".
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus;	And if necessary, do more.
et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	And if the pain is felt below the knee towards the thigh, apply a cautery with an ellipsoidal or circular cautery, and take care in all your cauteries not to leave the cautery on too long so that you burn the nerves and large arteries, and do not cause greater harm and contraction to the patient.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	And I myself have seen many who have performed cautery on the ankle of the foot, and they left it until the whole leg was swollen, and the foot likewise, and it became perforated and corrupted completely.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	After a bellyache that resulted in death.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	And if the pain is in both parts together, perform cautery on one and the other, according to this manner.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce;	And the wise say in cauterizing hair, of which this is the method: make such iron and let it be at the head as thick as a hazelnut or somewhat less, and let it be perforated and let there be spaces between each perforation equal to the thickness of a hazelnut.
et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait;	And let the perforations be open at both ends, like nuts, and let there be many well-made iron pieces;
et c’est li forme:	This is the shape:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit;	And let it be heated until it is entirely red-hot and then place it on the diseased scalp, turning it towards the sound side;
et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors;	and cauterize once with one cautery, and leave it three days;
et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens;	And then make an ointment of butter and let the wound remain open for a long time;
aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	after treating with ointment until it is healed.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent;	Albucasis says that we use this cautery little because of its great heat, and few see those who use it;
et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	And furthermore this is one of the good cauteries which he can withstand; and at the place where it adheres.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi;	And the cauterizing iron for burning is such that you make an instrument with interlaced openings in which the edges of the door descend, and it should be of brass or iron on one flat side, and have two nuts at the top, each separated by the quantity of a finger.
et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	and let them be turned over and open above, and join together according to this shape:
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche;	Then place the box of the poultice on the sick person lying on their healthy side, and press your hand firmly on top of the box.
aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	Then place between the two circles of the hot awl which has been heated in the fire for a little while, and let it sit there for an hour of time, and let the patient bear the heat and burning from it.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu;	For it finds biting like that of fire.
et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit;	And when the blisters have passed, raise your hand with the instrument and lift the hair from the wound gently, and leave it thus for three days, and apply butter until what is blackened by the burn is gone.
et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait;	And leave it for three days until corruption comes out of it.
et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	And this would be the final help after the treatment with ointments, as long as it is healed.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument;	And if the pain has spread to the thigh or leg, make another instrument like the one you used on the wound and increase it accordingly.
et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	And this is the manner of the hot cautery, which I have written about in the treatment of medicine.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	Take quicklime and live chalk, an equal amount of each, grind them together, and place them in nine pots.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir;	where there is a small hole through which the point of a razor can enter;
et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main;	And put another well-sealed pot over it and place quicklime and hot water and gentle heat on top until there are two fingers' width of powder when you press it in your hand.
et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	And let it be thus until it descends with water and iron or lead, then take all that water and throw it onto heat and into alkali as before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres.	Then it will be very hot and administered in many works of medicine and cauteries on other members.
Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	But it performs the same work as fire, and has other medicines with which one may cauterize the hair well, such as treacle and myrobalan honey, heat with soap, all these things mixed together.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	And Galen tells us of a cure where a man was healed from the pain in his hair and sciatic vein. He praised it greatly, saying that no other treatment was needed, and the man was completely cured after just one application, as described below:
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie;	And say in this way that you take fresh and dry green copper vitriol, grind it much with a spoonful of fat, place it on the hair, thigh, and leg where the pain resides, and let it sit;
et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	and leave it for three hours until the patient no longer feels burning.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	Then have him enter a bath until his body is somewhat warmed, and lay him in bed; then the pain will all go away and he will be healthy.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	And know that no one should use a cautery with such medicines unless after an evacuation of blood.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout;	And Dioscorides says that when the sciatic vein is cauterized with goat's gall, it helps much;
et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	And the cautery must be applied in this manner.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	Take linen, anoint it with old oil, and place it on the hollow between the big toe of the foot and the one called the cuboid.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains;	After taking dry goat hair, set it on fire until it becomes charcoal; then put it on wool and let it stay until it is extinguished.
et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee;	and do this again in the same way; do not stop doing this until you think it is time to reach the hair and the pain has stopped.
et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	This method of cautery is called "goat's cautery".
de la dolor dou dos	of the pain in the back
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back, whether from falling or impact or from too great an evacuation, or from signs of spread cold matter, none of these signs warrant cauterization except for that which comes from infusion of cold matter.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir;	After the patient is emptied of fetid pills or similar substances, one should perform three rows of five cauteries or more on their back where the pain is located, depending on the strength and amount that the patient can tolerate.
et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»;	And the cauteries should be performed using a cautery called "the point".
et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	If you see fit, perform three or four cauteries on the middle clavicle according to this shape:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor;	Frequently this disease affects young children; its beginning is marked by them having a narrow gait when they stand up, and fear;
et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	And you find in the lower spine of the back, near to the appearance that comes upon the other spines.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this, if you wish to cure it, then cauterize with the clavicle cautery according to this form:
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	So that the cautery may evenly burn each part of the spine.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	And if you see fit, cauterize around the spine with a cautery point that burns two or three lines deep, and let the points be close together.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	Then heal the place until it is clean according to what we have said, and make sure you do not apply cautery on any gibbosity that is near a nerve.
de la dolor des jointes	of pain in the joints
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere:	When pain in the joints comes from moistures that are spread throughout each member of the body; and when pain comes into the feet, which doctors properly call 'podagra'; and when it is from a cold cause and cannot be cured by medicines, then it is treated with cauterization in this manner:
fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	Make many cauteries around the ankle joint, and let the cautery be olive-shaped according to this form:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	And if it is necessary to prick the face of the foot, use the cautery called "point".
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire;	And if the pains extend to the knees and other joints, which happens often, then make three or four cauteries on each knee, all olive-shaped.
et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if you need more, then make them; but do not hold your hand far from it until the point of the knife is burned.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	And if the pains descend to the knees and back, then administer the cautery that we have mentioned in our chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes;	And if the pains are at the hands, then make prickings around the fist two lines;
et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main;	If there remains no pain in the fingers, then make prickings on each joint and on the hair of the hand;
et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	And if the pains come up to the elbows or up to the shoulders, then cauterize each part, and have good care of the patient and take medicine.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	But if you provide good care and purge phlegm, he will be healed with the help of God.
de la routure dou syfac	"on the rupture of the scrotum"
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor;	When rupture comes to the anus, and the bowels descend to the hips which is recently happened, then it is necessary that when you see him cure, he should not eat that day;
et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre;	And that he use things that leave the stomach empty so that the feces descend from his belly;
aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors;	Afterwards make him sit on his back between your hands, and command him to hold his ankle until the bowels are replaced, and then move them to his thighs, and press firmly below the rupture onto the bone of the wrist, and there will be a sign like half a circle above the body;
puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	Then heat the cautery whose shape is described here:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	Until it becomes white and casts shadows.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu;	Then reset the bowels to their place
et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier;	and the attendant shall keep his hand upon them so that they do not slip back
et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains;	and open the patient's thighs wide, place a cushion and two blankets beneath them, and another one on their chest to keep their hands warm
puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os;	then place the cautery on the sign with your whole hand, holding it with your right hand and pressing until you reach the bone, and if you do not reach it the first time, try again until you feel the bone
et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere;	and be careful that the bowel does not slip out while performing the cautery
que tu ne le brulasses;	lest you burn it
et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	or else the patient dies or suffers some other harm.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And know that if you do not reach the bone with the cautery, your efforts are worth nothing.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure;	And the cauteries for children must be thin according to their size, and those for adults large enough according to theirs
aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	after three days, treat the wound from the cautery with butter until the burn is healed
aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee;	After treating other wounds until they are clean, let the patient lie on their back for 40 days until the wound is well healed.
et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	And it is necessary that his bindings be left on for a long time so that his bowels do not protrude when he gets up to go to bed.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors;	And after 40 days, when he wishes to rise, provide him with a well-made bandage and let him wear it for another 40 days.
et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire;	And let him have good rest, working little and guarding against excessive consumption of drink and food, and against loud laughter.
et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	And when he follows this instruction, he will be entirely healed.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	And I shall tell you after the cure of cutting in its chapter.
de la routure dou ventre	Here is how to perform a laparotomy:
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur;	When fistulas appear in other bellies and are known to be growing, if you see that they are not increasing any further, apply a cautery iron according to their size, and burn the third of the heart.
aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit;	After treating according to what we have said;
et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	And some of the ancients have said that it should be cauterized with the cautery at three angles according to this form:
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	But first mark the point of beginning and draw a line across the width above the rupture, and another below it, and then cauterize with your hand in the middle at all points.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	But the first cauteries are lighter and gentler.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	"From ancient pain in a certain limb"
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	If pain comes to any limb, from falling or striking, and that pain persists for a long time, and medical treatments do not help, then it must be cauterized with the cautery called 'poins', and the cautery should be performed according to the length of the limb and its size, weakness, strength, location of twists, and the nature of the pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien;	If it is without the first cautery, that's good;
se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	If not, then recommence another cautery on top of it, for it is customary that it must move to the limb that it is near, so you should make the cauteries until the patient is healed.
de meselerie	"Of dislocation"
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	Some cases are sometimes helped by cautery with great benefit, especially those diseases that arise from the putrefaction of phlegm and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief:	When cauterizing the eye, be careful if the disease is at its beginning; and if it is cured according to what we have said in the division, and neither descends nor remains, and you doubt that corruption may spread throughout the patient, then make five cauteries on top of it
I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous;	One at the nape of the neck, and another towards the forehead at the end of the eyebrows;
et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel;	And two on each horn, and one behind on the hairet;
et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir;	And leave your hand there until the cautery reaches the bone, and until the scabs come out so that the vapors of the thick humors can escape.
et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	And cauterize the mouse according to what is written beforehand.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse;	And if the swelling is widespread;
et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules;	And if it is clear that [the swelling] is present, then you should cauterize [the patient] with these cauteries that we have mentioned: one at the head, and one near the neck, and two on the spine of the neck, and six on the spine of the back, and one large one on the breastbone and another nearby, and two on the shoulders;
et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains;	And two on the ribs, and two on the tendons of the foot, and one on each joint of the hands and feet, and on the hollows of the hands;
et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler;	and beware of the nerves that are behind the heel bone, so that you do not burn them;
et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	And sometimes one cautery is made on the wrist bone, and another on the stomach bone, and another on the liver.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite;	And know that the more cauteries you make, the greater the benefit will be to the patient.
et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	Know this: the patient feels no pain from the cautery as the healthy do, because the body is already entirely corrupted.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	And it is necessary that the cauteries be large and small according to the members and joints, as you will find them described in the various forms of irons.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	After applying a poultice of vetch flour with honey, perform other treatments until it is healed.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre;	When swelling occurs in any limb and is treated with medications, oils, and plasters, but it does not heal, then apply cauteries to the limb according to its size and smallness.
et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur;	And let the cautery be a bit deep into the flesh of the heart;
puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat it with oils until it is healed.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure;	And sometimes cautery is applied to the hand, foot, and back at the exit of the nerve that moves the limb, and thus the swelling is removed;
et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	Yet let no one intervene who is not knowledgeable about limbs and the exits of moving nerves in the body.
de albaras	de Albares
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color;	When the disease called 'albaras' is inflamed, and the means of medicine do no good, then cauterize it with a deep cautery according to the quantity of the flesh of the heart until the inflammation is removed and its color changed;
puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie;	Then apply a poultice of wheat flour, lentils, and rose oil mixed with plantain leaves, and donkey's blood and almond milk, each in equal parts.
et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	And mix everything together, tie it with a cloth, and apply it to the place until it is healed.
li cure de chancre par cautere	Li cure de chancre par cautere est bonne chose et utile; quar quanque il est enveilli et eschauchié et dure longuement, il s’ensuit que la membre devient chee et que l’en est empeschie. Donc adonques le cauterise d’un cautere de fer ardant qui soit un pou entre en l’espés dou keur; puis ensi come li cautere est ostee, prent on une espice d’arsenic et de salemongier et les met ensemble, et fait on de la farine. Ensemble met on une partie de sanc dou chancre et une partie de sanc de chèvre ou de brebis, ou de sanc dou chevaulx ou de l’autel; puis prent on un peu de la farine d’arsenic et de salemongier et la mele a ces sanz et a oile roset. Et soit ceste medicine mise sus le chancre tant que li cautere y soit ostee et que li sanc dou chancre ne chei plus; puis fait on un emplestre de farine de fuces et de lentilles, de plantain et d’ache avec oile roset, et met on ceste medicina sur le chancre. Et quant il est tout gueris, adonques on l’envele et on mete y une medicine de vinaigre de vin blanc et de farine de fuces et de lentilles avec oile roset; et puis fait on une cautere plus petit que li autre, qui soit un pou entre en l’espés dou keur; puis le cure continue de la medicina de vinaigre et d’oile jusques a tant qu’il soit tout sanez.
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	When a chancre appears at the beginning, and you see it has stopped, then cauterize it with a hot iron that seems to resemble an ellipse, all around the circumference of the chancre.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre;	Also, wise men said that one should perform cautery in the middle of the cancer;
et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois;	But I do not think this is good advice, for I fear that it may cause ulceration and corruption, as it has happened before in some cases;
et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	And a more correct thing to do is to perform circumcision-like cautery around it, as we have described in many cauteries.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	de l'enfleure qui ne peut meurer
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens;	When someone has an illness called "adubelati," which lingers due to the excess it produces or due to the weakness of the patient when they are very old (i.e., too elderly), and they have poor blood flow, or due to the time;
et tu la vues haster de meurer:	And you shall hasten its death:
adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant;	Then cauterize it around with many small cauteries, pricking it.
aprés le laisse ensi.	After that, leave it thus.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	For she will rush to die.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	Et se tu la ves percir à tot le cautère,
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	And place your hand on the middle of that disease called 'adubelati' until the cautery has pierced the heart, and let the cautery be so hot that the patient feels it like this: so that the course of the corruption is eased.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	After the treatment, as long as he is perfectly healthy.
li cure dou feu par fer	"The treatment with fire by iron"
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	Another kind of disease called 'corrodens', which is nothing other than the destruction of limbs, for it consumes them like fire consumes dry logs.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est;	If you see this disease in a place that can bear the cautery together with fire, then heat the cauteries of small and large nails according to what is needed for the place where the disease is located;
aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	Then cauterize it on all sides until you remove all the corruption, and nothing remains of it, so that everything that is corrupted may be removed.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	And then leave it for three days, and place over the cauterized places a poultice made with oil until the burns of the fire are healed, and all corruption is removed.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	After the treatment of ointments generating heat.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin;	And if after three days you see that healthy flesh does not grow, then it is good;
et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	If not, then recommence the cautery on what remains of the corrupted places.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu;	And this wound has sometimes been cured with hot medicine instead of fire cautery;
mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division:	But still, fire cautery is of greater help, and I have already mentioned the cure of hot medicine in its proper place.
pren la quant tu en as mestier.	Take as much as you need.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	"Porrelz" refers to swellings or tumors. The phrase "des porrelz qui vienent as piez" means "swellings that come from the feet." Here's an example of how it might be used in a sentence:
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	Often there occurs at the feet a disease called "closure" according to our understanding, and it is a large broken thing that wounds the foot.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	And the cauteries for this disease are in two ways
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	That is to say fire cautery, and cautery of hot water
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges;	Fire cautery is such that you heat the hair cauterizer like an owl's feather, and it should be made of good iron to the measure that it can encompass the nail on all sides, and have subtle edges;
aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou;	After placing it hot on the nail, twist your hand all around the nail until it reaches the base of the nail;
et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture;	And leave it like that for 3 days until it begins to discharge pus;
puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	Then make a poultice of wild mallows crushed with salt, and leave the poultice on all night, and the nail will fall out and be extracted from its roots.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then anoint the location with healing ointment until it is clean.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude;	And if they are inverted by force against the body, which happens often in hands and feet, then you must bring a cautery of hot water.
et est en teil maniere:	And it is done in this manner:
pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues;	Take a tin or iron pipe, or an owl's feather, and place it on the nail and the surrounding skin, that is to say, warts;
et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine;	And place the vessel on so that it grips all around, then put a bit of warm water inside, and hold your hand steady, and press your hand as you turn so that the edge of the vessel reaches the root of the nail, and can find the deep warm water pathway to the root.
et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre;	And let the patient endure a little the biting of the hot water for an hour;
puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	Then leave it thus, and it will be pulled out entirely by all its roots.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	Do this one after another until you have rooted out all those on the body, then treat them with healing ointments that bring forth flesh.
li cure dou trembler	Here is a remedy for the trembling:
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee;	When someone trembles from coldness of the nerves, or from quartan fever or other, then you must make them four cauteries or five on the spine of the back, one cautery between each spine;
et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire;	And one cautery on the foot, and one on the stomach at the olive-shaped cautery.
si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	This will stop the trembling, and the warmth of health will chase away the cold disease.
des pustules puans	Stinking pimples
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	Sometimes it is apparent on the body's surface when there are wet ulcers or foul pustules which come from corrupt matter.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule:	When they first appear, it is necessary to make a cautery on each head of the boil;
un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	A subtle cautery made of myrtle wood, whose point has been heated in fire, or of long Aristologus root, or of the lenticular cautery.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez;	And sometimes they cauterize at the beginning when they appear, in this manner, and they cannot grow back afterwards; but the excess from which they come is dried up, and they are sound.
mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	but it is necessary that this be done after the evacuation of blood
quant li artere est copee	When an artery is cut
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses;	Many times there are great flows of blood from the artery that is cut at the wound that comes from behind, or at the incision of an abscess, or at the cautery of a limb, and similar things
et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	and it is very difficult to stop.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus;	And furthermore, when this happens to anyone, quickly place your index finger on the vein wound and press firmly until the blood quiets under your finger and no more drops come out
puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge;	Then put olive oil cauteries of various sizes, both small and large, into the fire until they are all red.
puis empren I, ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	Then take one, whether large or small according to the wound and where the artery is situated, and place the cautery on that vein while you hold your finger [or forceps], and hold it until the bleeding stops.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement .i. autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	And if it happens that when you lift your finger from the vein and the cautery is extinguished, then quickly take another one of the cauteries that are in the fire.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez;	And continue doing this one after another until the bleeding has stopped;
et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide;	Be careful not to burn the nerve that is nearby, and ensure that no other harm comes to the patient;
et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit:	And know that when blood flows from an artery, it cannot be easily stopped, especially if the artery is large, unless by one of the four methods we have mentioned;
ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc;	Either by cautery, or by extracting it if not already treated, or by tightly tying a thread, or by applying medicines that have the power to stop bleeding;
et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	And let it be bound and compressed properly.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	And do not think that stopping bleeding will be brought about by binding too tightly with bandages or putting hot things on it, or other similar things, for it profits little if at all.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne;	And if this happens to anyone and he does not have a physician or medication present, then he should place his right index finger on the vein wound as we have said, stretching it out well until it is tense over the wound and the vein.
et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez;	And do not move your finger, but moisten it with cold water often enough so that it is very cold until the blood congeals, thickens and becomes tense.
et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	And make preparations ahead of time for those who need cauteries and medications.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	Here begins the second book of remedies for wounds
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres;	We have told you in the first chapter all diseases for which a fire cautery or burning medicine is necessary, and the ointments, causes, instruments, and forms of cauteries.
et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	I have placed this chapter from head to foot in the previous one, and I will follow the same path in this chapter so that one may find more easily what one desires.
Et ainsois que je encomence ceu, il covient, chier fil, que vos aprenez que en cest chapistre a plus de peril et de paor que ou premier des cauteres, et por ceu il covient plus grant cautele.	And before I begin this one, dear friend, you must know that in this chapter there is more danger and fear than in the first about cauteries, and therefore it requires greater caution.
Car en l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses;	For in the work of this chapter, there is often evacuation of blood when opening a vein, and incising an abscess, and in treating wounds, and extracting arrows, and cutting into stones, and similar things.
ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.	Where there is doubt and fear, many die.
Et je vos amoneste que vos n’entreprenez folie.	And I warn you not to undertake foolishness.
Car mout de manieres de gens vienent en cures.	For many kinds of people come seeking treatment.
si vienent de telz qui s’aïrent si avec lor maladie qu’il muerent legierement por la forsenerie qu’il trueve de sa maladie, et de la grandour de son malice;	If some come from those who harm themselves so much with their illness that they die easily because of the madness that comes from it and the greatness of their wickedness;
et de ces doit on avoir paor.	And one should fear these things.
Et de ces i a qui te done son sens, et dit:	And there are those who give you their sense and say:
«atendez, je sui garis»;	Wait, I am healed.
et li maladie est despitouse.	And the disease is stubborn.
Il ne covient mie que vos vos consentez a ces qui vienent a vos qui ont ceste maniere, mais mettez plus grant cusanson en vostre honor qu’en vostre covoitise, et n’ovrez mie folement mais saigement de ceu dont vos estes certain, et dont vos poez avoir pris et los;	You should not consent to those who come to you with this manner, but put greater care in your honor than in your desire, and do not open foolishly but wisely for those from whom you are certain, and for whom you can take glory.
et usez de pronostication et de indication en cures de vos malaides a coi salus soit convertie;	And use prognosis and indication in treating your patients so that salvation may be achieved;
et ceu vos aidera a aquester bone renommee, et gloire, et memoire de loenge.	This will help you acquire good reputation, glory, and praise.
Tres chier fil, Nostres Sires vos doint boin entendement et droiture, et se vos vuelle espireir de la sainte inspiration de sa main, amen.	"Dear son, our Lord grant you good understanding and uprightness, and if you wish to aspire to the holy inspiration of His hand, amen."
Or je vos ai ordeneit cest chapistre en devisant par chapistres, selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre des cauteres, que je vos ai deviseit des le chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que vos trovez plus legierement ceu dont vos avrez mestier.	"And I have arranged this chapter for you in sections, divided into chapters according to what is before the chapter on cauterization, which I previously discussed from head to foot, so that you may find more easily what you need."
dou chief plein d’aigue	"head full of water"
Saiches que ceste maladie vient mout de fois as enfans a l’enfanter, et quant li baille estraint trop fort le chief de l’enfant;	Know that this disease often comes to children during childbirth, especially when the birth canal squeezes the head of the child too tightly;
et aucune fois vient ceu de cause reponue que on ne seit.	And sometimes this occurs due to a hidden cause that remains unknown.
Et je ne vis onques ceste maladie fuers qu’en enfans, et a toz ces que j’ai veus se hastait li mors;	I have never seen this disease affect anyone but children, and all those I saw died quickly.
et por ceu me semble qu’il me vaut mues lassier l’ovraige en teilz cures.	And therefore it seems to me that I should leave off working on such cures.
Et je vis I enfant de coi li chiés estoit plains d’aigue, et li chief engroissoit chescun jor tant qu’il ne lou pooit sostenir;	I saw a child whose head was filled with water, and it grew bigger every day until he could no longer hold it up.
et crut tant li moistor qu’il fut mors, et ceste moistor si est assemblee desoz l’os sus lou syphac, entre lou keur et l’os;	And the moisture increased so much that he died, and this moisture collected under the bone above the nape of the neck, between the heart and the bone.
et li ovraiges si est telz se li moistor est entre lou keur et l’os, et li apostemes est petis, que tu fendes emmi lou chief une fendure large;	And if this moisture is located between the heart and the bone, with small abscesses present, you should make a wide cut in the middle of the head.
et soit ausi longe com II nous, tant que li mostor corre;	and it should be as long as two fingers, so that the moisture runs out;
et vez ci la forme dou spatumile:	And here is the shape of the spina bifida:
Se li moistor est plus creue, et li aposteme soit plus grans, si fai .ij. fendures en maniere d’une croix, selonc ceste forme:	"If the moisture has grown more and the swelling is larger, then make two incisions in the form of a cross, according to this shape:"
Et se li moistor est desoz l’os, et li signes que tu vois les commissures dou chief overtes de chescune partie, et li aigue saut fuer quant tu la presses de ta main au dedens, et ceu ne t’est mie reponut:	And if the moisture is under the bone, and you see signs such as the head's scalp raised on both sides, and water squirts out when pressed with your hand inside, but nothing comes out:
si covient que tu fendes enmi lou chief III fendures selonc ceste maniere:	If you must cut around the head, make three incisions as follows:
Et aprés l’incision estrai la moistor toute fuers.	And after the incision, remove all the moisture outside.
Aprés estraint les fendures de drapelz et de poudres, et i met vin et oile, et laisse ensi jusc’a cinquieme jor;	After straining the wounds with cloths and powders, apply vinegar and oil, leaving it thus until the fifth day;
puis le deslie, et cure la plaie par tentes et par oignemens, et laisse estraindre le chief egaument, et done mengier au malaide viande seche de poc de moistor tant que li membre soit confortez et sanez.	Then unbind it, and dress the wound with compresses and ointments, keeping the head wrapped evenly. Give the patient dry food from a moist-free pot until the limb is healed.
Et une autre maniere d’incision est que tu regardes ou apert li grandor de l’aposteme, et li assemblé de l’aigue;	And another method of incision is to observe where the abscess appears large and its assembly of water;
car aucune fois est elle devant;	for sometimes it is in front.
aucune fois derrier;	sometimes behind;
aucune fois en destre;	sometimes on the right
et aucune fois en senestre.	and sometimes on the left.
Taille donques lai ou li aposteme apert, et l’emplissement de l’aigue, et lou fent selonc ce que tu en as le pooir;	Cut where the abscess appears and where the water collects, according to your ability;
et warde que tu ne coper l’artere;	and be sure not to cut the artery.
et veigne flun de sanc, si que li malaides muere dou decorrement de sanc et de l’evacuation de moistor.	Lest the patient die from blood loss and evacuation of moisture.
de reume	"de reume" translates to "of urine".
Quant il avient a aucun une maladie qui est apelee «catarre» as eulz ou au pis, et li maladie est anciainne, et li cure de medicine ne profite mie, adonques li derraine cure si est li cauteres avec ceu c’on li copera les .ij. arteres.	"When someone has an illness called 'catarra' in the ears or in the anus, and the illness is chronic, and medicinal treatment does not help, then the last resort is cauterization with the cutting of the two arteries."
Il covient donques, cant tu les vues coper, que li malaides faice rere son chief;	It is therefore necessary, when you cover the eyes, that the patient turns his head back;
aprés li frotte lou leu d’un drapel aspre tant que les arteres aperent, puis estraingne li malaides son col a tout I drapel;	afterward rub the place with a coarse cloth until the arteries appear, then wrap the patient's neck tightly in the cloth;
puis regarde ou li voine bait, et li leus de l’une et de l’autre sont aprés les oreilles, et poc sont reponues;	then look where the vein lies, and its location is near both ears, with few being behind them.
puis signe les leus d’enche, puis cope l’une et l’autre d’un spatumile agut de II pars, tant que li taille veigne jusc’a l’os, et ceu soit par lou large dou chief.	then mark the locations of the ears, then cut both with a sharp spathule of two parts until the vein is cut to the bone, and this should be done near the width of the head.
Et se tu vues, boute le spatumile desoz l’artere et la cope au desus, en taillant ausi com .ij. dois au traver.	"And if you see that you have not cut deep enough, slide the scalpel under the artery and cut it from above, cutting horizontally about two fingers wide."
Et quant li voinne est copee, si saut li sans en haut continuelment fuers.	"Once the vein is cut, blood flows out continuously."
Et se li artere n’apert au sentir, si covient que tu mesures la quantiteit de l’espaice de III dois, puis seigne d’enche et fent jusc’a l’os;	And if the arteries do not appear upon feeling, then measure the distance of three fingers' width, then mark and cut until you reach the bone.
et ceu qu’il covient dou sanc mettre fuers si est VI c/, et par aventure un poc plus ou moins, selonc ce que li malaides puet soffrir, et la repletion de l’artere;	and the amount of blood that should be let out is six ounces, and sometimes a little more or less, depending on what the patient can tolerate, and the filling of the artery.
puis regarde la plaie:	Then examine the wound:
s’il remaint sus l’os point dou syphac, si le cope que apostemes chaus n’i veigne, puis estrain la plaie et lie, et la cure d’oignement tant qu’ele soit sanee.	If it remains on the bony point of the hip, if swelling prevents abscesses from appearing, then press the wound and bind it, applying ointment until it heals.
de emigrainne	"de emigraine" translates to "of migraine".
Quant emigrainne anciaine vient, et catarre agut, por les moistors des larmes et les chalors en temples et sode anciene forsenee et semblans choses, et il est medicinez par manieres de cures de medicine et tout ceu ne li profite mie, si estraions les arteres des temples et lou cauterizons, si com nos avons conteit.	"When chronic migraine comes with severe catarrh, accompanied by moisture in the tears and heat in the temples, along with long-standing frenzy and similar symptoms, and medicinal treatment does not help, then we should cut the arteries of the temples and perform cauterization as described earlier."
Et li maniere de l’estraction d’elles si est que li malaides faice rere les poilz de ses temples, et entende a l’artere qui apert en la temple, car elle apert bien par son batement, et est poc reponue fuers que en aucuns homes qui sont trop froit;	And the manner of extracting them is thus: let the patient raise the hairs on their temples and listen to the artery that opens in the temple, for it beats well and is rarely heard outside except in some men who are too cold
et s’elle est reponue, si estraigne son col li malaides d’aucuns drapelz, puis frote le leu d’aucun aspre drap, et arose le leu d’aigue chaude tant que li artere apere manifestement;	and if it is heard, then the patient should tie their neck with some cloths, then rub the place with an abrasive cloth and raise the place with warm water until the artery appears plainly
puis pren le spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	then take the speculum made from this form
puis escorche le cuir legierement tant que tu veignes a l’artere, puis la trai en haut as pinceures, et la depart bien des toiles que sont desoz li de chescune partie;	then carefully scrape away the skin until you reach the artery, then grasp it with forceps and pull it upwards, cutting it well from the tissues beneath each part
et se li artere est subtilz, si la torne a la pointe de l’uncine, puis la cope de celle partie selonc la quantiteit des II chiés.	And if the artery is slender, then twist it with the point of the nail clipper; afterward cut off that portion according to the quantity of two heads.
Car s’elle n’est copee, si ne saut mie li sans dou tout en tout.	If it is not cut, blood will not flow freely throughout.
Et trai dou sanc des VI c/, jusc’a III;	And draw out six drops [of blood], up to three at a time;
et se li artere est grans, si covient que tu la lies en II leus d’un fil double fort de soie, que porriture n’i veigne devant le soudement de la plaie, et veigne decorremens de sanc;	And if the artery is large, then you must tie it in two places with a strong doubled silk thread so that putrefaction does not come before the wound heals and bleeding stops.
puis cope la superfluiteit qui est entre les II liiens en celle houre meisme, et puis, se tu vues, si lou cauterize dou cautere cutellaire jusc’a l’os tant que li chiés soient copez;	Then cut off the excess that is between the two ties at that very moment, and then, if you wish, cauterize with a hot cautery knife until the bone is exposed.
et c’est li muedre oevre, se li malaides n’a fievre et il est de chaude complexion.	And this is the major work, if the patient does not have fever and has a warm constitution.
Car li cauteres est aide por finir les moistors:	For the cautery helps to finish off moisture:
por ceu est il de plus grant aide as moistors.	So it is of greater help in moist conditions.
Ou il covient por l’estraction des arteres que om emplisse lou leu de viel coton et mette on sus tentes bien faites;	For the extraction of arteries, one must fill the space with old cotton and place well-made tents upon them;
et quant on les desliera, si soit curez de medicines seches que font naistre char, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez;	And when they are dislocated, they should be treated with dry medicines that cause flesh to grow, and with bandages, until they are healed.
et se sans cort de l’artere tant dis com tu i oevres, si te haste dou coper par cautere, ou tu emple lou leu de vitriole et l’estrain a ta main que li sans soit estainchiez;	And if the skin of the artery is torn as often as you work there, hurry to cover it with a cautery, or use the place of vitriol and press your hand so that the blood is staunched.
et se tu n’as ceu present, si met sor le leu ton doit tant que li sans soit congelez, et arose le leu d’aigue froide tant que li sans cesse, et soit estraint si com il covient;	And if you do not have vitriol present, place your thumb on the location until the blood congeals, then rinse the location with cold water until the bleeding stops, and apply pressure as needed.
et ceu qui est muedre et plus legier en l’estraction de l’artere est que tu cauterizes la voinne de cest cautere trenchant de II pars, mais li trenchant soient bien espés por warder plus longement lor chalor.	And those who are skilled and lighter in extracting the artery should cauterize the vein with this cutting cautery of two parts, but let the cuts be well-spaced to retain heat longer.
Car quant li estrumens est trop tenves, si tient moins sa chalor.	For when the tools are too thin, they retain less heat.
Et doit avoir entre les II coutelz I doit de gros d’espaice, et puis quant tu as signiet d’enche les II leus, et tu mes lou fer ardant sus tant qu’il viegne jusc’a l’os, et cope la voinne en II leus;	And there should be one thick nail of space between the two knives, and then when you have marked the two locations with incisions, place the red-hot iron upon them until it reaches the bone, and cut the vein in two places;
et soient esloigniet entre les II chiés car il n’est mie soudez de cest cautere dou tout en tout;	And let the two shoulder blades be kept apart, for they are not completely suited to this cautery.
et c’est li forme dou cautere:	And this is the shape of the cautery:
des larmes	of tears
Quant les larmes des eulz sont dessendans des voinnes que sont sus lou test dou chief de fuer, et il ne profite mie cure de medicine c’on i faice, et tu vois la faice dou malaide enrougir, et sent ou front ambulation si com de fremis;	When the tears of the eyes descend into the veins that are above the forehead on the head, and there is no benefit from any medication applied there, and you see the patient's face become reddened, and they feel a throbbing in their forehead like tremors;
et sui oil sont tenve et moiste si que li poil des papieres sont cheut, et sont eschaufees les papieres, et escorchies de l’ardor des larmes, si ait mestier de ceste cure.	and the eyes are thin and moist such that the hairs of the eyelashes have fallen out, and the eyelids are heated and burned by the heat of the tears, thus this treatment is necessary.
Et l’apelerent li ancien «cure contuse», et est que tu faices a rere au malaide qui a ceste maladie les poilz qu’il ait ou front, puis li fai III fendures ou front igalment selonc la longesce dou front;	And the ancients called this 'treatment for contusion', and it is to be done thus: first, have the patient with this illness grow hairs on their forehead, then make three evenly spaced incisions along the length of the forehead;
