puis point le leu qui est entre les II liens d’un intromissoire tant que li sans en isse qui i est, et soit deliiez li aposteme;	Then insert an introjector into the space between the two ligatures until blood comes out from there, and let the abscess be opened.
puis amenistre la cure que enjanre bowe, tant que li liien chient;	Then dress the wound every day until the ligation falls off.
puis cure ceu d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then apply an appropriate ointment until it is healed.
et se li apostemes est por la taille de la voinne, si covient que tu teignes a ta main ceu que tu pues de l’aposteme a tout le cuir, puis boute l’aguille desoz le leu que tu tiens a ta main, et la fai percier, et i ait I fil double, si que tu le trais de l’autre costeit;	If the abscess is caused by a vein incision, then you must hold what you can of it in your hand with forceps. Then place the needle underneath the spot you are holding and pierce it until it reaches the other side, so that you may draw out one double thread.
puis lie l’aposteme, si com je t’ai dit, ou liien de l’une de II pars as II chiés dou fil;	Then tie the abscess, as I told you, with thread taken from one of its two parts on the skin.
et se tu doutes que li filz n’isse fuer, si i reboute une autre aguille a tout I fil desoz tout l’aposteme a l’incision de la premiere aguille, et estraint les filz en IIII leus;	And if you doubt that the threads may break, then insert another needle through all of the threads beneath the entire abscess at the incision of the first needle, and tie the threads at four points.
puis cope l’aposteme tant que li superfluitez en isse, puis cope la superfluiteit dou keur et laisse ceu qui est liiez;	Then cut away the abscess until the superfluity comes out; then cut away the excess from around the heart, leaving what is tied.
puis met sus I drapeil moilliet en vin et en oile, puis li amenistre cures de tentes et d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then place a damp cloth soaked in wine and oil on it; then apply dressings and ointments until it is healed.
des apostemes des ners	"Apostumes of the nerves"
Ausi com aposteme vienent en l’artere et en la voine, vienent aposteme as ners quant il sont ferut, ou par trop grant travail, et semblans choses.	Also, boils come to the artery and vein,
Et ceu avient plus sovent as adjutoires et as dois et en toz leus ou il ait jointures, et c’est I grief apostemes, et sa color semble la color dou cors, et est em plusors dispositions sens dolor;	And this occurs more often on shoulders and toes, and in all places where there are joints; these are serious abscesses, their color resembling the color of flesh, and they exist in many forms without pain.
et quant on l’estraint forment, si sent li malaides dolor, et n’est mie em parfont dou cors, mais desoz lou keur;	And when it is pressed strongly, the patient feels pain; but this is not deep within the body, rather near the heart.
et muet bien de toutes pars, et ne va ne avant ne arrier, ne desoz ne desus, et celui qui est en jointures ne covient mie coper par fer:	And it moves well on all sides, neither going forward nor backward, nor below nor above, and one that is in joints should not be covered with iron:
par aventure i vanroit contraction;	For fear of contraction occurring there;
et cil qui est ou chief ou ou front, fent le cuir au spatumile.	And the one that is on the head or forehead, cut the skin at the temples.
Se li apostemes est petis, si le tien a unes tenailles, et le cope en sa racine;	If the abscess is small, grasp it with tweezers and cut its root;
et s’il est grans, si le sospent a l’oncine, et l’escorche, puis l’oste et assemble la plaie a la costure, et lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if it is large, suspend it with forceps, scrape it off, then cut and sew the wound together, caring for it until it heals.
des grosses boces pendans	"from hanging bags of fat"
Aucune fois avient en ventres et ne mie autre part thelul, et est une maladie qui est apelee «funge» par la semblance d’aus, et est li racine subtilz, et li chiez gros;	Sometimes occurs in bellies and nowhere else, called 'fungus' due to its appearance, with thin roots and large heads;
et en i a de petis et de mout grans;	And there are both small ones and very large ones.
et je vis I home qui en avoit II ou ventre qui estoient plus semblans a funges que ai autre chose, et n’i avoit point de difference, et estoient blanc, et avoient menue racine, et estoient jai fendut, et en corroit adés moistor.	And I saw a man who had two in his belly that were more like fungi than anything else; they were white and had thin roots, and they were often cracked open with moisture flowing from them.
Je les copai et trovai en l’un XVIII onces pesant, et en l’autre VI З., et li ovraiges en l’incision si est que tu regardes se li malaides est moistes, et li color de l’artelul est blainche et moiste et de subtil racine;	I weighed them and found one weighing XVIII ounces, the other VI. The procedure for incision is such that you should consider whether the patient is moist; the color of the artery is pale and moist with a subtle root.
si le cope au spatumile large, et soient en ta presence li cautere au feu.	If the cut is wide, have the cauterizing iron hot and ready in your presence.
Car au taillier vient maintes fois trop grans decorremens de sanc, et se li sans te vaint, si te haste donques dou cauterizer;	For at cutting comes often too great a flow of blood; if the blood overcomes you, then hasten to use the cautery.
et se tu vois le malaide espoanteit et paourous de l’incision dou fer, si prent I fil de plonc bien fait, et en lie l’artelul si com nos avons dit, et le laisse II jors;	And if you see the patient afraid and fearful of the incision of iron, then take a well-made thread of tow, tie the artery as we have said, and leave it for two days.
et puis le restraint, et ne cesser d’estraindre lou fil de plonc tant qu’il cope l’artelul, et chiece par lui sens travail;	Then tie it again; do not cease pulling on the thread of tow until it cuts through the artery without effort.
et se les racines sont grosses, si a paour au coper meismement por le ventre, mais tu em pues bien coper la moitiet, puis le cauterize qu’il ne reviegne;	And if the roots are large, one fears cutting even for the belly; but you can cut half of it and then cauterize so that it does not bleed again.
puis cure la plaie, et garde que tu ne coper le thelul qui est de fuxe color et de povre sens et de lait regart.	Then heal the wound, but ensure you do not cover the telum which is of fox-like hue, poor sense, and produces milk.
Car c’est uns apostemes enchancrez, et je venrai a la cure de chancre ci aprés.	"For this is an enchanted aposteme, and I will speak of the cure of chancre later on."
quant li boude ist fuer	"When the belly is full"
Se li apparance de la boude vient par cautere de plaie ou de fendure de syfac, et est sus le ventre et en ist aucuns des bouez, si com il avient en autres routures, ou de sanc qui cort de voines ou d’arteres selonc ceu qui est devant, ou de ventositeit;	If the appearance of the wound comes from a cautery burn or a fissure of syphilis, and is located on the belly, as it happens in other ruptures, or from blood flowing from veins or arteries as mentioned earlier, or from windiness
et se c’est par la routure dou syfac et par l’issue dou bouel, si est li color de l’aposteme semblans a la color dou cors, et est legiere chose sens dolor, et apert de diverse issue.	and if it is due to the rupture of syphilis and the exit of the bowel, then the color of the abscess is similar to the color of the body, and it causes little pain or discomfort with varied discharge.
Et se c’est por l’issue de l’intestine, adonques est il plus divers, et quant on le presse a ses dois si se repont, et puis revient, et par aventure si est sarrez, et agrandist mout a l’entree dou bain et por fort travail.	And if it is due to an intestinal issue, then it becomes more diverse, and when pressed with two fingers it sinks in and then returns, and sometimes it becomes hard, and increases greatly at the entrance of the bath and with heavy labor.
Et se c’est por moistor, c’est legiere chose, et apert bien quant tu le presses a ta main, ne ne constraint mie;	And if it's due to moisture, it's not serious; when you press it with your hand, it yields well without being tense.
et se c’est por sanc, si apert par ces signes li apostemes gros et dur, et est fichiez selonc une quantiteit;	and if it's due to blood, then the abscess appears large and hard, adhering firmly like a quantity.
et se c’est por ventositeit, si est souef au tochier, et li ovraiges si est que tu regarde se li apparance est por le sanc de l’artere, ou de la voine, ou ventositeit.	and if it's due to windiness, it is soft to the touch, and its appearance can indicate whether it's from arterial or venous blood, or windiness.
Si covient que tu laisses la cure.	Therefore, you should leave the treatment alone.
Car il en a doutance et paor, si com je t’ai dit ou chapistre des apostemes, por l’artere et por la voine.	Fear and doubt exist regarding this matter, as I have said in the chapter on abscesses, concerning both artery and vein.
Et se li apparance est por l’intestine ou lou boueil, si covient que tu comandes au malaide qu’il teigne son alaine, et soit estendus tout drois, puis seigne d’enche tout entor la boude;	And if the appearance is for the intestine or bowel, then you must command the patient to draw up their knee and extend it fully straight, then press firmly all around the belly.
puis le comande a gesir sovin entre tes mains, puis va entor le leu que tu as signiet a tout le spatumile, puis estent la moitiet de l’aposteme au desus a tout le grant uncine;	then have them lie down constantly between your hands; then go around the place you marked with the entire palm of your hand, then stretch half of the abscess upwards with the full width of your index finger.
puis le lie entor d’un fil fort, ou d’une corde de fort soie fermement, et soit li nous dou liien assolz;	Then bind it firmly with a strong thread or cord of strong silk, and let the swelling be released completely.
puis oevre la moitiet de l’aposteme estendut sus le liien, et i boute ton doit indice, et quier l’intestine;	then open half of the abscess stretched over the bandage, and insert your index finger, and search for the intestine
se tu le trueves pris dou liien, si le deslie, et boute l’intestine au defuer dou ventre;	if you find it trapped by the bandage, untie it, and bring the intestine out from in front of the abdomen
et se tu trueves le boueil, si le prent a l’oncine, et en cope la superfluiteit;	and if you find the bowel, grasp it with your index finger and cut away any excess.
et se li artere te fait contraire, ou li voine, si vai belement entor, puis revien a ton ovraige et pren II aguilles, et i boute II fors filz, et boute les II aguilles entor ceu que tu as fait en crois que tu feis percier;	and if the artery opposes you or the vein, then proceed gently around; then return to your work and take two needles, and thread them with two strong threads, and insert the two needles around what you have pierced in a cross shape
puis estrain l’aposteme en IIII leus sus les aguilles, et se tu vues, oste les aguilles, et laisse lou leu tant qu’il porrisse, et chiece li char morte par soi;	Then press the boil at four points over the needles; if you see, remove the needles and let it alone until it rots; and cut away the dead flesh.
ou tu la cope quant elle iert subtiliie et porrie, puis le cure de ceu qu’il covient, et cheve l’aposteme si com nos avons dit;	Then cut it when it is ripe and ready; then treat it as necessary, and cut away the boil as we have said.
et estrai le sanc ou la moistor que tu trueves, puis cure le leu de ceu qu’il couvient, et soude le leu.	And draw out the blood or moisture that you find, then treat the spot as needed, and close it up.
dou chancre	chancre
Nos avons dit en la division les semblances de chancre, et coment on i doit ovrer par medicines, et coment on doit eschuer la cure de fer;	We have said in the previous section about the kinds of chancres and how one must operate by medicines, and how to avoid surgical treatment.
et disons le chancre enjanreit en la marris, et grant cautele a en la cure, et dirent li ancien que quant chancres est en leu ou on le puet raier si com chancre qui est em mameles, et en la cuixe, et en semblans leus, et le doit tout oster quant il est en l’encomencement;	And let's discuss the chancre in the marrow, and caution must be taken in treating it; ancient authorities say that when a chancre is in a location where it can be shaved off completely, like those on the breast or hip, they should be removed entirely at the outset.
et quant il est grans et anciens, si ne covient mie que tu l’aproches, car je n’en poi onques nul saner;	But when it is large and old, do not attempt to approach it, for I have never seen anyone recover from it;
ne nulz n’en sana onques devant moi.	No one has ever been healed from this before me.
Et li ovraiges, quant il est en leu ou on le puet oster, si com nos avons dit, est que tu purge aucune fois le malaide de cole noire;	And the operation, when it is in place where it can be removed, as we have said, is that you should purge the patient of black bile at least once;
puis le fai sainier s’il ait manifeste repletion, puis afaite le malaide I boin leu por faire l’ovraige;	Then make the patient fast if he has shown signs ofpletion, then prepare the patient in a good place to perform the operation;
puis giete tes oncines ou chancre, et le cheve de toutes pars, et l’oste de toutes pars sens rien laissier;	then cut away your Oncines or Chancres, and shave the hair from all around it, and remove it completely without leaving anything behind;
et laisse corre le sanc tout fuer, et espreint bien le leu a ta main ou a aucune chose, et se li decorremens de sanc te fait contraire de l’incision de l’artere ou de la voine, si le cauterize tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	and let the blood flow freely, and press firmly on the wound with your hand or some other thing, and if the bleeding from the incision of the artery or vein opposes you, cauterize it until the bleeding stops;
puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat him with another remedy until he is healed.
de ydropisie	of dropsy
Nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’idropisie, et en queil maniere li assemblee de l’aigue est faite, et les signes de chescune semblance, et la cure qui est faite par medicines, et cele qui est curee par fer:	We have already spoken in the previous section about the similarities of dropsy, how water collects in the body and the signs of each kind, as well as the remedies made by medicines and those treated with iron;
si est eclites soulement;	If it is merely bruised;
et ne doit on touchier de fer en ces II semblances:	and one must not use iron in these two cases:
c’est a savoir, tympanites et yposarche, car c’est mortelz chose;	namely, tympanites and hiposarches, for they are deadly matters.
donques quant tu medicines ceste semblance de ydropisie qui est apelee «eclites» de medicines, et li cure ne profite, si regarde se li malaides est foibles, ou s’il ait autre maladie que ydropisie, si com toust et solution de ventre et semblans choses;	Therefore, when treating this type of dropsy called "eclites," if the treatment does not help and the patient is weak or has other illnesses such as dropsy, tumors, or similar conditions;
si n’i touchier de fer, car il i a doutance;	then do not use iron, for there is doubt involved.
et se tu vois le malaide de fort vertut, et il n’a autre maladie que ydropisie soulement, et il n’est mie trop jones ne trop vielz, si dois ensi ovrer:	And if you see that the patient has strong vitality, and they have no other illness besides dropsy alone, and are not too young nor too old, then you should proceed thus:
lieve le malaide droit sus tes mains, et li ministres presse le ventre em boutant l’aigue a la plus basse partie dou pis, puis pren le spatumile espinous selonc ceste forme:	Have the patient lie down straight on your hands, and have an assistant press the abdomen strongly while pouring water onto the lowest part of the back, then take the spinehook shaped thus:
Et soit trenchans de II pars.	And let it be cut into two parts.
a pointe, et toutevoie ne soit mie si entrans qu’il puist venir jusc’a l’intestine quant on le fiche ens, et ne le puist blecier;	with its point, but not so deeply that it can reach the intestines when inserted, nor cause injury;
puis regarde se li ydropisie est enjanree devers les intestines:	then look if dropsy has entered towards the intestines
si covient que tu fendes ensus de la boude III dois droit desoz sus lou poignil;	if it is necessary that you cut with a lancet three inches below and above on the shin bone.
et se li ydropisie est por la maladie dou foie, si soit ta fendure au senestre de la boude III dois;	and if dropsy is due to liver disease, then make your incision on the left side of the shinbone three inches below.
et se c’est por la miuce, si soit a destre, et ne covient mie que li malaides gise sus la fendure que les superfluitez ne corrent a celui foible leu;	and if it is due to phlegm, then cut on the right side, and ensure that the patient does not lie upon the incision so that the excesses do not flow into that weak area.
puis perce tout le cuir a l’estrument, et le boute, et lieve ta main a tout le spatumile entre le cuir et le syfac ausi com en escorchant a la quantiteit d’une ungle ou enqui entor;	then pierce the skin with an awl and insert it, raise your hand to cut through the entire spermatic cord between the skin and the scrotum as in castration.
puis perce lou syfac tant que li spatumile viegne au leu vuit, et c’est li leus de l’aigue, puis le trai fuer, et i boute cest estrument de coi ci est li forme:	then pierce the scrotum until the spermatic cord reaches its proper place, and this is the opening for water, then draw it out and insert this instrument of which I have described.
Et est semblans a une caine d’argent subtil, et est d’arain ou d’archaut legier, et a en la partie desoz I petit pertus;	And it is similar to a fine silver needle, made of brass or light copper, with a small hole at the end.
et ou costeit d’une part, III pertus;	And on one side there are three openings.
et II d’autre part, et I d’autre;	And two on the other side, and one on the other.
et est li chiés tailliez si com une penne, et c’est li forme de l’incision dont li escrivains taille la penne:	And the head is cut like a feather, and this is the shape of the incision that scribes use to cut feathers:
au chief desus est li alemele, si que quant li estrumens vient a l’aigue, si dessent maintenant sus l’estrument;	At the top of it is the almond; so when the tool reaches the water, it sinks now upon the tool.
vuide la donques la moitiet ou la tierce part, car se tu en vuides plus qu’il ne covient en celle houre, par aventure si muert li malaides por la resolution de son esperit de l’arme, ou il chiet paumez, ou il aproche a la mort;	Therefore empty about half or one third of it; because if you empty more than is necessary at that time, perhaps the patient will die due to the release of his spirit from the weapon, or he may faint, or come close to death.
mais en vuide selonc la quantiteit de sa vertut, et selonc ceu que les dispositions de la vertut dou malaide signifient, et ses poulz;	But empty according to the amount of its power, and according to what the indications of the patient's power signify, and his pulse.
puis trai l’estrument et retien l’aigue, et elle est retenue maintenant por le keur qui estoupe le pertus qui est sus le syfac, de coi j’ai parleit, que tu perces selonc ceste maniere;	Then withdraw the tool and hold the water back; it is held back now by the heart, which stops up the hole that is above the stomach, as I have spoken of.
puis rencomence l’estrument l’autre jor, se tu vois le malaide soffrant ceu, et trai de l’aigue une petite quantiteit;	Then restart the treatment the next day if you see the patient enduring this, and apply a small amount of water.
fai ce aucun jor, et te garde de foloier tant qu’il ni demore mais c’un poc d’aigue.	Do this for several days, but be careful not to remain there too long, just a moment with a little water.
Et se tu doutes sus le malaide, et tu i lais mout d’aigue, si le cure de la sepulture ou sablon chaut, et par mout sueir ou bain et au soleil, et se teigne de boivre;	And if you doubt about the patient and leave too much water on them, their cure will be like that of the grave or hot sand; they will sweat excessively or take a bath in the sun; they should drink sparingly.
et le cure de medicines desiccatives tant qu’il soit sanez, et cauterize sus l’estomac et sus lou foie et sus l’esplen aprés l’estraction de l’aigue, si com j’ai dit devant.	And apply drying medications until they are healthy again; cauterize the stomach, liver, and spleen after removing the water, as I have mentioned earlier.
de l’estopement de la verge	Of the swelling of the penis
Aucune fois naissent enfant qui n’ont point de pertus en la verge, ou li pertus est petis, ou il n’est mie en son leu.	Never are children born without an opening in the penis, or with a small one, or one that is not in its proper place.
Si le covient tantost qu’il n’aist percier a tout I spatumile molt subtil selonc ceste forme:	If it must be, let it be pierced at once with a very fine lancet according to this form:
puis met ou pertus I clo subtil de plonc, et le lie et le tien ensi III jors ou IIII et quant il vuet faire urine, si soit ostez li clos, et faice urine, et puis li remet;	Then place a subtle skin clip of lead there; tie it and hold it for three or four days. When he wants to urinate, remove the clip, let him do so, and then replace it.
et par aventure nen i couvient point, car li urine qui vient fuer ne lou laisse close.	And perhaps this is not necessary, because the urine that comes forth does not remain closed.
Cil de cui li pertus est petis, si est medicinez dou clo de plonc, si com nos avons dit, si s’eslargera.	He whose hole is small shall be treated with lead ointment as we have said; it will widen.
Cil qui n’ont mie le pertus en lor leu sont bleciet, car aucun naissent qui ont le pertus au chief de la verge, por coi il ne puient pissier avant s’il ne lievent lor verge en haut;	Those whose opening is not in its proper place are blind, for some are born with the opening at the head of the penis, which prevents them from urinating until they lift their penis upwards;
et ne pueent enjanrer por ceu que li matiere ne puet venir jusc’a la marris, et c’est une male maladie.	and cannot void properly because matter cannot reach the bladder, and this is a serious illness.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos, puies estent le chief de la verge et le cope ausi com la taille d’une penne, si ke li pertus chiece em mileu, si com il covient;	And the method of treatment is that the patient should lie on their back, then raise the head of the penis and cut it like the shape of a feather's tip so that the opening falls in the middle, as it should be;
et te garde de decorrement de sanc qui i vient maintes fois, et s’il avient, si l’estainche de ceu qui estainche sanc, et cure la plaie tant qu’il soit sanez.	and beware of excessive bleeding that often occurs there; if it happens, use something to stop the bleeding and heal the wound until it is clean.
des pustules de la verge	sores on the penis
Maintes fois vienent cist albathe en la verge, et est une apparance de char laide;	Many times these swellings come on the penis, which are ugly looking growths of flesh;
et en i a malignes et non malignes;	and some are malignant and others not.
si covient que tu les preignes a I oncine subtil, et les cope et munde toutes, puis met sus coton moilliet en oignement egiptien;	Therefore you should seize them with a delicate pincer, cut and cleanse them all, then apply moistened cotton in Egyptian ointment.
puis le cure d’oignement diafinicon tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then, the treatment of anointing with ointment, until it is healed.
Et se li albathe est maligne, de pute color et depuant, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere.	And if the bath is malignant, of foul color and stinking, then you must bring cautery to it.
Quant tu l’as copeit, et se li albathe est en som la verge, et en ait partie dedens la peil et partie defuer, si covient que tu oste l’albathe qui est dedens premier;	When you have seized [the dislocation], and if the hip is above the penis, and part of it is inside the skin and part outside, then you must remove the hipbone that is inside first;
et quant il est soudez, si le cure defuer.	and once it is removed, then treat what remains outside.
Car quant tu le cures ensamble, si n’est mie asseurez li chiez de la verge qu’il ne soit perciez, et vient noiror et corruption en son la verge et ou coion;	For if you treat them together, the head of the penis is not secure and may be pierced, and blackness and corruption come to its tip and in the scrotum;
si covient chever tout ceu qui est noir et corrumput, puis lie sus l’emplaustre de miel et de farine qui soit fait d’escorce de poumes grenates et de veces, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	Therefore cut away all that is black and corrupt, then apply a plaster of honey and flour mixed with the rind of pomegranates and figs, then treat it further until it is healed.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si amenistre le cautere lunaire selonc ceste forme:	And if bleeding occurs, then apply the lunar cautery according to this form:
Li cauteres si aide as II dispositions ensamble:	The cautery helps in two ways together:
c’est asavoir, au decorrement de sanc, et a la corruption;	namely, for the discharge of blood and for corruption;
et se li chiés de la verge est corrumpus et retrais, si covient que tu boutes ou conduit de la verge une cainne de plonc, et pisse li malaides parmi;	And if the head of the penis is corrupted and retracted, then you must insert a lead tube into the channel of the penis, so that the patient can urinate through it;
et quant li pelz iert aerse au chief de la verge qui avient a ces qui n’ont mie esteit circoncis, ou il avient por plaie ou por aposteme, si covient donques que tu l’escorches a I estrument cheveit, tant que li liiens soit desliiez, et soit delivrez li chiez de la verge de toutes pars;	And when the skin is raised at the head of the penis, which happens to those who have not been circumcised, whether due to wound or abscess, then you must cauterize it with a hair-removing instrument until the adhesion is loosened, and the head of the penis is delivered from all sides.
et se c’est grief chose de deviser ceu, si covient que tu l’escorches a I spatumile aucun poc dou chief de la verge et de la peil;	And if it is difficult to separate them, then you must cauterize with the spatumalium at some point near the head of the penis and the skin.
puis dessevre belement entre II, et i met I subtil drapeil de lin moilliet an aigue froide, qu’il n’aerse derechief.	Then carefully separate them again, and place a thin linen cloth moistened in cold water between them to prevent them from sticking together again.
de la circoncision	de la circoncision
Circoncision n’est mie desliemens de continuation si com les autres plaies;	Circumcision is not a continuous cleansing like other wounds;
toutevoie quant nos faison ceste oevre de nostre volenteit, et proprement as enfans, si est mestier que nos faisiens la millor oevre, et la plus legiere a salut.	Nevertheless, when we perform this operation willingly and properly on children, it is necessary that we do the best work and cause the least harm.
Je dis que li ancien ne dirent mie la circoncision de lor enfans, car il n’en usent mie en lor loi, et n’en avons mais que ceu que nos avons aquis par experiment.	I say that the ancients did not practice the circumcision of their children, for they did not use it in their law, and we have only what we have acquired by experience.
Car j’ai veut la plus grant partie des maistres et des sainors qui faisoient circumcision entor I dal, et as forces, et a tout une novacule;	For most masters and surgeons who perform circumcisions cut around the foreskin with forceps, using only one instrument.
si fuioit li keurs car il i a II toiles, et par aventure si cope on celi desus et demore celle desoz.	If the heart fails because there are two valves, and by chance one above is cut and the other below remains.
Or la recovient coper, et est li dolor double, et a la mundification qui est dou dal n’est mie asseuree li pointe dou membre;	Or if it recovers, it feels doubled pain, and at the cleansing that comes from the removal of the bone, the point of the limb is not securely held.
et a la mundification de l’ungle par aventure eschaipe li fer, et corront l’uevre, et maintes fois naissent ensi qu’il n’ont mestier de mundification et je l’ai veut.	and during the cleansing of the nail, the iron might escape and damage the work, and many times they grow such that they do not need cleansing, which I have seen.
De la mondification qui est faite as forces a tout le liien de fil ai je troveit la bonteit de l’experiment, car les forces taillent justement ausi bien desus com desoz.	As for the cleansing that is done with force on all the length of the thread, I have found its goodness through experimentation, for it cuts evenly both above and below.
Car quant tu presses ta main, si tailles igalment en I tout soul tens;	For when you press your hand down evenly in one second.
mais que li filz soit bien estrois entor lou cuir;	but make sure the threads are tightly woven around the leather;
et soit li maniere dou premier ovraige si est que tu faices penser l’enfant, s’il entent, que tu ne li fais fuer que liier le fil entor la verge tant soulement, et pues le fai esjoir en toutes les manieres que tu pues;	and that the way of the first work is such that you make the child understand, if he hears, that you are only tying the thread around the rod, and then let him try all the ways that he can.
puis le fai ester entre tes mains tout droit, et repont les forces entre tes mains ou desoz tes piez que li enfes ne les voie, ne aucun des estrumens;	Then hold it upright between your hands, and hide the cords between your hands or under your feet so that the child does not see them or any tools.
puis boute ta main a la verge et souffle ou keur, et la trai en haut tant que li chiés de la verge soit ens;	Then place your hand on the root [of the dislocation] and blow towards the heart, drawing it upwards until the head of the shoulder is in.
puis la mundifie bien de l’ordure qui i est assemblee, puis lie le leu signiet d’un fil double, puis la lie desoz I poc a I autre liien;	Then cleanse it well from the dirt that has gathered there; then bind the joint with a doubled thread, then bind it under the buttock with another binding.
et la tien as II dois par la seconde lieeure au pouchet et au doit indice, et cope entre les II liiens, puis lieve le keur desus hastanment et trai le chief de la verge;	and hold it thus with the second band at the pouch and index finger of the hand, and cut between the two bands; then raise the heart quickly upwards and draw the head of the shoulder.
puis laisse corre le sanc poc et poc, car c’est li muedres;	then let flow the blood from buttock to buttock, for this is the cure.
et met poudre sus et sus la poudre I drapeil glueit d’un moieuf d’uef cuit destempreit d’aigue rose, confit avec oile roset boin et fres, et lou laisse sus jusc’a l’autre jor, et le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and put powder on it and on the powder a bandage of a half of a cooked egg yolk tempered with rose water, mixed with good fresh rose oil; and leave it thus until the next day, and treat further until he is healed.
Li forme des forces a la mundification si est ceste:	The formula for preparing the plaster is as follows:
li dui chiés soient tenves et soient trenchans, et soient li chiés ausi grant com li mainche igalment:	Let the two halves be thin and sharp-pointed, and let the heads be likewise large and equal in size to a hazelnut:
li error de la mundification si est quant li keurs dedens fuit a l’incision;	The error of washing is when the heart fails during an incision;
donques il covient que tu l’estendes a ton ungle, ainsois que li leus faice aposteme;	Therefore you must stretch it to your fingernail before the place forms an abscess.
et le cope igalment, et se tu ne lou pues tenir a ton ungle, si le tien as tenailles, et puis le cope.	And cut evenly; and if you cannot hold it with your fingernail, then use tongs to cut it.
Et s’il trespassent III jors, et ceu qui est desoz la verge est enflez, si le laisse tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez, et l’escorche legierement;	And if they pass three days, and the area below the bone is swollen, let it be until the abscess is quieted, and scrape it gently.
si le cope si com tu pues mues, et te garde de la partie de la verge, ce ne li nuira niant.	Then cut as much as you can move, and be careful around the bone; this will not harm anything at all.
Cure donques le leu de choses soudans plaie de poudre, que nos avons dit ou traitier des poudres, et s’on cope dou keur outre mesure, et il va au desus, si ne nuira point;	Therefore treat the place with powder for sudden wounds, as we have said when treating powders; and if you cut into the heart too much, and it goes upwards, then it will not harm.
cure le donques, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Therefore treat it, as we have said, until it is healed.
dou retenement de l’urine	On the retention of urine
Li retenue de l’urine si est d’opilation de piere, ou de sanc congeleit, ou de bowe, ou de char nee, ou de semblans choses, que nos avons dit en la division;	The retention of urine is due to the obstruction of a stone, or coagulation of blood, or bowels, or birth, or similar things, which we have mentioned in the division.
et se li urine n’est desliie , et tu vois estre la retenue por la piere qui est jai ou col de la vessie, si covient que li malaides soit corbés sus ses genoulz;	And if the urine is not released, and you see that it is retained because of a stone in the neck of the bladder, then the patient must bend over on his knees.
et li soient mis li piez sor le dos, et estende son ventre de la partie desus lou dos, et restraigne li malaides s’alainne tant com il puet;	And have him place his feet on his back, extend his belly from the part above his back, and let the patient strain as much as he can;
et adonques est constrains li colz de la vessie a l’expression de la piere au desus, por coi li urine est desliie e;	and thus the neck of the bladder is pressed for the expulsion of the stone above, so that the urine is released.
et s’elle ne vient, si com nos avons dit, et li malaides sent grant dolor, si covient que tu i aministres extraction a tout l’estrument qui est apelez «siringue», de coi ci est li forme:	and if it does not come out as we have said, and the patient feels great pain, then you must perform an extraction with all the instruments called 'syringe', of which this is the form:
et soit d’argent subtilz legiere chevee, si com li penne d’un oiseil;	and it should be made of thin, light silver wire, like a bird's feather;
et soit li caine d’une palme de lonc et demie, et soit subtilz au chief.	And the tube should be one and a half palms long, and thin at the tip.
Et li maniere de l’issue de l’urine si est que tu pren I fil double, et lie au chief I poc de laine ou de couton, et boute le chief dou fil dedens la siringue;	And the method of extracting urine is that you take a doubled thread, and tie at its head a ball of wool or cotton, and put the head of the thread inside the syringe;
et cope la superfluiteit de la lainne et le boute jusc’au chief de la siringue, puis oint la siringue d’oile ou de burre et d’aubin d’uef, et fai seoir le malaide sus I siege, et li arose la vessie et la verge d’oile moiste et d’oile d’olive et d’aigue tede;	And remove the excess of the linen and place it up to the top of the syringe, then oil the syringe with oil or butter and ashes of eggs, and make the patient sit on the seat, and raise the bladder and penis with moist oil and olive oil and hot water.
puis met legierement la siringue en la verge, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la verge, puis double la verge desus devers la boude;	Then gently place the syringe in the penis until it reaches the root of the penis, then bend the penis upwards towards the belly.
puis boute la siringue avant jusc’a la vessie, et la sente li malaides venir jusc’a la chose vuide, et ceu n’est mie fait selonc cest ordre fuer que por ceu que li conduis ou elle vait est tors;	Then push the syringe forward until it reaches the bladder, and the patient feels that it has reached its destination. However, if this is not done correctly according to this procedure, it may be because the tube leading there is twisted.
puis estent le fil a tout la laine poc et poc, et li urine en suit la laine, puis l’estrai fuer, et fai corre l’urine;	Then stretch out the thread along with all the linen slowly and gently, and let the urine follow the linen, then remove it quickly, and direct the flow of urine.
et rencomence la siringue tant que li vessie soit vuidie, et soit aligiez li malaides.	And continue with the syringe until the bladder is emptied, and the patient feels relieved.
des maladies de la vessie	bladder diseases
Quant escorcheures ou sanc vient en la vessie, ou porriture i est assemblee, et tu i vues distiller aigues et medicines, si fai a tout l’estrument qui est apellé «clepsedre», et c’est li forme:	When urine or blood enters the bladder and decay accumulates there, and you see water and medicine being distilled out of it, do this with all the instrument called "clepsydra," and its shape is:
Elle est close, et si a III pertus:	It is closed, but has three perforations:
II d’une part, et I d’autre, si com tu vois;	Two on one side, and one on the other, as you can see;
et li leus chevez par coi li medicine cort soit telz qu’il estoupe bien la verge sens adition, si c’on em puisse traire la moistor, et bouter quant mestier est;	And the high place is raised so that the medical compress may fit tightly on the wound without needing additional padding, so that moisture can be drawn out and applied when necessary;
et quant tu vues giter tes medicines en la vessie, met le chief dou keusteur en la moistor, et trai au traiant qui est ens;	And when you see your medicines going into the bladder, place the head of the catheter in the moisture and draw while squeezing what is inside.
si trairas la moistor au kesteur, et puis reboute fort le traiant ens;	Then draw out the moisture from the catheter, and then strongly push the catheter back in;
si entrera li moistors ens, et venra a la vessie maintenant, si que li malaides la sentira;	So the moisture will enter and go to the bladder now, so that the patient will feel it.
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil dont on clisterize la vessie:	And this is the form of the subtle enema used to irrigate the bladder.
si est ci:	Here it is
Et est d’argent ou d’archaut, et est li chiés plus haut;	It is made of silver or brass, with the head higher up;
et desoz a I sein ou li liiens chiet;	And below has one seam where the ligature falls.
puis pren une vessie de mouton et i met la moistor dont tu vues clisterizer la vessie, puis la lie entre les II seins forment d’un boin fil double, et chaufe I poc celle moistor sus le feu;	Then take a sheep's bladder and put in the moisture you want to use to irrigate the bladder, then tie it between the two seams with a doubled thread, and heat one part of that moisture over the fire;
puis boute le chief dou clistere en la verge, puis estrain ta main sus la vessie a tout la moistor avenanment, tant que li malaides sente que celle moistor est jai venue a la vessie;	Then place the tip of the clyster in the rectum, then press your hand on the bladder until all the moisture arrives, until the patient feels that that moisture has reached the bladder.
et se tu n’as la vessie, si pren une piece de parchemin, et en fai I cercle, et le perce rondement entor;	And if you don't have a bladder, take a piece of parchment, make it into a circle, and pierce it evenly all around.
puis boute I fil fort en ces pertus, puis assemble le cercle si com on assemble I dal, et met dedens ceu que tu vues d’oile et de moistor et d’aigue, et le lie en l’estrument;	Then insert a strong thread through these holes, then gather the circle as one gathers a net, and put within it what you want of oil and moisture and water, and tie it in the instrument.
et fai si com tu as fait de la vessie, de presser a ta main tant que li moistor veigne a la vessie.	And do as you did with the bladder, pressing your hand until the moisture reaches the bladder.
de la piere	"from the stone"
Nos avons jai dit en la division les manieres de piere, et l’estraction ensamble medicines;	We have already discussed in the chapter on stones their types and combined extraction methods;
et ai dit la difference entre la piere enjanree as rains, et toz les signes, et en queil piere on doit ovrer de taille;	and I have spoken of the difference between kidney stones and bladder stones, all their signs, and in which stone one should operate by cutting.
et en la vessie, et en la verge;	and in the bladder and in the rectum;
et je le vos dirai apertement et briément.	And I will tell you plainly and briefly.
Je dis que li piere qui est enjanree en la vessie si avient plus sovent as enfans, et c’est signe que li aigue saut de la vessie semblans a aigue en sa subtiliteit;	I say that stones which are inserted into the bladder happen more often to children, and this is a sign that water jumps from the bladder similarly to water in its subtlety;
et i apert harene, et graite li malaides sa verge, et li pent maintes fois, et puis enroidist;	And it opens widely, and the patient's penis becomes hard, and he pants many times, and then it becomes rigid;
et a mout de ces saut li fondemens;	And many of these jumps cause foundation problems;
et est legiere li sanation des enfans jusqu’il ont IIII ans, et est mout grief en viellars, et est as jones moiene, a ces qui sont entre jonesce et viellece;	and is easy to treat in children until they are four years old, and is very severe in the elderly, and is moderate in young men, those who are between youth and old age;
et est li cure plus legiere de ces qui ont la piere grans, que de ces qui l’ont petite.	And it is easier to treat those with large stones than those with small ones.
Et quant nos venons a la cure, si couvient premier mundifier le malaide per clistere, por traire tout le fiens qui est as intestines.	And when we come to the treatment, it is first necessary to cleanse the patient with an enema, in order to remove all the waste that is in the intestines.
Car il encombre aucune fois a querir la piere.	For sometimes it hinders searching for the stone.
Puis prenez le malaide par les piez, et lou deboutez et movez au desoz, si que li piere dessende au parfont de la vessie, et saille aucune fois dou leu haut;	Then take the patient by the feet, and lay them down and move them below so that the stone descends to the bottom of the bladder, and sometimes comes out from above;
puis le fai seoir entre tes mains appareilliet, et ses mains soient desoz ses cuisses, si que li vessie soit toute declinans aval;	Then have him sit between your hands prepared, and his hands should be under his thighs, so that the bladder is completely tilted downward;
puis la quier et la touche dedens;	Then seek and touch within [the dislocation].
se tu sens la piere en l’espaice, si te haste maintenant de taillier sus la piere.	If you feel the stone in the space, then quickly cut above the stone.
Et s’elle ne chiet au touchier dou tout, si moille ton doi indice d’oile de la main senestre, se li malaides est enfes, ou ton doi moien, se li malaides est jovencelz acomplis;	And if it does not fall out on touching completely, then moisten your left-hand index finger with oil, if the patient is a child, or moisturize your middle finger if the patient is mature.
et le boute en son fondement, et quier la piere, et quant tu la sens a ton doi, si l’amoine au col de la vessie;	And insert it into its base, and seek out the stone, and when you feel it with your finger, guide it towards the neck of the bladder.
puis presse sus a ton doi, et la boute au defuer lai ou tu vues taillier.	Then press with your finger, and push it to the outside where you see to cut.
Et comande au ministre qu’il presse la vessie a sa main, et li comande qu’il estende a sa main destre les coions en haut, et a sa main senestre oste le cuir qui est desoz les coions en la partie ou on fait la taille;	And instruct the helper to press the bladder with their hand, and command the patient to extend their right hand upwards, and with their left hand remove the skin that is underneath the pubic hair in the area where the incision will be made.
puis i boute le spatumile copant, de coi ce est li forme:	Then insert the spatula like this:
Et fent entre ceu qui est entre les coions et le fondement, ne mie em mileu mais au costeit de la naige senestre;	And make an incision between what is between the pubic hair and the buttocks, not in the middle but on the left side of the navel.
et soit drois sus la piere, et tes dois soit adés ou fondement, et soit li taille dou traver si qu’ele soit large par defuer, et dedens estroite, selonc la quantiteit de la piere, ne mie trop grans;	And let it be right upon the stone, and your two hands always at the base, and hold the cutting edge so that it is wide on the surface, and narrow inside, according to the quantity of the stone, not too large.
par aventure la presse si li dois qui est ou fondement, qu’elle saut fuer sens travail;	Perhaps the pressure from the hand at the base may cause it to slip without effort;
et saiches qu’il i a teil piere ou il a angles, et marges:	And know that there are such stones with angles and edges:
si est griés a issir;	It is difficult to remove them
et si a teil qui est souez, semblans a une glant, et reonde, dont li issue est legiere.	And some are smooth, like a glass marble, and round, from which the exit is easy.
A celi donques ou il a angles et marge, fai la taille plus grant;	Therefore, for those with angles and edges, make your incision larger
et s’elle ne saut, si covient que tu estraignes sus as tenailles qui sont ausi com une lime au chief, por mues estraindre la piere si qu’elle n’eschaipe;	And if it does not come out, then you must extract with forceps that are like a pair of tongs at the end, to move and extract the stone so that it does not escape;
ou tu boute desoz li I estrument subtil corbé au chief;	Or you insert underneath it a fine, curved instrument at the tip
et se tu ne la pues engignier ensi, si eslarge I poc lou pertus, et se li sans decort, si l’estrainche de vitriole;	And if you cannot grab it this way, then widen the hole a little, and if blood oozes out, stop it with vitriol
et s’il i a plus d’une piere, si boute premier la plus grant au col de la vessie, puis cope sus, puis le trai fuer, et les petites aprés s’il en i a plusors.	And if there is more than one stone, first place the largest at the neck of the bladder, then cut above it, then burn the track, and then the smaller ones afterwards if there are many.
Et s’elle est mout grans, si la covient soier, et faire plus grant plaie.	And if it is very large, then it must be done carefully, causing a larger wound.
Car II choses avienent au malaide:	When two things happen to the patient:
ou il muert, ou li urine vient adés par lai que li leus ne puet souder;	Either he dies, or urine flows constantly where the wound cannot heal.
mais toutevoie t’efforce dou traire, ou dou debrisier as tenailles, tant que tu la traies par pieces;	But nevertheless, try to remove it with forceps, or extract it with tweezers, piece by piece;
et quant tu as acomplit ton oevre, si emple la plaie d’encens et d’aloe et de sanc de dragon, et l’estraint, et met par sus I drapeil moilliet en oile et en vin, ou en oile et en aigue rose et aigue froide, por apaisier l’aposteme chaut;	And once you have completed your task, fill the wound with incense and aloe and dragon's blood, then bind it, and place over it a wet cloth soaked in oil and wine, or oil and rosewater and cold water, to cool the hot abscess.
puis resovine le malaide sus son col, et ne desliier lou lien jusc’au tier jor.	Then cover the patient with his cloak, and do not untie the bandage until the third day.
Et quant tu le desliies, si arose mout bien lou leu d’oile et d’aigue, puis le cure d’oignement dyafinicon et d’oignement basilicon, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when you do untie it, wash the wound very well with oil and water, then dress it with balsam of Joppa and balsam of Basilicon until it is healed.
Et se apostemes chaus vient en la plaie et corrosions, et congelemens de sanc en la vessie, et soit par ceu retenue li urine, qui est conue en teil maniere que sans saut avec l’urine:	And if hot abscesses and corrosion appear in the wound, and clots of blood form in the bladder, causing urine retention that occurs in this manner without any pain with urination:
boutes donques ton doi en la plaie, et estrai celui sanc, car s’il i remaint, si corront la vessie, et la porrit;	Then press your thumb on the wound, and extract that blood, for if it remains there, it will corrupt the bladder and cause it to swell.
puis leve la plaie d’aigue et d’aisil et de seil, et li aide en toutes les manieres que tu seis, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then wash the wound with water and wipe it clean with a cloth or bandage, and assist him in every way you know until he is healed.
et covient que toutes les oures que tu le cures, que tu li lie les II cuisses, et assemble les medicines sus le leu.	And it is necessary that all the times that you treat him, you bind his two thighs together and apply the medications on the spot.
Et se li piere est petite, et ele est ou conduit de la verge, et fichie ens, et li urine ne puet issir;	And if the stone is small, and it is in the passage of the penis and stuck within it, and urine cannot pass out
si le cure de ceu que je dis ainsois, que tu lou tailles maintes fois, est on escusez de la taille per ceste cure.	then the cure that I mentioned earlier, cutting him many times, is excused from cutting for this cure.
Je ai ja ce proveit ensi.	I have already proven this to be so.
Pren .i. foret de fer selonc ceste forme et soit a .iij. angles fichiees en .i. tison:	Take one iron rod according to this shape and having three prongs forged into one piece of charcoal:
puis pren I fil et lou lie entor la verge desoz la piere, si qu’ele ne puist venir arrier en la vessie;	Then take a thread and tie it around the penis below the stone so that it cannot move back into the bladder
puis boute le foret en la verge legierement, tant qu’il viegne a la piere;	then insert the probe gently into the penis until it reaches the stone
et torne le foret a ta main en la piere poc et poc, tant que tu puisses percier la piere d’autre part;	and turn the probe with your hand against the stone, little by little, until you can pierce through to the other side of the stone
si venra tantost li urine, puis presse ta main sus ceu qui est demorez de la piere qui est dedens la verge.	If urine comes quickly, then press your hand upon what remains of the stone inside the penis.
Si est tantost brisie, et saut fuer avec l’urine, et est garis li malaides;	If it breaks soon, and jumps out with the urine, the patient is healed;
et se tu ne pues ce faire por aucune chose qui le deffent, si lie I fil desoz la piere et I autre desus, puis fent la verge endroit la piere entre les II liiens, puis l’estrai fuer, et deslie lou liien, et mundifie lou sanc congeleit qui est en la plaie;	and if you cannot do this for any reason that hinders it, then tie a thread underneath the stone and another above it; then make an incision in the penis at the stone's location between the two threads; then pull it out, untie the thread, and cleanse the wound with congealed blood.
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and continue treating him until he is healed
de la piere des femmes	Of the stone of women
Poc avient que piere soit enjanree en femmes, et s’il avient aucune fois, si est li cure grief, et est deffendut por III choses:	It sometimes happens that a stone gets lodged inside women, and if it does happen occasionally, its treatment is difficult, and it is prohibited for three reasons:
l’une est que per aventure li femme est vierge;	one reason is that perhaps the woman is a virgin;
et li seconde est c’on ne puet trover femme bien saichant qui se descuevre as mires, meismement quant elle est caste.	and the second reason is that one cannot find a skilled woman who can uncover herself for physicians, especially if she is modest.
Et li tierce maniere si est que par aventure on ne puet trover femme bien saichant en cest art de mains;	And the third manner is that perhaps one cannot find a skilled woman in this field of medicine;
et li quarte maniere si est que li piere de la femme si est plus em parfont que li piere de l’ome, por coi il i couvient faire plus parfonde taille, et grant paour i a. Et se necessitez semont a ceu, si covient que tu preignes une mieresse bien sachant, et a poines la trueve on, et se tu n’en trueves, point si quier I caste mire subtil;	And the fourth manner is such that the stone of the woman is more profound than that of the man; therefore it must be cut deeper and there is great fear involved. And if you advise them to do this, then you must take a knowledgeable doctor with little experience, and if you cannot find one, search diligently for a skilled surgeon
et li presente une baile bien saige en la vie des femmes, ou une femme qui saiche une partie de l’art, et li comande qu’ele faice ceu que tu li comandes de l’inquisicion de la piere;	And present to him a wise woman who understands the lives of women or a woman who knows some part of this art, and instruct her to perform what you command regarding the examination of the stone
et regarde mout bien se li femme est vierge:	and examine very carefully whether the woman is a virgin
adonques li covient bouter son doit ou fondement et querir la piere;	Then she must put her finger into the fundament and search for the stone
et s’ele la trueve, si la constraigne desoz son doit, et li recomande qu’elle boute son doit ou con la malaide, et quiere et presse sa main senestre sus la vessie forment.	And if she finds it, she should press down on it with her finger and instruct the patient to lie on their back, then insert her finger into the vagina and seek and press firmly with her left hand on the bladder.
S’elle la trueve, si covient qu’elle la mueve de greit en greit des l’entree de la vessie jusque desoz, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la cuisse;	If she finds it, then she must move it little by little from the entrance of the bladder until it reaches below the root of the thigh
puis cope sus la piere en la racine de la cuisse encontre le mileu dou con, lai ou il est mues apparilliet, et sent la piere en celle partie;	Then strike upon the stone at the root of the thigh against the middle of the knee, where it moves and appears distorted; feel the stone in that part.
et ne mueve son doi desus la piere ou desoz, et soit li taille au premier petite;	And do not move his toe above or below the stone; let the cut be small at first.
puis boute lou rait en la taille, se tu sens la piere si acroi la plaie tant que li piere puisse issir fuer, et saiches que maintes manieres de pieres sont:	Then insert the probe into the cut; if you feel the stone, widen the wound until the stone can exit forcefully; know that there are many kinds of stones.
c’est a savoir, petites et grans et aspres et souez, longes et reondes, et qui ont rains.	 namely: small and large, sharp and smooth, long and round, and those with roots.
si saiches les semblances por savoir l’issue.	if you know their appearances to recognize the outcome.
Et se li sans te vaint, si met au leu vitriole broiet, et li tien une houre tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	And if blood is abundant, then put powdered vitriol in the wound; hold it there for an hour until the blood stops flowing.
puis revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer, et aies des estrumens que je t’ai dit en l’estraction de la piere as homes por toi aidier en ton oevre;	Then return to your work until the stone is expelled; have tools ready that I told you about for extracting stones from men to help you in your task.
et se li sans te vaint, et c’est de l’artere qui est copee, si met la poudre sus le leu et l’estrain de tentes et de bendelz, et ne rencomencier plus ceu, et laisse la piere et ne la traire mie, que par aventure morroit li malaide;	And if blood flows abundantly, and this is due to an artery being cut, then place powder on the wound; press it with bandages and cloths; do not resume cutting again; leave the stone alone and do not attempt to remove it, lest the patient die.
puis cure la plaie.	Then heal the wound.
Et quant li chalor dou sanc est apaisie, et li leus porrist, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer.	And once the heat of the blood is subdued and the spot is healed, then return to your work until the stone is removed.
de hernie carnouse	Here's a possible translation of the given Old French text into modern English:
Ramice aquouse n’est autre chose que assemblee de moistor ou blanc syfac, qui est desoz lou keur des coions, que contient l’uef;	A white substance is called ramice aquouse that is located under the liver of hens, which contains the egg;
et est apelez «syfac», et aucune fois est proprement en la toile de l’uef, si c’on cuide que ce soit I autre oef;	and is called 'saffron,' and sometimes it is properly found in the membrane of the egg, so that one might think it to be another egg;
et c’est li cuir dou coion entre lou blanc syfac que nos avons dit;	And it is the skin of the hen between the white saffron we have mentioned;
et ceu n’avient se poc non.	There would not be any if not.
Et li generation de cest ramice si est de foibleteit que vient as coions, et est espandue celle matiere.	And the formation of this hernia occurs due to weakness in the testicles, with the matter being spread out and expanding
Et aucune fois si vient de percussion sus les coions, et ceste moistor si a maintes colors:	Sometimes it comes from striking hens, and this moisture has many colors:
ou c’est color declinans a jaunice, ou c’est sans rouge, ou noir, ou aquous blans, et ce avient plus;	Either it is colored declining towards yellow, or it is red without, black, white, aqueous and watery, and other things happen;
et ce sont li signe de conoistre ceste assemblee, car s’elle est ou blanc syfac que nos avons dit, si est li apostemes reons, I poc lonc si com li figure d’un oef, et n’apert mie li coions, car il a moistor tout entor.	And these are the signs to know this assembly: for if it is in the white saffron we have mentioned, then the abscess will be round and long like the shape of an egg, and it will not burst open because there is moisture all around.
Et s’il a moistor en la propre toile, si est li apostemes reons avec une partie de l’uef, et por ceu pense on que c’est uns autres oef;	And if there is moisture in its own lining, then the abscess is ripe with part of an egg, and therefore it is believed that this is another egg.
et se li moistor est entre le cuir des coions et le blanc syfac, si le sent om bien;	And if the moisture is between the skin and the flesh, then one can sense it well.
donques quant tu vues savoir la color de la moistor, si esprueve a tout l’intromissoire quarreit, de coi li forme est ci devant.	Therefore, when you want to know the color of the moisture, test the entire instrument with square openings, as its shape is shown here.
Selonc ceu donques qui vient aprés l’intromissoire, juge de ceu qui est dedens.	Therefore, based on what comes out after using the instrument, you can make a judgment about what is inside.
Et quant nos la curons par fer, si covient que li malaides soit sainiez selonc som pooir et la repletion de son cors;	And when we cauterize it with iron, then the patient must be strengthened according to his ability and the fullness of his body.
puis le sovine sus son dos, sus une chose un poc haute, et met desoz lui mout de drapelz;	Then have him lie on his back on something slightly raised, and place many blankets underneath him;
puis sié sus sa senestre, et comande au ministre qu’il sié a destre, et estende la verge a l’un des II costelz dou keur des coions;	Then sit on his left side, and instruct the assistant to sit on his right, and extend the cautery iron towards one of the two ribs near the heart of the lung.
puis pren le spatumile leit, et cope le cuir des coions parmi leu dou lonc jusque delez lou poignil, et soit ta fendure toute droite en devisant le cuir des coions jusc’a syfac blanc, et l’escorche subtilment selonc tom pooir;	Then take the spatula and make an incision in the skin of the lung near where the long muscle joins the chest wall, ensuring that the cut is straight and reaches down to the white flesh of the lung. Then strip it thinly according to your ability;
puis perce lou syfac plain d’aigue a I large pertus, et estrai toute l’aigue, et puis met tes oncines, et estent lou syfac amont;	Then pierce the bladder full of water with a large opening, and remove all the water, and then place your bandages, and let the bladder remain above.
et ne touchier le keur des coions, mais que le syfac soulement;	And do not touch the heart of the kidneys, but only the bladder itself.
cope tout ou par pieces meismement le costeit de lui subtil, que se tu ne le copes bien saigement, si revenra li aigue;	Remove it all or in pieces yourself carefully, so that if you do not cut it well, water will return
et se l’uef saut fuer a ton oevre, si le ramoinne en son leu quant tu avras acomplit l’uevre dou syfac;	And if the egg jumps out during your work, put it back in its place once you have finished the task with the bladder
puis assemble les II leivres dou keur des coions a une costure, puis le cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then sew together the two layers of the kidney's heart using stitches, then heal it as you would other wounds until it is healthy.
Et se tu trueves l’uef corromput d’autre maladie, si covient que tu lies les vasselz que sont suspensoire, en doutant le decorrement de sanc;	And if you find the egg corrupted by another disease, then tie up the vessels that suspend it, preventing blood flow.
puis cope le coion a tout le suspensoire, et estrai l’uef, et le cure si com nos avons dit.	Then cut the kidney along with all its suspensions, remove the egg, and heal it as we have said
Et se aigue est assemblee en II parties ensamble, saiches que ce sont II ramices;	And know that if water is gathered into two parts together, they are both branches.
si cope l’autre partie si com tu as fait la premiere igalment, puis essue lou sanc, et met en la plaie lainne moillie en oile roset;	If you cut the other part just as you did the first one evenly, then wipe away the blood, and put moist lint soaked in rose oil into the wound.
et met defuer autre laine moillie en vin et en oile, et met sus les II coions, et met desus drapelz doublés, et le lie sus a tout le liien qui est selonc ceste forme:	And put another piece of moist lint soaked in wine and oil on top of the two wounds, then place doubled cloths over them, and tie it all together according to this method:
Puis pren II drapelz, et les emple de laine charpie selonc ceste semblance et soient assemblez par cousture en la gorle des braies, et li uns des chiés preigne sus le fondement jusc’au dos, et li autres a la partie dou poignil;	Then take two cloths, fill them with lint according to this shape and sew them together at the waistband of the breeches, one should cover the buttocks up to the back, and the other should cover the elbow area.
et li autre dui chief sus les II angres, et soit toute assemblee li restreinture en la boucle dou braier;	And the other two ends should be tied together over the two angles, and all the restraints should be gathered together at the loop of the breeches.
et aucune fois est medicinee ceste ramice de cautere en leu de taille de fer, et est que tu preignes I cautere cultellaire subtil, et cope le cuir des coions, et soit eschaufez si com nos avons dit, si que li syfac blanc que contient l’aigue est descovers;	And sometimes this dressing is used instead of iron branding, and you should take one scalpel, carefully cut the skin around the wounds, heat it as we have said, so that the white surface which contains water is exposed.
si pren lou cautere selonc ceste forme, et perce celui syfac as oncines, et l’escorche a cest subtil cautere chaut:	Take the cautery according to this form, pierce the skin thusly once, then scrape it with this subtle hot cautery.
Et lou cope en toutes les manieres que tu pues, tant que tu esraiches tout;	And cut in every way you can until you remove everything;
et garde que li feus ne touche l’uef;	and make sure the fire does not touch the eye;
et saiches que ceste oevre est plus salve;	Know that this operation is safer.
et mues gardans de decorrement de sanc, et muedres que li ovraiges de taille;	Move cautiously to avoid bleeding and close the incision.
et se nulle chose te fait contraire, ou aposteme chaus ou decorremens de sanc ou autre chose, si cure ce qui te fait contraire, selonc ceu qui est devant dit.	And if anything goes wrong, such as an abscess forming or bleeding occurring or any other issue, treat it according to what is written above.
Et se li malaides est paourous, et ne vuet atendre cest ovraige por son horribleteit, si amenistre perforation, si com je te di, et est que quant tu es bien certains par les significations que nos avons dit que ramice aquouse est lai, si fai seoir le malaide sus I siege leveit;	And if the patient is fearful and unwilling to undergo this procedure due to its horrifying nature, perform a perforation as I instruct you. When you are certain that the patient has lain down on his left side according to the signs we have described, make him sit upright on a raised seat;
pues perce l’aposteme an la partie desoz a tout le spatumile large, et met la perforation dou lonc dou cors;	Then pierce the abscess at its lowest point near the entire scrotum and insert the hot iron of the cautery into the body.
et soit larges li pertus, si que toute li aigue corre fuer;	And let the opening be wide enough so that all the water runs freely.
puis met coton sus le leu, et le lie, et laisse por corre le remenant de l’aigue, puis le cure tant que li plaie soit sanee;	Then place cotton on the wound, tie it, and let the rest of the water flow out; then treat it until the wound is healed.
et se li blainche toile ne laisse issir l’aigue en la bouche de la plaie, si covient que tu i boutes une penne ou l’estrument dont on trait l’aigue des ydropiques, de coi li forme est ci devant;	And if the white cloth does not let water flow out of the mouth of the wound, then you must insert a feather or the instrument used to treat water from dropsies, the shape of which is shown here.
et eslarge I poc la plaie, et saiches que li aigue revient, et est assemblee aprés VI mois ou enqui entor, et quant elle est assemblee si com devant, et ensi passera li malaides ses jors.	And widen the wound's opening, and know that when water returns and gathers again after six months or so, then it will be assembled as before; and thus the patient will pass their days.
de l’aposteme des coions	"wound of the birthing canal"
Saiches que en la section de ceste ramice a paor em plusors dispositions, por coi il me semble que mues vaut c’on la laisse;	Know that in cutting this artery there is danger and many difficulties, which is why it seems to me better to leave it alone.
et je vos dirai l’ovraige et les semblances de l’aposteme.	I will tell you the work and the similar things about an abscess.
Je dis donques que maint aposteme vienent ou cors, et meismement as coions;	I say therefore that many abscesses come to be in the body, especially in the thighs.
et c’est par mout de cas.	And it often happens.
C’est a savoir par superfluiteit aigre et ague, qui est espandue as coions, ou de percussion;	It is known to happen due to acute acidity and heat, which spreads to the joints or occurs due to impact;
et est li color de l’aposteme selonc la color dou cors;	And the color of the abscess matches the skin color;
et ne trueve point de dolor, et est aposteme grief;	And there is no pain felt, yet it is a serious abscess;
et par aventure est uns apostemes griés paourous et pierous, et de fuxe color, et aucune fois vient de nout d’artere, ou d’enfleure de voine.	Sometimes an abscess may be pale and purple, and have a foul smell, and sometimes it comes from near an artery or swelling of a vein.
Quant c’est par nout d’artere, si est conus par la disposition d’aposteme chaut, quant tu la presses a tes dois;	When it is near an artery, it is recognized by the hot appearance of the abscess when pressed with two fingers;
et ne covient mie que tu i touches.	And you should not touch it.
Cil qui est fais d’enfleure de voine est conus par sa disposition a l’expression dou touchement des dois, et puet om bien faire la taille sus ceste semblance, et sus les autres chars;	That which is caused by swelling of a vein is recognized by its appearance when touched with two fingers, and one can also perform the incision on this type of abscess, as well as others.
et est que tu cope lou keur des coions, puis estent l’uef en haut, et le trai fuer dou blanc syfac, et delivre lou suspensoire de toutes pars de l’uef.	And you should cut the skin of the joints, then stretch it upwards, and the egg-white-colored tissue should be delivered from all around the egg.
Se li uef est ja sodez avec ces chars nees, si covient donques que tu traies l’uef, et lou cope;	If the egg is already hard-boiled with these new roots, then you must draw out the egg, and remove the shell.
et s’il est aers au syfac, ou en ceu qui est dedens les vasselz, si covient que tu delivre toute celle tenve, et la cope reondement.	And if it is air-filled in the syringe or those inside the vessels, then you must release all that tension, and cut around neatly.
Et se li naissance de la char est ou leu derrier, si covient que tu la copes toute, et estrai l’uef, si com nous avons dit.	"And if the birth of the flesh is behind the joint, then you should cut all of it and extract the egg, as we have said."
Et quant tes ovraiges est acomplis, si emple la plaie de laine moillie en oile roset et en vin, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	"And when your work is complete, dress the wound with oil and wine-soaked wool, then apply other dressings until it is healed."
de l’aposteme des coions	"wound of the birthing canal"
Cis est uns apostemes envoloupez d’un envoloupement semblant a I borjon, avec le mollifiement des coions, et se muet li malaides griement quant il vait;	This is an abscess enclosed in an enclosure resembling the testicle, with softening of the joints, and the patient cries out in pain when he walks.
et li cure de ceste maladie si est bien pres ausi paourouse com ceste ci devant, et toutevoie nos vos dirons l’ovraige de li, selonc ceu que li ancien firent.	And the treatment of this disease is also as dangerous as the one mentioned earlier, yet we will tell you its workings according to what the ancients did.
Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus I siege aleveit, puis li boute le suspensoire des coions aval a tes dois, a tout le vasseil qui sont prochien a la verge, et les teigne li maistres, et les estende forment;	You must make the patient sit on an elevated seat, then place the suspension device for the testicles below your hands, near all the vessels close to the penis, and hold them gently but firmly.
puis cope au spatumile trenchant large dou traver endroit les vasselz, tant qu’il soient descovert, et puis escorche de chescune part, si com nos avons dit en l’estraction des arteres qui sont en temples;	Then cut sharply and wide with the scalpel across the vessels until they are exposed, and then strip from each side as we have described in the extraction of arteries in the temples.
puis i fiche une aguille ou il ait I fil double, et le lie au premier leu ou li vis est venue, et le lie derechief a l’autre chief;	Then he inserts a needle where there is double thread, and ties it to the first place where the wound appeared, and ties it again at the other end.
puis les cope em mileu droitement, selonc la longesce dou cors, et en trai les moistors corrumpues;	Then cut the threads evenly in the middle according to the length of the body, and remove the corrupted moisture.
puis cure la plaie si com les autres ou on enjanre bowe, si que aucun vassel chiecent que norrissent l’un des coions;	Then dress the wound as one would for other injuries caused by a blow, so that no vessel may fall out of its place.
car par ceu n’i vient point de mal, et se a toz les vasselz vient vis, si covient traire les coions a tout les vasselz;	For this reason, there is no harm done, and if blood comes from all the vessels, then one must draw out the threads from all the vessels.
si que li oes ne perde son norrissement por l’incision des vasselz, et sechent et ne se puient aidier.	So that the bone does not lose its nourishment due to the cutting of the vessels, and they dry up and cannot help each other.
de la routure dou syfac	"on the rupture of the scrotum"
Li avenemens de ceste ramice si est par la section que vient ou syfac, ou l’estension sus le ventre en la partie des angres, por coi li intestine dessendent de celle routure a l’un des coions;	The outcome of this procedure is the opening that comes from the groin or the extension on the abdomen in the region of the hips, through which the intestines descend towards one of the threads.
et ceste routure est ou dou syfac, ou de l’estension de li, et vienent ces II manieres de mout de causes:	And this opening is found either at the groin or from the extension of it, and these two ways come from many causes
ou de percussion, ou de saut, ou de braire, ou de levement de grief faix, et par semblans choses;	From blows, from falls, from throwing oneself down, from lifting heavy weights, and similar causes.
et li signes quant c’est de l’estension dou syfac, si est qu’il avient poc et poc, en lonc tens, et ne vient mie soudainnement;	And the sign when it is due to stretching of the hip joint is that it happens gradually, over a long period, and does not come suddenly.
et est li apostemes igalz jusque vers le parfont, por ceu que li syfac apresse l’intestine.	The abscesses are even up to the depth because the hip pushes on the intestines.
Et li signes est quant c’est de la section dou syfac, qu’elle fait venir a l’encomencement dolor soudaine, et est li apostemes divers apparans, desoz le cuir pres, et c’est por l’issue de l’intestine et le cors au defuer dou syfac.	"And the sign of this rupture is that it causes sudden pain at the beginning, and there is uneven swelling under the skin near the scrotum, due to the exit of the intestines from the body through the opening in the scrotum."
Et aucune fois dessent li cirbes avec l’intestine, et est retenus enqui, et fait grant dolor soffrir au malaide, meismement quant il est pressez.	"Sometimes the testicles also descend with the intestines and become trapped there, causing great pain for the patient, especially when they are pressed upon."
Et en ces cures de fer a paor, por coi il s’en covient eschuir.	"And in such cases where there is fear of injury from iron, one must avoid using it."
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que tu comande ou malaide qu’il ramoine l’intestine a sa main au dedens en la plaie, s’il i puet rentreir;	And the manner of treatment is that you instruct the patient to insert their hand into the wound and push back the intestines if possible.
puis soit sovinez sus son col. entre tes mains, et lieve les cuixes;	Then press firmly on his neck with your hands and lift up the thighs;
puis estent le keur au desus, et cope tout le cuir des coions dou lonc;	then raise the heart above them and cut away all the long sinews of the hips.
puis boute dedens les leivres de la taille uncines selonc ceu que tu en as mestier por ovrir la plaie, et soit telz que li oes em puist issir;	Then insert hooks into the sides of the waist according to what you need to open the wound, and make them wide enough for the bladder to come out.
puis escorche lou syfac que est desoz lou cuir des coions, tant que li blans syfac dur soit descovers de toutes pars;	Then strip off the hip joint that is beneath the long sinews of the hips until all sides of the white hard bone are exposed.
puis boute ton doi indice en ceu qui enseut lou coion, en ceu qui est entre lou blanc syfac qui est desoz lou cuir de l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac, et depart ceu qui est derrier l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac;	Then place your two index fingers into that which instructs the loin, that which is between the first lumbar vertebra below the skin of the kidney and between the second lumbar vertebra, and separate what is behind the kidney and between the second lumbar vertebra.
et pues muef a la main destre dedens lou keur des coions, et estent lou blanc syfac en haut a ta main senestre, et lieve l’uef a tout lou syfac devers la taille;	And then move your right hand inside the kidneys' heart, and stretch the lumbar vertebra upwards with your left hand, and lift the kidney towards the lumbar vertebrae at the waist.
et comande au ministre qu’il estende l’uef en haut, et deslie ceu qui est aers derrier le liement;	And instruct the assistant to extend the kidney upwards, and loosen that which is behind the ligament.
et quier a tes dois s’il a point de l’intestine envoloupeit ou blanc syfac dur, et se tu en trueves aucune chose, si le boute au ventre desoz;	And seek with your two hands if there is any intestine wrapped around or hard lumbar vertebra, and if you find anything, put it back into the abdomen below.
puis pren une aguille ou il ait I gros fil fait de X filz, et la boute en la derriere partie dou syfac, qui est aprés lou cuir des coions;	Then take a needle with a large thread made of silk, and insert it into the rear part of the lumbar vertebra, which is behind the kidney's skin.
aprés la taille, puis cope les chiés qui apperent des filz, tant qu’il i ait IIII filz;	After the waist, then cut the heads that appear from the threads, until there are four threads remaining.
puis les assemble l’un sus l’autre en maniere de croix, et en lie lou syfac, dont nos avons dit qui est desoz lou cuir des coions, d’un fort liien de II pars;	Then they put them together one on top of the other in the shape of a cross, and tie it with sinew, which we have discussed earlier, being underneath the skin of the thighs, with a strong thread of two parts.
