puis envoloupe les chiés des filz, et les lie forment de II pars, si que nuls des vasselz que les norrissent ne puissent entrer en ous, que aposteme chaus n’i viegne;	Then wrap the heads of the thighs and tie them firmly with two parts, so that none of the vessels that nourish them can enter inside, lest any abscess come there.
et met derechief le liien selonc le premier liien lonc II dois de celui, et aprés ces II liiens laisse dou syfac qui est desoz lou keur des coions le grant d’un doi;	And then place the second tie according to the first one, two fingers away from it. After these two ties, leave some sinew that is under the skin of the thighs for a finger's length.
et aprés tout l’autre selonc la rondesce que li euf porte;	And after everything else, shape it according to the roundness that an egg has.
puis cope en la partie qui est desoz le cuir des coions, tant qui li sans corre, et li bowe, si com nos avons dit ci devant;	Then cut into the part that is under the skin of the thighs until blood flows and the bowels, as we have said earlier
puis amenistre laine moillie en oile, et met em plaies, et i amenistre le liien que nos avons dit.	Then prepare wool moistened in oil, place it on wounds, and bring the tie that we have mentioned.
Et aucune fois est cauterizez li blans syfac que nos avons dit, aprés l’incision, par doutance de decorrement de sanc.	"And sometimes it is necessary to cauterize the white fibrous tunic of the scrotum that we have mentioned after the incision, in case of excessive bleeding."
Car ce avient maintes fois, et laisse le liien tant qu’il chiece per lui;	For this happened many times, leaving the ligature to fall through itself.
et s’il tarde au cheoir, si soit arosez d’aigue chaude, et met sus ceu que nos avons dit, tant qu’il chiece;	and if it is delayed in falling, let it be raised with warm water, and place upon it what we have said until it falls.
puis cure la plaie d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	then heal the wound with another remedy until it is perfectly sound.
de hernie carnouse	Here's a possible translation of the given Old French text into modern English:
En ceste ramice ne vis je onques nul qui osast faire la cure par fer.	In this branch of medicine, I never saw anyone daring to treat by iron.
Et li ancien dirent qu’ele est faite si com li ramice qui est ensamble la vis, en teil maniere que tu lie les vasselz, aprés la taille sus ous legierement au desoz;	And the ancients said that it is done like the branch which is bound around the wrist, tying the vessels lightly after the incision below.
puis cope em mi, et cure l’aposteme de ceu qui oevre, tant que li vasselz chient;	then cut through it in the middle, and heal the abscess with what opens until the vessels fall out;
et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and heal it as we have said until it is sound.
Aucune fois vient routure ens angres, si com nos avons dit, et apert li leus;	Sometimes a rupture occurs in the angles, as we have said, exposing the place;
et ne dessent nulz des intestines as coions, et s’il en i dessent, c’est poc, et repaire toutes houres;	and no intestines descend to the corners, and if any do, it is little, and repair them all hours.
et toutevoie s’il demoure trop en cest point, si croit li plaie ou syphac, tant que li intestine dessent;	And yet if it remains too long in this place, the wound becomes large or inflamed until the intestines descend;
et ceu avient par l’estension dou syfac qui est as angres, si com nos avons dit, car il est estendus, puis est mollifiez et enflez li leus et apert;	And this happens due to the stretching of the sinew which is at the joints, as we have said, for it becomes stretched, then softened and swollen the place and opened.
et li cure si est par cautere, si com nos avons devant dit;	And its treatment is by cautery, as we have previously stated;
et aucune fois est curee par fer en ceste maniere:	Sometimes it is treated with iron in this manner:
et est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos entre tes mains, puis cope le leu de la routure enfleit dou large selonc la quantiteit de III dois;	And the patient lies on their back between your hands, then cut the swollen place of the rupture three finger-breadths wide;
et puis estrai le syfac qui est desoz le cuir que l’ensuet, puis pren lou rait et lou met sor le leu apparant dou syfac;	Then extract the sinew that is under the skin where it was cut, then take a thread and place it over the exposed surface of the sinew;
et lou presse au parfont dou ventre, puis cout les II leus apparans dou syfac sus lou chief dou rait, et cout l’un et l’autre;	And press it at the depth of the abdomen, then sew up the two exposed surfaces of the sinew over the head of the thread, and sew both one and the other;
puis estrai le chief dou rait, et ne coper point dou syfac ne n’estendre l’uef n’autre chose, si com je t’ai fait savoir en la cure de la ramice des intestines;	Then remove the head of the thread, and do not cut into the sinew nor stretch it further, as I have taught you in the treatment of intestinal prolapse;
puis le cure par la cure des plaies.	Then treat it with wound care.
Et quant tu copes les filz, si le mundefie et cure la plaie, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	When you cut threads, cleanse it and dress the wound until it is healed.
Li syfac est constrains, et n’a point d’apparance en la routure, et li cauteres est muedres en cest leu, et plus prochiens a salut.	"Gangrene is constrained and does not appear in the rupture; cauterization is milder in this site and closer to healing."
de l’amollissement dou cuir des coions	Regarding the softening of the skin of the scrotum
Maintes fois est amollis li cuirs des coions en aucuns homes, por ceu que les chars que sont dedens sont mollifiees, et est lait a veoir;	Often the skin of the thighs becomes softened in some men because the flesh inside is softened, and it is easy to see.
et est mestier, quant on le vuet curer, c’on faice gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et li cope le cuir qui est mollifiez sus le cuir natureil;	and when you wish to treat it, make the patient lie on their back, and cut away the softened skin from the natural skin.
puis assemble les II levres a une costure, et se tu vues, cout premier la superfluiteit dou cuir mollifiiez a III costures ou IIII fermement;	Then join the two lips together with a suture, and if you wish, first sew up the excess softened skin with three or four stitches firmly.
puis cope entre les costures, et lou cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez, et chient li fil.	Then cut between the sutures, and heal it like other wounds until it is sound, then remove the thread.
dou chastrement	Regarding castration
Saiches que chastremens est escomeniez en nostre loi, et por ceu il me plairoit que je n’en parlasse mie en cest livre;	I know that astrologers are reproved in our law, and therefore I would like not to speak of them in this book.
et n’est necessaires fuer que por II manieres:	And it is necessary to make an exception for two reasons:
dont l’une est que li mires en saiche respondre quant on li demandera, et en saiche la cure;	one reason being that the doctor should be able to answer when asked about it and know its treatment.
et li autre, por ceu que nos avons sovent mestier de chastrement d’aucunes bestes por nos aidier, si com de bouc et de mouton et de chait et d’autres bestes.	And the other one, because we often need to castrate certain beasts to help us, like goats and sheep and cats and others.
Je dis donques que chastremens est fais selonc II manieres:	I say therefore that castration is done in two ways:
ou par atraction, ou par fendure.	Either by attraction or by cutting open.
En celle que nos faisons par attraction, faisons nos seoir la beste en aigue chaude, tant que li coion soient mollifiez et pendant;	In the one we do by attraction, we make the beast sit in warm water until the testicles are softened and hanging down;
puis les preing a ta main, tant qu’il soient remis et que tu ne les sentes plus.	Then grasp them with your hand so they are held back and you no longer feel them.
Du chastrement de taille:	On castration by cutting:
covient que tu teignes la beste, et li presse le cuir des coions a ta main senestre, puis lie le suspensoire, et cope sus chescun oef a I cop, quant tu les avras bien escorchiez;	It is necessary that you tie down the beast, press the skin of the testicles with your left hand, then tie the suspensory ligament, and cut each one with one cut after you have well scraped them.
et i laisse aucun poc dou syfac et lou subtil syfac qui est sor les vasselz;	And leave some small part of the scrotum and the thin skin that is over the vessels;
et ceste maniere de chastrement est muedre que cele qui est faite par attraction, por ceu que a l’atraction demoure par aventure aucune chose des coions, par coi li beste desire luxure;	And this manner of castration is more effective than that done by attraction because sometimes some part of the testicles remains, causing the beast to desire lust.
puis cure la plaie tant qu’ele soit sanee.	Then heal the wound until it is healed.
des hermofrodites	Of hermaphrodites
Hermofrodie est selonc II manieres as homes:	Hermaphroditism exists among men in two ways:
l’une si est que entre les II coions apert ausi com li figure de la nature d’une femme, ou il ait poil, et aucunes fois en cort li urine.	The first way is when between the two testicles opens also like the figure of the nature of a woman's genitals, with hair growing there, and sometimes it is opened even in the skin.
Et li autre maniere si est en femmes, et ait sus lou poignil ausi com une verge et II coions.	And another way in women, they have on their pubis both a penis and two testicles.
Et li cure de l’ome et de la fame si est que tu copes les chars ajostees toutes, et les cure si com autres plaies;	And the treatment for both men and women is to cut away all the attached skin, and heal it like other wounds;
en la seconde maniere, des homes dont li urine saut par lou cuir des coions, si n’a point de cure.	In the second way, there are those men whose urine flows through the skin of the testicles, for whom there is no treatment.
de la tentigene	Of tenaciousness
Tentigene est une chars ajostee sus la partie natureil, tant qu’elle est trop laide a veoir;	Tentigene is an attached skin on the natural part that is too ugly to see;
et aucunes femmes l’ont ausi grant com une main, et c’est li cure.	And some women have it as large as their hand, and this is its treatment.
Il covient que tu teignes la superfluiteit de la tentigene a ta main ou as oncines, et la cope legierement;	You must shave off the excess skin of the tentigene with your hand or scissors, and cut it away gently;
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne, puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	And do not go too deep, so that there is no bleeding, then heal it with other remedies until it is healed.
et a une autre char que naist a la bouche de la marris, et l’emple, et par aventure saut fuer, et est selonc la semblance d’une kowe, et por ceu l’apelerent li ancien «maladie kowee».	And there is another ulcer that appears at the mouth of the womb, and the belly button, sometimes it jumps fire, and is like the appearance of a cow, therefore the ancients called it 'cow disease'.
Si covient que tu la copes, si com nos avons dit la tentigene, et la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	If it is necessary to cut it, as we have described for tenetio, and continue treatment until it is healed.
de erratique	Of erratic
Erratique si est quant li nature de la femme n’est mie percie, ou li pertus est petis;	An error occurs when the woman's nature is not pierced, or the hole is small;
et est naturez par naissance, ou accidens par maladie que venue i est;	and it is either natural from birth, or accidental due to illness that has come about there;
ou c’est par char ajostee, ou dou syfac subtil ou espés, et est fais em parfont en la marris, ou en costez, ou desoz, ou que soit;	or it is caused by adherent flesh, either thin or thick, and it is formed deeply within the womb, or on the sides, or below, wherever it may be;
et deffent le concevoir, et l’enfantement, et par aventure les flors a avoir;	And prevents conception, childbirth, and sometimes the flow of menstruation;
et li connoissance de ceu si est par le regart de la baile.	The knowledge of this is by the appearance of the womb.
Se li estoupemens est prochiens apparans, si quier a tes dois ou au rait.	If the stoppages are close at hand, then seek them with your two fingers or the reed.
S’il est dou syfac subtil, et il est prochiens as II leivres, si te haste, et la ront ensi:	If it is thin and close to the second leaf, then hasten and cut around it like this:
met tes II dois indices ensamble, et li femme soit sus son dos, espandues ses jambes;	Place your two index fingers together, and have the woman lie on her back with her legs spread;
puis estent les II leivres forment, tant que li subtilz syfac soit rons, et soit overs li estoupemens;	Then are the two books so shaped that the subtle sieve is round, and it overlies the stoppers.
puis pren laine, et la moille en oile, et la met sus le leu, et gise li femme a home chescun jor, si qu’il ne puist souder.	Then take wool, wet it in oil, place it on the spot, and lay the woman on her back each day so that it cannot dry.
Et se li syfac est dur et espés, si covient que tu lou copes au spatumile semblant a foille de mirte.	And if the bone is hard and dense, you must cut it like a leaf of laurel.
Se li estoupemens est de char nee, si la sospent a l’oncine et la cope;	If the stopper is of newborn flesh, then suspend it on the donkey's horn and cut it off;
et aies les medicines estainchans sanc, si com acaice, sanc de dragon, encens, ensamble abun d’uef;	And have ready blood-stopping medicines such as achiote, dragon's blood, frankincense, mixed with egg yolk.
puis amenistre une caine de plonc large, si que li plaie ne puisse souder;	Then prepare a wide lead funnel so that the wound cannot heal shut;
et ensi soit longement, et li amenistre une tente de lin sec;	And so let it be for a long time, and let them provide a tent made of dry linen.
puis soit curez d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then other treatments should be applied until he is healed.
Et quant en la marris vient char nee, si la covient coper selonc ceste maniere, se ce n’est apostemes enchancrez.	And when flesh-colored matter comes to the wound, you must cut it according to this manner, unless it is an incurable abscess.
Car a l’aposteme enchancreit qui est en la marris, ne doit on touchier de feir.	For an incurable abscess that is in the wound, one must not touch it with fire.
des emorroides	Emorroides are swollen veins that occur around the rectum and anus. They can cause discomfort, pain, and bleeding during bowel movements. Here's how they were described by ancient physicians:
Emorroydes sont overtures de voines dont sans cort acostumeement, et quant les emorroydes sont vielles si devienent thelul;	Hemorrhoids are veins that normally do not release blood, and when hemorrhoids become old they become hard (thelul).
et nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’aus, et les signes, et je dirai ci celles qui resoivent curation.	And we have already spoken in the section on their likeness and signs, now I will speak of those that require treatment.
Je di que les emorroides et li thelul, quant il sont em parfont en la marris, et il n’aperent au sentir, si n’est mie li cure par fer.	I say that hemorrhoids and piles, when deeply embedded in the marrow, and cannot be felt upon examination, are not suited for iron treatment.
Cil qui sont a la bouche de la marris, c’on puet sentir, sont cil c’on puet curer.	Those which are at the mouth of the anus, that can be felt, are those which can be cured.
Il covient donques que tu mettes la femme en une maison froide, puis estent l’altelul as tenailles, et le cope en ses racines, puis poudre sus medicines restraignans sanc, si com acaice et sanc de dragon et encens, et semblans choses;	It is therefore necessary that you place the woman in a cold house, then set the altar with pincers, and grasp the womb by its roots, then powder it with medicines that restrict blood, such as acacia and dragon's blood, and similar things.
puis boute ses piez a la paroit une houre, puis la met en aigue froide;	then place her feet against the wall for an hour, then immerse her in cold water.
et se decorremens de sanc i vient, si la fai seoir en une decoction de sumac et d’escorce de pomes grenates et de gales et de semblans choses, et puis pren farine d’orge, et la confis avec miel et aisil, et en fai I emplaustre sus son dos.	and if blood flows abundantly, then make her sit in a decoction of sumac and pomegranate bark and gall nuts and similar things, and then take barley flour and mix it with honey and bile, and apply the poultice on her back.
Et se il estainche, c’est boin.	And if she is cured, that is good.
Se ceu non, se li fai aerdre ventouses au dos et as mameles sens ferir;	If not, make her swallow leeches placed on her back and breasts without piercing them.
puis pren lainne, et la moille en jus de plantain ou en jus d’aglentier avec vin viel, et fai aerdre au leu.	then take linen, wet it in plantain juice or elderberry juice with old wine, and apply it to the affected area.
Et quant li aposteme repose, si cure lou leu d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez;	And when the abscess has broken, then dress the wound with ointment until it is clean.
et celle qui est apelee «albathir» est rouge, et est semblans a I chief aspre, si le covient coper si com j’ai dit le thelul;	And that which is called 'albathir' is red, resembling a sharp head, thus it must be covered as I have said earlier.
et puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And then care for him until he is healthy.
des apostemes de la marris	Of boils of the belly
Maintes manieres d’aposteme vienent en la marris, si com chancre et aposteme pierous et herpes et estiomenes et fistules et emorroides et aposteme chaut, et plusors autres maladies que j’ai dit en la division.	Many kinds of abscesses occur in the marrow, such as cancer and bone abscesses, herpes, chilblains, fistulas, hemorrhoids, hot abscesses, and many other diseases that I have mentioned in the divisions.
Il covient donques que je die en cest traitier l’aposteme chaut qui vient en la marris, qui n’est mie des apostemes que coillent bowe;	It therefore behooves me to discuss in this treatise the hot boil that appears on the buttocks, which is not among those that burst.
et se tu vues savoir l’ovraige de fer, si regarde se li apostemes est agus en l’encomencement de sa venue, et plain de chalor et de fievre, et s’il devient rouge se tu le pues veoir.	And if you wish to know the work of iron, look to see if the boil is hot at its beginning, full of heat and fever, and turns red as you can see.
Adonques ne te haster mie de percier, mais lou fais meurer tant que li dolor soit apaisie;	Therefore do not hasten to pierce it, but make it burst when the pain is subdued;
et puis fai seoir lou malaide sus I siege, et ait II petis sieges ou il se cline, et apoie sus son dos et assemble ses piez as parties defuer la jambe;	and then have the patient sit on a chair, with two small chairs for them to lean on, and support their back while bringing their feet together.
et soient ses cuixes espandues, et mette ses braz desoz ses genous, et les lie bien d’un boin liien;	And let their thighs be spread wide, place their arms beneath their knees, and bind them securely with a good bandage;
puis succe li baille devers lou destre costeit, et i amenistre l’estrument dont on oevre la bouche de la marris, de coi ci aprés vient li forme;	Then follows the bile towards the right side, and there brings the tool with which one opens the mouth of the gallbladder, about which comes later its form;
et covient que quant tu i vues amenistrer cest estrument, que tu fiches le rait premier ens por savoir la parfondeté de la marris, si que ceu qui entre ens de l’estrument n’i viegne plus em parfont qu’il ne doit, et qu’il ne blece la malaide;	And it is necessary that when you bring this tool there, you first insert the reed to know the depth of the gallbladder, so that what enters from the tool does not go deeper than it should, and does not harm the patient;
et se li estrumens est plus grans, si covient covrir la parfondesce de la marris de drapelz, si que li estrumens ne li grieve;	And if the tool is too large, then one must cover the depth of the gallbladder with rags so that the tool does not cause injury;
et covient qu’il mette le cornet de l’estrument au desus, et qu’il teigne l’estrument.	And it is necessary to place the funnel of the tool on top, and to grease the tool.
Et quant li apostemes apert, et on lou fent a la main mol, si le covient coper au chief, au spatumile leit;	When the abscess opens, and one cuts with soft hand, then it is necessary to cover it with warm linen;
et quant li bowe est vuidie, si covient que tu mettes en la plaie tentes moillies en oile roset, ou en oile vert sec;	When the gallbladder is emptied, then you must put in the wound clean rags moistened with rose oil or dry green oil;
et met la tente fuer de la plaie au parfont de la marris, et met par defuer sus la marris et sus le poignil lainne nette moillie en aigue ou malves soient cuites;	And place a hot cloth on the wound, and put it over the wadding, and lay on top of that a linen cloth moistened with water or mallows that have been cooked.
puis le cure aprés II jors d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then, after two days of appropriate ointment application, until it is healed.
et aucune fois leve on la marris et la plaie par clistere d’aigue et de miel, et puis d’aigue ou racines de lis et aristologe longe soient cuites;	And sometimes lift off the wadding and the wound with an enema of water and honey, then water in which lilies and long-stemmed aristolochia have been cooked.
puis reveigne a l’oignement.	Then reapply the ointment.
Et se li plaie est reponue en la marris, si covient que tu te gardes de cuire de fer, mais cure la si com nos avons dit en la division.	And if the wound is located in the marrow, then it is necessary that you guard against cooking with fire, but cure it as we have said in the division.
de l’enfantement	Of childbirth
Mestier est premier a la baile qu’elle conoisse la figure de l’enfantement natureil, et li signes si est quant tu vois la femme apresser aval, et desire odorer l’ar:	It is first necessary that she knows the figure of natural childbirth, and the signs are when you see the woman bearing down and wanting to smell the air.
adonques se haste li enfes de fuer issir;	Then the child quickly emerges from outside.
adonc saiches que cil enfantemens est selonc la figure natureil, et est li issue soz son chief, et li secondine avec lui;	Therefore know that this birth is according to the natural form, and the afterbirth is beneath its head, along with the child.
et quant tu vois ces signes, si covient presser legierement son ventre, si que li enfes isse tost;	And when you see these signs, then gently press her belly so that the child emerges quickly.
car quant il dessent sus son chief, si ist li secondine avec lui, et est mondee li marris de ses superfluitez par bone mundification;	Because when it descends upon its head, so also does the second one with it, and the uterus is cleansed of its excesses by good cleansing.
et cist qui vient autrement ne vient mie naturelment.	And that which comes differently does not come naturally
Car il vient aucune fois sus ses piez, et vient fuer li cors ou li chiés, et les mains, ou il vient sus son ventre, ou sovin, et est convertis par aventure sor son col, et par autres figures malvaises;	For sometimes it comes on its feet, causing the body or head to bend over backwards and the hands to stretch out, or it comes on its belly, or at times it turns upside down on its neck, assuming various evil forms;
si est mestier a la baile qu’elle soit saige et subtilz en ces choses, et se warse d’error et de decevement, et je vos mostrerai toutes les figures coment on li doit aidier.	Therefore it is necessary for the midwife to be wise and skilled in these matters, watchful against error and deception, and I will show you all the forms and how one must assist her.
Se li enfes vient sus son chief par issue natureil, et li femme enfante griement, et li vertus de li est foible, si la fai seoir sus une selle, ou les femmes la tienent;	If the child comes out on its head naturally and the woman delivers it with difficulty, and her strength is weak, then make her sit on a saddle or have women hold her up;
et arose sa nature d’oile ou fenugreic soit cuit, et puis boute li baile entre ses dois le petit spatumile dont ci est li forme:	and raise her nature with oil or cooked fenugreek, and then place the little spatula between her thighs, of which this is the form
et fende la secondine, et cope a son ungle tant que li moistors qui est ens corre fuers;	and pierce the secundine, and cut with its nail until the moisture within flows out;
et preint lou ventre de la femme tant que li enfes dessende, et s’il ne dessent, si covient clisterizer la femme de muscillaige de fenugrec avec oile de sisament;	And press down on the woman's belly until the child descends; and if it does not descend, then you must administer to the woman a suppository of ground fennel seed with sesame oil.
puis la fai preindre et esternuer de condisi, et tien sa bouche et son neis une houre:	then make her inhale condimentum and sneeze; hold her mouth and nose for one hour:
si istra maintenant l’enfes.	The child will now be born.
Et se les II mains issent fuer, si covient que tu les ramoinne legierement poc et poc;	And if the two hands come out first, you must gently push them back little by little;
et s’elles n’i puent entrer, si met la femme sus I siege, et li lieve les piés en haut;	and if they cannot be pushed back in, then have the woman sit down and lift her feet up.
puis deboute le siege sus terre, et teigne on la femme, qu’elle ne chiece au deboutement;	then tilt the chair towards the ground, and hold onto the woman so she does not fall during this maneuver;
et se li mains n’i puet entrer, et li enfes muert, si li cope les mains au couteil qui est ci devant mis, et estrai l’enfant, et ramoine igalment.	and if the hands still cannot be pushed in and the child is dying, then cut through the skin at the joint placed beforehand, extract the child, and reset it evenly.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses piés	after the child emerges feet-first
Quant li enfes vient sus ses piez, si lou covient bouter en haut;	When the child comes onto his feet, then you must lift him up.
et puis le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit igalz;	And then slowly turn him bit by bit until he is even;
puis preigne I des piez et l’estende poc et poc.	Then seize one of the legs and stretch it gradually.
Cant il saut jusc’as cuixes, si la comande a preindre, et la fai esternuer de condisi;	When it reaches the thighs, then command him to grasp it, and let him sneeze accordingly;
si saut fuer, se Deus vuet.	If fever occurs, God willing.
Et s’il n’ist fuer si com nos avons dit, si le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit selonc la figure natureil.	And if it does not come forth as we have said, then turn it little by little until it is according to the natural figure.
Car adonques ist il legierement.	For then it will come forth easily.
Et s’il ne vient fuer si com nos avons, dit si pren muscillaige de altee, et oile de sisament, et gomme fondue, et broie tout en I mortier;	And if fever does not occur as we have said, then take musk, aloe, sesame oil, melted gum, and grind them all together in one mortar;
et met sus la nature de la femme dedens et defuer cest oignement, puis la fai seoir en aigue tede jusque desoz les costelz;	And place this ointment on the woman's womb and keep her sitting in hot water up to her chest;
et quant elle est moillifie desoz, se li fai I coliere de mirre, et li met desoz, et li laisse une houre;	And when she is warmed underneath, place for her a collar of myrrh, put it beneath her, and let her wear it for an hour;
puis la fai seoir sus I siege, puis la fai esternuer et estraint sa bouche et son neis, et li preint le ventre legierement, car li enfes saut maintenant.	Then have her sit on a chair, then make her sneeze and hold her mouth and nose, and gently press her belly, for the child is coming out now.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses genous	"of the birth of the child onto her knees"
Quant li enfes vient en ceste forme, si i mette li baile ses mains poc et poc;	When a child arrives in this form, then the bailiff puts his hands softly and softly.
puis soit sovinee sus son col, et li pendent li piez aval, et soit gisans sor I lit;	Then he is suspended by his neck, with his feet dangling down, lying on the bed
et plie ses mains poc et poc, et puis li preint les mains sus lou ventre, et li oste les cussins desoz, tant qu’elle soit appareillie aval;	And folds his hands gently and gently, then he takes the hands onto the belly, removing cushions underneath until it's aligned below
et se li enfes ne saut, si pren ses piez et li muef forment, puis li muef lou ventre amont, puis i boute tes mains;	If the child does not jump, take his feet and shake them firmly, then move your belly upwards, then place your hands
et ewe l’enfant poc et poc;	And raise the child gently
et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse.	and instruct the woman to hold on until the child comes out
de l’issue de l’enfant qui vient dou large une main pendant	"of the birth of the child that comes from the womb with one hand held back;"
I covient engignier a ramener la main:	I must devise how to reset the hand
s’on ne la puet ramener, si fai lever la femme, et aler;	If it cannot be reset, then have the woman stand up and walk around
s’elle ne puet aler, si la fai gesir sus I lit, et li deboute les jambes forment;	If she cannot walk, then have her lie on the bed and forcefully raise her legs
puis amenistre lou muscillaige que j’ai conteit;	then apply the muscilage that I described
et s’elle n’enfante, si la fai seoir sus I siege, puis estudie au rameneir la main;	And if she does not give birth, have her sit on a seat and then examine how to reset the hand
et ewe l’enfant selonc la figure natureil, et la fai esternuer, et li comande qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse fuer.	Wash the child according to its natural figure, and make it sneeze, and instruct her to take so much that the child passes wind.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus son col, et ait espandues ses mains, et sa faice tornee devers lou dos sa mere	"of the birth of the child onto its neck with hands spread out and face turned towards its mother's back;"
I covient que li baile teigne sa main, puis le torne poc et poc, et l’ewe legierement;	It is necessary for the servant to take his hand, then turn it little by little, and wash it gently;
et quant il est igalz, si met sus la nature muscillaige de altee et oile, si com nos avons dit, puis li comande qu’elle se mueve poc et poc;	And when it is even, put on the muscular nature of old mallow and oil, as we have said, then instruct her to move little by little;
et quant tu avras ce fait, si la fai seoir sus I siege, et li comande k’elle se preigne;	After you have done this, make her sit on the seat, and instruct her to take it;
et la fai esternuer.	And make her sneeze.
de ceste meisme maniere a tout la secondine	"In the same manner for the afterbirth;"
Quant il vient fuer en ceste maniere a tout la secondine, si cope la secondine a ton ungle, tant que li moistors soit vuidie;	When the child passes wind in this manner throughout the entire afterbirth, cut off the afterbirth with your fingernail until all moisture is emptied;
et se li enfes pent sus sa faice et sus son col, si la cope des la boude, qu’elle ne soit retenue, et muere li enfes;	And if the child lies on its face and neck, cut off the umbilical cord at the navel so that it is not retained, lest the child die;
puis boute l’enfant dedens, tant que tu l’aies mis si com il covient, et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne aucune fois:	Then place the child inside, until you have positioned it as necessary, and instruct the woman to push once more:
adonques si istra legierement.	Therefore, it must be straightened gently.
de l’issue des gemelz	"Concerning the birth of twins;"
Saiches que gemeil naissent maintes fois, et aucune fois en naissent III ou IIII;	It happens frequently that twins are born, sometimes three or four at a time;
et ceu n’est mie estrainge chose, et poc avient.	and this is not an uncommon occurrence.
Dui sont estrainge chose, et ne vivent mie, se poc nom;	It is rare for them to live long, if they are even born.
je sai ceu, qu’il soient multipliiet, et sont desevrez par lou syfac qui les devise, qui est liiez a la boude;	I know that they are multiplied in number and are destroyed by the evil spirit who cuts them apart, which is joined to the womb;
et aucune fois issent ausi naturelment com uns tous sous, si com nos avons dit.	and sometimes they come out naturally like one whole, as we have said.
Et s’il issent griement, si la cure si com nos avons dit, et soit li baile subtilz, et faice tost et legierement ceu qu’elle fait;	And if they are born crying, then the treatment should be carried out as we have said, and the physician should be skilled and act quickly and gently.
et faice ensi com il vaut mues a salut.	He should do this in such a way that it leads to healing.
de plusors enfans	"Concerning multiple births;"
Aucune fois sont formez en la marris I ou II ou III ou IIII ou V ou VI ou VII, ou plusors jusc’a XV, et sont tout formeit en forme d’enfant par le mesurement dou saige glorious, et couvient que li baile saiche tout ceu, car par aventure semblans chose li avient;	Sometimes they are formed in the mother’s womb one, two, three, four, five, six, seven, or even more up to fifteen, and all are perfectly formed into the shape of a child by the measure of the glorious sage, and the physician should know all these things because such things may happen.
si faice selonc ceu qu’il covient.	If it is done according to what is necessary.
de l’enfant mort	Concerning a dead child:
Quant tu cures la femme de l’enfant mort ou ventre, si com j’ai dit en la division, et il ne vient fuers, et tu es constrains d’ovraige de mains;	When you treat a woman for a dead fetus or pregnancy outside of its usual course, and there is no progress, and you are compelled to intervene.
si covient que tu saiches se li femme est de saine vertut, et n’ait accident ou elle ait paor de mort;	It is necessary that you know if the woman has a healthy temperament, and whether she has any accidents or fears death.
si covient que li femme soit sovinee sus son dos, et soit ses chiés enclins aval, et les jambes levees;	It is necessary for the woman to be laid on her back, with her head inclined downward, and her legs raised.
et li ministre la teigne de II pars, ou elle soit liie au lit si qu’elle ne soit traite au dessendement de l’enfant;	And the assistant should hold her thighs at a 90-degree angle, or tie her to the bed so that she does not slide down during childbirth.
puis frotez la bouche de la marris d’oiles moistes avec muscillaige de altee et de fenugrec et semence de lin, puis oigne li baile ses mains de ces oiles et de ces muscillaiges;	Then rub the woman's mouth with moist oil made from mastic and fenugreek seeds and flaxseed, then anoint your hands with these oils and preparations.
puis les boute en la marris legierement, puis quiere I leu ou elle boute les oncines que soient covenaubles a ceu, et pren warde se li enfes est apparilliez qu’il dessende sus son chief;	Then insert your hand into the woman gently, then seek the location where she feels contractions, and ensure that if the child is coming out, it does so face down.
si fiche les oncines en ses eulz ou en son col ou en sa bouche ou en som palais ou desoz la barbe ou en la forcele ou pres des costez, et se li dessendemens est sus piez, se li fiche ou poignil et as costes moienes;	If you insert the hot iron into his eyes or neck or mouth or throat or cheeks or below the beard or in the armpit or near the ribs, and if the descent is on foot, insert it or prick at the sides of the chest.
et covient qu’il teigne l’oncine a sa main destre, et mette la corbeure entre ses dois de la senestre main, et li boute a tout sa main legierement, et fiche l’oncine en aucun de ces leus que nos avons dit, tant qu’il viegne a la chose vuide;	and he must hold the hot iron in his right hand, place the curve between the fingers of his left hand, and gently press it with all his might, inserting it into any of these places that we have mentioned until the thing is emptied.
et c’est li forme de l’oncine:	And this is the shape of the cautery iron:
puis fiche encontre I autre oncine, ou le tier se tu en as mestier, si que li estractions soit igalz;	Then insert it against the other cautery iron, or the third one if necessary, so that the extraction is even.
et puis l’estent igalment en movant d’une part et d’autre, por mues issir, et soit li oncines dentez por mues tenir, si com ci est li forme:	And then stretch it evenly by moving from one side to the other for easier removal, and let the cautery iron have teeth for better grip, as shown here:
Et s’il en demoure une partie, si oigne li baile aucuns de ses dois d’oile, et les boute en celle partie, et traie l’autre partie;	And if some part remains, then oil some of his fingers and press them on that part, and pull the other part.
et s’il en i demoure point, si met cest oncine ou plus haut leu, et fai ceu tant qu’il s’en isse tout fuers.	If it remains there not at all, place this poultice higher up and do so until all the fire exits.
Et se l’une mains vient devant l’autre, et il ne puet ramener por l’estreignement, si covient que tu envoloupes sus I drapeil, tant qu’il isse tote;	And if one hand comes before the other and it cannot return due to tension, you must wrap a cloth around it until it releases all.
puis la cope en la jointure de la plante ou au coute, et ensi covient que tu faices en l’autre main, et as II piés.	Then strike at the joint of the sole or the wrist, and likewise do so for the other hand, and for both feet.
Et se li chiés de l’enfant est gros et il est estrois en l’issue, ou il ait ou chief aigue assemblee, si covient que tu boute le spatumile espinous entre tes dois, et fent le chief et estrai l’aigue;	If the child's head is large and narrow at the outlet, or has a sharp point assembled there, you must insert the spine of the spatula between your two fingers, split open the top, and extract the point.
ou tu la ront a l’estrument qui est apelez «almidach», de coi li forme vient avec les estrumens ou chapistre qui est aprés cestui;	Or else round it with the instrument called 'almidach', from which the form comes with the instruments that are in the chapter following this one.
et ensi meisme faice se li enfes a grant chief naturelment;	And do likewise if the child is born with a large head naturally.
et puis traie fuer les osses as tenailles, et se li chiés saut fuer et il estraint a la forcele, si soit fendus, tant que li moistors qui est ou pis issue fuer;	Then pull out the bones with tongs; and if the head is stuck and held by forceps, split it open until the moisture in the piss outlet comes out.
et s’elle ne puet issir, si le cope par pieces au mues que tu pues;	If it cannot come out, then cut it apart piece by piece until you can.
et s’il est enflez au ventre ou desoz les costez, si covient que tu lou perces tant que li moistors corre.	If the abdomen or lower ribs are swollen, you must pierce it so that the moisture escapes.
Et se li enfes est sus ses piez, si est li attraction legiere, et li adrecemens a la bouche de la marris est legier.	And if the child is on its feet, the attraction is light and the directions at the mouth of the uterus are easy
Et s’il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l’estraies a I drapeil envoloupeit sus la main;	And if it is stuck in the belly or breast, you must pull it out with a cloth wrapped around your hand;
et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre;	and make an incision into the belly or breast until the moisture comes out.
et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure, si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc’a la bouche de la marris;	And if other bones remain and the head stays in place, insert your hand deeply into the socket and pull it out through the mouth of the socket;
puis i boute I oncine ou II, et le trai fuer;	then put one or two fingers inside and pull it out forcefully.
et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n’i covient mie travillier, ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses;	And if the mouth of the socket is narrowed by heat from inflammation that has come there, then do not work it further, but apply moist and fatty substances.
et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.	And use plasters for treatment, as well as warm, softening, and moistening ointments.
Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif;	And if the child is on his side, and you can make him even, then apply what we have said regarding a living child.
et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.	And if there is no power [i.e., no one available to help], then perform trepanation with caution, leaving nothing of the afterbirth behind.
Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris;	And once you have done this, if [the patient] is suffering from hot abscesses that come about in the marrow.
et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.	And if there is bleeding from the veins, let it be drawn with warm water, and other treatments applied [to the patient].
Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut .i. autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	And I saw a woman in whose belly one child had been killed, then she conceived another upon it, and the other was killed.
Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	After many days, there appeared an abscess on his cheek, which swelled until it opened, and then began to discharge copiously.
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	I was summoned to the hospital, where I pondered long and could not heal the wound.
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	I applied a plaster with strong adhesion, from which came forth one bone, and after some days another one.
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	I marveled greatly because the belly has no bones.
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	I thought that it was the bones of a dead child.
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em millor point;	I saw the wound, and many bones were injured, until the woman was at her wit's end;
et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu;	And the woman lived thus for a long time, and a little bit of bone came out from its place [i.e., the wound].
et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	I wrote this chapter so that when a master finds something unusual, he may know how to provide assistance.
dou ramener la marris a son leu	to reset the dislocation
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres;	Hereafter comes the form of the pressure [appliance], which is illustrated in books;
et a II tornans as II chiés des II liiens.	And to the return of the two heads of the two kidneys.
Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux;	Nevertheless, let the horn be more subtle than the restrictor, and let it be made of ebony or boxwood;
et soit li bouche dou fust I doi de large, et li marge des arbres I doit, et de lonc une palme et demi;	And let the mouth of the wood be two inches wide, and the edge of the tree one-half a palm long;
et enmi les II liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;	And in the two ligaments there should be two joints of this same wood that close on both ends, each half a palm long or a little more;
et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les II cornes.	And these two joints are placed in the mouth of the mallet to open when one turns the two horns.
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles;	Another form, more subtle and lighter in appearance, should be made of ebony or boxwood wood, resembling tweezers;
et ait as II chiés II ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et II dois de large;	And have at both ends two joints, each half a palm long and two inches wide;
et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor I lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes, puis boute les II ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes;	And when you want to open the mallet with all the instruments, have the woman sit on a bed with her feet dangling and legs spread apart, then place the two joints joined together into the mallet and hold the head of the instrument underneath between her thighs;
puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	Then open your hand to the instrument, just as you have done with even forceps, according to the quantity that you see opening the mouth of the wound, until the boil bursts.
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances;	These instruments are all mounted, and their appearances are multiplied;
et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	And when the physician has prepared them, the faster the operation is, and the greater it appears to people because of its quantity.
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	Do not disregard any instrument until you have prepared it, for their necessity is not negligible.
Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis;	When the secondine is retained during childbirth, you must instruct the woman to raise her buttocks and then make her sneeze with condisium powder, while holding your hands over her mouth and nose;
et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	And if she sneezes because of it, all the better.
Se ceu non, si prent I pot, et fai I pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire;	If not, then take a pot and make a hole in the lid, and put herbs that can open the mouth of the wound in it, such as calamint, rue, anise, chamomile, alkanet, and centory;
toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu;	All these herbs, or some of them, should be cooked in water over the fire.
puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris, et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris;	Then place a tube with holes from the pot's opening into the mouth of the patient and hold it until steam enters the patient.
puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.	Then make them sneeze, as we have said.
Si saut li secondine hastanment.	If the woman expels quickly
Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature, et quiere la secondine;	And if after this treatment it remains uncured and not free of fever, then order the maidservant to moisten her left hand in sesame oil or in musk-mallow ointment, then place it on the navel and rub gently.
et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction;	And when she has found it, take it and pull it out gradually and gently, so that the patient does not fall during extraction.
mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie;	But one must move it lightly to the right and left, then draw it out.
si venra et se desaerdra.	If it comes and gets disentangled
Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d’esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes;	And if the patient's mouth is narrow, we have mentioned the treatment of sneezing and fumigation with herbs.
et s’elle n’ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire;	And if it is not as we have said, then make sure you do not err in the treatment.
mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d’oignement tetrafarmaçon;	However, you must tie what is at the mouth of the womb to the woman's thigh, then perform a cleansing with oil of tetraharmacon.
si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer;	If it swells and returns, then fire will come.
mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide.	But nonetheless, when it swells, evil odor comes to the stomach and head, and harms the patient.
Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu:	Therefore, fumigations suitable for this are necessary:
aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.	Many of the ancients have proven fumigation with mustard and dried figs.
Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	The form of the instrument used to fumigate women retained in labor or delivery is as follows
Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu;	And it is similar in appearance to a cake, and one places the head carefully on its nature, and the wide heads on the fire;
et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.	and let the fumigation be upon the coals, until the thread is consumed, then begin another.
de percier lou fondement	to pierce the fundament
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:	Many children are born whose anus is not pierced but obstructed by some subtle membrane:
si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche;	Therefore it is necessary for the bath attendant to prick this part with her finger, and not pricking with a sharp point, carefully cleansing the wound so that she does not touch it.
puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then place moist linen soaked in wine and oil on it, then apply the remedy of ointment until it is clean.
Et se tu doutes qu’il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.	And if you suspect that it may become blocked again, insert a lead tube into the opening and leave it in place for several days, then remove it when the child is ready to go to bed
Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d’aposteme;	And sometimes this swelling comes suddenly from a wound or an abscess;
si covient coper celui soudement:	So one must cover it suddenly:
si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.	Whether it is cauterized, as we have said about the boil.
de la fistule dou fondement	of fistula of the anus
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des II parties, si a une fistule ou plusors;	Fistulas that come underneath the fundament are called nodations, and growths that come near to the fundament, or in the space of the anus, if there is one fistula or more;
et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe, et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans;	And when that nodation is ancient, it opens up, and emits moist foul-smelling or subtle bowels, and sometimes these fistulas are persistent;
et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	And they are recognized by this: that there is a discharge of wind or farting when the patient excretes, and sometimes one sees a worm leap out.
Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge;	And there are fistulas that pierce up to the bladder, and up to half of the penis;
et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	and reach as far as the hip joint, and even up to the knee.
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:	And thus one recognizes a fistula piercing the fundament, not the skin:
et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	and it is necessary that you insert your two index fingers into the fundament and insert a thin needle of brass or iron into the fistula where there is no winding.
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou I poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;	And if it has windings, then insert a thin reed or horsehair into the fistula until you feel the reed or hair with your finger;
et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:	and if you do not feel it and there is no discharge of air through the opening, as we have said:
saiches qu’elle ne perce mie;	know that it does not pierce.
si te haste dou curer.	If you hurry to cure it.
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	"And when the fistula persists down to the bladder or down to the passage of urine, so that urine squirts out and cannot be stopped by medication."
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;	If it pierces as far as the hip joint, then the reed comes out at that place;
s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	if there is no winding and the pain around it increases, then it is necessary to leave it be, and no medication or salve will help;
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	And for these Persian fistulas there is no remedy except effort, it is the vainty of foolish physicians who meddle with them.
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit, et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos;	In those that are not Persian nor ancient, there is hope of healing through iron; as I have experienced, and it is necessary for the patient to lie on their back between your hands.
et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;	And lift the legs up to the thighs, and keep the thighs inclined toward the abdomen;
puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	Then insert an awl or trocar if there is coiling, until you know where the tube emerges.
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice, se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet;	If the patient feels it around their anus, then you must insert your two index fingers there, until you feel that the tube has pierced through.
et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;	And when you feel between your fingers either the sigmoid or the flesh, then know that it is Persian;
si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	If not, do not work on it unless one can heal it.
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;	It is said everywhere that some can be healed well, but this happens rarely.
et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	And the aid one performs here, is to heat the cautery according to the width of the fistula, as it has been said before.
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement;	And place the heated cautery into the fistula until it reaches the bottom;
et faice ceu II fois ou III, tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	Repeat this twice or three times, until you know that these broken hairs are burnt, which resemble a bird's feather;
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	And then apply wet lint to burn until those hairs fall out, and finally apply ointment around the wound and bandage it.
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	If it is healed thus, all the better.
Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	If not, otherwise it cannot be healed;
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	And if the tent enters but does not reach the depth of the fistula, place between your two fingers and the tent a thick covering of flesh or wax, so that you can see where the fistula opens.
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	So find the entrance of the fistula, insert the tent first, and then apply the cautery afterward until it reaches the tip of the tent;
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra;	and the pain will cease, and it will fall away;
puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	then remove those shattered bones that resemble a bird's feather, so that nothing remains.
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	"And if your hand trembles and cuts between you and the work, then cauterize it with fire or with hot medicine."
Car li cauteres de feu assemble II bones choses:	For the fire cautery has two uses:
c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	that is to say, the burning of these adhering bones and the stopping of blood flow and the drying of moisture.
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	then treat moist pains with wax or crushed herbs until the place swells up and the burned bone appears in the swelling
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	then treat the wound by applying poultices of hot oils and hard grease, which are dry medicines.
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	"For when it is restored, then it is healed and does not return."
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	"And if the fistula comes from deep inside the fundament and is far away from the body, put your finger into the fundament and feel for it."
Se tu sens la tente, et entre II est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des III manieres:	If you feel the pain and between two there is cloth or skin or bone where it is about to pierce through, then use fire with caution and hope, by administering one of these three methods:
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	either cauterize it as we have said, or cut it until it reaches the bottom, or if you can, apply dressings and treat it as at first.
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	And go not too deep, lest thou touch the holding that holds the fundament; let the evacuation come forth without will.
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	Then the treatment, as we have said;
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	Perhaps it will then be healed; or remove that covering and cleanse it after it has been cut near the fundament, either by attempt or by some other pointed instrument;
puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues;	Then cleanse that faulty flesh which is in the wound as much as thou canst;
puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement:	Then consider how to restore the wound and keep the fistula away from the fundament:
si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	So that it may be easier for the patient.
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere:	And sometimes fistulas are of this manner:
et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus, si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	When thou dost thrust the needle into the fistula, and it is on the side of the fundament near the skin above, then take a needle pierced at the head thus:
Et i boute .i. fil tort en .ij., et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	"And tie one thread around two places, and put the probe all the way into the fistula until it reaches the tip."
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	If it passes into the margin of the fundament within, then pull out the thread from that piercing, so that thou dost thrust thy thumb upon the fundament;
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les II chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse I jor ou II;	And draw the head of the thread, bring together the two shoulder blades, bind one to the other, leave it for one or two days;
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	And restrain it several times until the threads cut through these tissues that lie between them and separate;
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	Then dress the wound until it is healed and clean.
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	"If the fistula does not open on its own, then make it open in every way that you can, if it is not too deep."
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	"For it is not necessary to cut so deeply for the closure and then treat it as we have said until it heals."
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	The shape of the spinal needle used to create a fistula should be thin and pointed.
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	And on the other hand not sharp, so that one does not cut what one should not cut, as you see here:
des emorroydes	"hemorrhoids"
Emorrydes sont selonc II manieres:	There are two kinds of emorydesis:
ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc, et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement;	Either they are within the fundament like grains of resin, some small and others large, there is blood on the skin at times, some have one and others have several, they are defective in the fundament or at the head of the fundament;
mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor, et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	But those that are defective lack moisture and appear on the skin with a little yellowish water or blood, having the color of flesh;
et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	And the treatment for those who have them in their fundament, it is that you instruct the patient to strain while going to the latrine, until the fundament expels them, and then they will appear.
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	If you hurry, grasp it with forceps or pinch it with your nail, then cut it at its roots;
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a I drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	And if the tweezers cannot hold them due to moisture, then grasp them with cloth or cotton, or a piece of chamois leather;
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	Then extract them with your two fingers, cut them off, and apply some warm powders in place of a cautery.
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, pues les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	Or you may cauterize them as is said in the chapter on cauteries, then treat them with other remedies until they are healed.
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	And if the fundament cannot expel them, then administer to the patient a strong and harsh enema to wash out what is in the fundament so that it can be excreted openly.
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	If the patient is unconscious, and if the hairs are forcibly removed at their base, then treatment is easy.
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	And you should grasp them with your nail or forceps and cut them, then treat them as we have said until they are healed, so that he fears incision by iron.
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere:	You must arrange the suturing in this manner:
pren I fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les II chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille, et si soit dou large;	Take one thread twisted, and pass it through a needle, then draw the thread upwards and pierce the needle on the other side, and turn both ends of the thread under the needle, and let them be wide.
et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse I por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	And pull the thread firmly, then tie it, remove the needle, and do likewise for all the others, leaving one free to correct any excess blood.
puis met sus le fondement I drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	Then place a damp cloth moistened with rose oil or wax on the base, and cover it, and instruct the patient to rest;
et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and then let him be until they fall out, and when they do, treat them with ointment and other treatment until he is healed.
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	on the drying of fecal matter on the fundament
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	Many times there is a drying of feces in the intestines, and this occurs due to constriction of nature, especially when the patient is elderly or when medication is ineffective
Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir;	If you must reset at the tip of a spatula or with your nail, scrape off the scurf on top so it does not get wet.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sodez si com il covient;	Then treat it until it is solid as it ought to be;
et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez;	And if it cannot hold fast, then start the scraping again more vigorously than before, until it bleeds freely and becomes raw.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat it until it is clean.
dou fremit	fever
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	Ants are small creatures that often appear on the body, and they bite deeply;
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	And sometimes the cold finds them, and it feels like death from trembling, spreading throughout the whole body, but especially in the hands.
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	And the treatment is this: take a cane made from a goose feather or a strong eagle feather, and place that cane on the trembling so that the circle encompasses the trembling entirely;
puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	Then twist your hand around the entire cane until you have covered all around the trembling, drive it deep inside and crush the trembling from its roots.
Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:	And if you see fit to do so with a feather of iron or steel according to this form, and it should be thin underneath and tapering at the tip
ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser.	Does not perceive, to hold the two, and press the muscles.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.	And if you see, cauterize the trembling, as it is before in the chapter of cautery.
de la forme dou clistere	of the shape of a clyster
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet;	Sometimes a silver or lead enema is made, or melted gold or hammered tin;
et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	and sometimes these tools are made small and large according to those for whom they are intended.
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	Therefore, those which are prepared for the treatment of children and those who are weak and feeble should be small
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	The shape of a small or large clyster is as follows: wide where the belly is bound in this manner
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez;	And if there is a disturbance or the belly is bound up, as you see, and the entrails are pierced within;
et ait a l’un des costez II pertus, et en l’autre I;	and there are two perforations on one side and one on the other.
et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus, et ait entre chescun pertus I doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus I fil fort de fil crut tort en X ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;	and the belly is placed where medicines are put into a beast's bladder or parchment, and is pierced all around with small perforations, and there is one space between each perforation; then strong thread of roughened wool is twisted in an X-shape or wound around, and the belly is closed like a goat.
et quant li medicine est dedens, si la lie a l’estrument devant d’un fil fort, puis clisterize;	And when the medicine is inside [the patient], then tie it to the instrument beforehand with a strong thread, and then administer an enema.
et c’est li forme dou cercle:	And this is the shape of the circle:
Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d’oile ou d’aubun d’uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement;	Let the medicine be neither too hot nor too cold, and grease the tip of the enema with oil or a mixture of egg yolk, or something similar, then insert it gently.
puis l’espreigne li ministres a ses II mains ensamble, tant qu’il soit toz vuis, puis estrai lou clistere, et lieve li malaides ses jambes a la paroit, et se li medicine vuet issir, si la teigne tant com il puet;	Then the minister presses with both hands together until it is completely empty, then remove the enema, and the patient lifts their legs towards the side, and if the medicine wants to come out, tie it as much as possible.
et s’il dort une nuit atot, si est plus grans aide.	And if he sleeps all night [after this treatment], it will be of greater benefit.
Et se tu le clisterizes em maladie de decorrement de ventre, et li medicine se haste d’issir, si le rencomence tant qu’il soit sanez.	"And if you perform a clyster on someone with abdominal descent disease, and the medication rushes to come out, then begin again until it is finished."
Et se li emorroide sont ou fondement, ou aposteme, si soit li clistere ausi subtilz com por I enfant;	And if the hemorrhoids are at the fundament or abscess, let the enema be as subtle as for a child;
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil sus coi li cuir soit estraint:	This is the shape of the subtle enema where the skin is stretched:
des plaies	"of wounds"
Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies;	We have already spoken about the treatment of wounds in the section on divisions;
or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l’acomplissement.	I shall tell you about treatments for hands and medicines according to their fulfillment.
Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu’elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.	"I say that wounds are diverse according to how they are made, and according to where the wounds are made, and of what they are made."
Les choses par coi plaies sont faites sont par gitement de piere, et taille d’espee et de couteil, ou de lance ou de fust ou de siette, ou de semblans choses;	Wounds are made by blows from stones, cuts from swords and knives, or from lances, clubs, arrows, or similar things.
ou que sont faites selonc les leus dou cors, si com plaie que chiet sus le col, ou sus le chief, ou le peis, ou le ventre, ou le foie, et semblans membres;	or according to the location on the body, such as wounds that fall on the neck, head, thigh, belly, liver, and similar limbs;
et je vos dirai la cure de chescune plaie, et encomencerai as plaies dou chief simples, car li remenbrance venra en son chapistre.	And I will tell you the treatment for each wound, beginning with simple head wounds, for memory will come in its chapter.
Je dis que quant simple plaie vient ou chief, et li os n’est brisiez, si pren garde se c’est de gitement de piere ou de semblans choses, et li cuir est toutevoie rompus et est li plaie grans, et tu doutes levement d’aposteme chaut:	I say that when a simple wound comes to the head and the bone is not broken, take care if it was caused by a blow from a stone or similar things, and if the skin is torn all around and the wound is large, be wary of a hot abscess forming.
si le fai tantost sainier de la cephalique meismement s’il vient poc de sanc de la plaie, et soit li sainie au contraire de la partie navree;	Then quickly wash it with cold water from the Cephalic source, especially if there is a flow of blood from the wound, and let the washing be done towards the opposite part of the injured area;
et eschuisse li malaides repletion de vin et de viandes grosses.	And let the patient avoid being full of wine and fatty foods.
Et s’il ne vuet sainier, si soit amenuisie sa viande, et ne boive point de vin, ne ne menjuce point de char;	And if he does not wish to recover, then his food should be reduced, and he should drink no wine nor eat meat.
et met sor la plaie, se apostemes chaus i vient, coton moilliet en oile roset soulement, ou en vin stiptice;	And put on the wound, if an abscess appears there, cotton moistened in rose oil alone or in astringent wine.
et s’il n’i a aposteme chaut, si met sus la plaie, s’elle est fresche a tout son sanc, et elle n’est muee par l’air, poudre, que je dirai un poc ci aprés;	And if there is no hot abscess, then put on the wound, fresh blood from its entirety and not moved by air, powder which I will mention later.
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucuns oignemens, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the air has moved it, then put some ointments on it until it is healed.
Et se li plaie est grans si com de tailleure d’espee et de semblans, et les levres ne se pueent assembler par tentes, si les assemble par cousture, si com je dirai as plaies dou ventre, de la costure.	"And if the wound is large, such as from a sword cut or similar things, and the lips cannot be brought together by tension, then bring them together by stitching, as I will describe for abdominal wounds."
Se li plaie est descoverte de l’os, et pent, et ne tient mais que a un poc, si le cope;	If the wound is open to the bone and gaping, and hangs only by a little, cut it off.
puis cure la plaie de medicine, et restoure char dure en leu de cuir, et comande au malaide a mengier grosses viandes, si com testes et froment cuit, ausi com poulz, et semblans choses.	Then treat the wound with medicines, and replace hard flesh in place of skin, and order the patient to eat fatty foods such as testicles and cooked wheat, also poultry and similar things.
Et se tu trueves ou cuir porriture, et il n’aert a l’os, si cope lou porrit tot, et giete fuer, puis le cure;	And if you find rottenness in the skin without reaching the bone, cut out all the rotting flesh and cast it away, then dress [the wound].
et se il ait artere en la plaie ou voine, dont sans cort, et il ne puet estainchier par medicines, si quier l’artere, et se tu la trueves desloie, si la lie d’un fil;	And if there is an artery in the wound or vein without skin, which cannot be stopped by medications, seek out the artery. If you find it dislocated, tie it with a thread.
et se ceu ne profite mie, si la cauterize.	And if this does not help, cauterize [the artery].
Et se ces plaies sont petites et simples, si est li cure legiere:	If these wounds are small and simple, the treatment is easy:
