Et est costume que li ajutoire et li jambe doient estre repris en XL jors dou tout;	It is customary for the shoulder and leg to be reset after 40 days;
et adonques lou doit on desliier et aministrer bain et medicines d’oignemens por le leu adrecier.	Then, one should untie it and apply baths and ointment medications to bring it back into place.
Et se li estricture est laide et emboee, si demore a desliier L jors ou II mois.	And if the strapping is tight and swollen, it should remain tied for forty days or two months.
de la brisure du bras	Chapter on the fracture of the arm
Li bras est compos de II os, qui sont apelez li dui «foscile», de coi li uns est petis, et est cil qui enseut le pouchet;	The arm is composed of two bones called the "two fosciles," one of which is small and extends to the elbow joint;
et li autres est grans, et est cil qui est desoz, devers lou petit doi;	and the other is large and is located underneath, towards the little finger;
par aventure brise li grans foscile soulement, ou li petis, et par aventure andui ensamble.	Sometimes only the large bone breaks, or sometimes only the small one, and sometimes both together.
Quant li petis fosciles est brisiez, li restaurations est legiere, et li sanations;	When the small bone is broken, restoration is easy, and healing occurs quickly;
et quant li grans est brisiez, si est li sanation male, et plus griés que quant il sont brisiez andui ensamble.	But when the large one is broken, healing is difficult, and it causes more pain than when both are broken together.
Se c’est li petis foscile qui est brisiez soulement, si le covient poc estendre legierement, et mettre igal.	If only the small bone is broken, it should be gently extended and set straight.
Et se c’est li grans foscile, si le covient estraindre plus fort;	And if it's the large dislocation, then it must be pulled out more strongly;
et l’estende sus I cussin, et teigne le pouchet de la main plus haut des autres, et li petis dois plus bas des autres dois, et soit li malaides croisiez sus lui meisme, et I cussin devant lui plus haut, que li malaides ne soffre nule labor;	And stretch it out on the cushion; raise your hand pouch higher than the others and lower the little toe; let the patient lie across themselves with the cushion in front of them raised up so they don't suffer any discomfort;
puis estende li ministres som bras a la partie desoz a sa main, ou a I liien, et uns autres ministres a I autre au desus.	Then extend the minister's arm beneath the patient's hand or elbow, and another minister at the other side above.
Et puis le mette li mires igal, selonc sa millor forme.	Then the surgeon should set it straight according to its best form.
Et se en la brisure a pieces, si met chescune en son leu, et s’il en i a nule desevree ke poigne lou keur, et tu ne la pues restorer en son leu, si fent sus et l’oste, si com nos avons dit devant.	And if there are any fragments in the break, then put each one back into its proper place; and if there is any excess that cannot be grasped with your fingers, then press upon it lightly as we have said earlier.
Et se avec la briseure a plaie, je en ai parleit au chapistre singuler;	And if it is with breaking open a wound, I have spoken of this in a separate chapter;
si pren la cure.	So take the treatment.
Et se en l’encomencement dou restorement sorvient apostemes chaus, si glue I drapeil de cerote fait d’oile roset et de cire blainche, que ne soit mie ne trop durs ne trop molz;	And if in the beginning of healing, large abscesses appear, then apply a cloth made from rose oil and white wax that is not too hard nor too soft.
et lie I drapeil par sus subtilment, tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez.	and tie the cloth on gently until the large abscess is soothed.
Et puis oste lou cerote, et i met l’emplaustre de la poudre dou molin avec abun d’uef, pues met les esteles, et soit li estele de la briseure adés plus fors, et un poc plus large que les autres;	Then remove the wax and apply a poultice made from mill flour powder with abundant egg whites; then place bandages on it, making sure that the bandage for breaking open is stronger and somewhat wider than the others;
et saiches que il doit avoir VI esteles ou bras em plusors dispositions:	And know that he must have six lines drawn on the arm in various positions:
soit que li briseure soit en l’un des os, soit en II;	Whether the break is in one bone or two;
et estraint plus sus la briseure que autre part, et toz jors moins en aloignant, si com j’ai dit au comencement dou chapistre;	And tighten more above the fracture than elsewhere, and always lessen while setting it apart, as I said at the beginning of the chapter;
et soient li drapelz que sont sus la briseure molz et moistes, et ne soient mie dur ne aspres;	And let the bandages that are on the fracture be soft and moist, not hard or harsh.
et soit li filz, dont il est estrains, de lin, ne trop gros ne trop menus, si com nos avons dit.	And let the thread used for binding be of linen, neither too thick nor too thin, as we have said.
Et rewarde lou membre et lou liien aprés aucuns jors.	And reward the limb and the bandage after some days.
Et se aucuns mavais accidens vient au membre, si com prurite ki vient au membre, si covient que tu aroses lou membre d’aigue chaude, tant que cil prurites soit apaisiez;	And if any bad accident occurs to the limb, such as itching that comes upon the limb, then you must rinse the limb with warm water until that itch is appeased;
et laisse le membre ne mie estroit reposer.	and let the limb rest without being too tight.
Et puis rencomence l’estrignement, et se li liiens est amolis et li os desevrez, et semblant chose, si l’adresce.	And then commence the stretching, and if the ligaments are softened and the bone dislocated, and suchlike things, so treat it.
Et se pren warde se li norrissemens ne puet venir au membre, por ceu qu’il est trop estrois, si covient que tu l’amollisses .i. poc, et laisse ensi aucuns jors, tant que li norrissemens i corre, et puis l’estraint.	And beware that the nourishment cannot reach the limb because it is too tight; if so, then loosen it slightly and leave it thus for a few days until the nourishment arrives, then tighten again.
Et se nules de ces choses que nos avons dit ne vient au malaide, si ne lou desliier jusc’a XX jors.	And if none of these things that we have said come to the patient, then do not release it until 20 days have passed.
ou enqui entor, puis li pent les mains a son col, et soit ses cols igalz, et se warde de movement et de degitement, et dorme sus son dos;	Or if around it swells up later, then he places his hands on his neck and keeps them even; he guards against movement and dislocation, and sleeps on his back;
et saiches que ceste briseure est restoree en XXX jors ou en XXXV, et par aventure en XX jors, selonc les compositions et les complexions des vertus.	Know that this dislocation is restored in thirty days or thirty-five, and sometimes in twenty, according to the mixtures and temperaments of the humors.
de la brisure de la main	Of the breaking of the hand
Saiches que au dos de la main et as nous des dois avient poc de briseures, et n’i vient mais que ploieure maintes fois.	This is because on the back of the hand and in both hands there are few breaks, but rather many dislocations.
Et quant li plante de la main est brisie ou ploie, si covient que li malaides siece croisiet, et siet droitement devant lui igalement;	And when the fingers of the hand are broken or bent, then the patient should sit crossed-legged, sitting upright and straight before him.
puis met sa main sus la toie estendue, et estende li ministres les os brisiez, et les mete igalz li mires, tant qu’il soient bien joint;	Then place his hand on an extended cloth, and the ministers extend the broken bones, aligning them properly until they are well joined;
et met l’emplastre et les estoupes, se apostemes n’i vient, puis i met une estele selonc la quantiteit dou leu;	And apply the emplaster and bandages, if there is no inflammation; then place a splint according to the size of the affected area;
et soit envoloupee en I drapeil de lin.	and wrap it in one linen cloth.
Et se li briseure est au pardedens entor lou ventre de la plante, si fai une spere de drapelz, et comande au malaide qu’il l’estrigne a sa plante brisie;	And if the dislocation is around the wrist, make a splint of cloth and instruct the patient to bind it tightly to their broken wrist;
et puis l’estrain d’un lonc drapeil, et soit li estele de keur souef ausi grans com li plante de la main, et l’estraint, si com il covient.	then wrap it with a long cloth strip, and let the splint be of soft wood about as large as the palm of the hand, binding it securely.
Et se li brisure est au defuer, si covient que tu mettes une estele sus, et une autre desoz en la plante, si que li mains soit overte et droite, puis le lie tot entor la main, et estanche lou liien entre les dois.	And if the fracture is on the outside edge, then it is necessary to place a splint above and another below in the palm so that the hand is open and straight, then wrap it all around the hand, and secure the tie between the two sides.
Et se li briseure vient a aucun des nous des dois, se c’est li pouchés, si le met igal, si com il covient;	And if the fracture comes to any of us on the hip, if it is dislocated, then set it even, as it ought.
et l’estraint avec la plante, et se tu vues si met une estele droite petite por lever la briseure, et ne se mueve;	And hold it with the sole of your foot, and if you see fit, place a small upright splint to raise the fracture, and do not move it.
et se li brisure est as autres dois, si com en l’indice ou l’un des autres, si le met igal, et lou lie avec lou doi sain qui est aprés;	And if the fracture is in another toe, such as the big toe or one of the others, then set it even and bind it with the sound toe that comes after.
ou tu les lie toz en I tenant, que mues vaut, ou tu met sus une estele, si com ou pouchet;	Or you can tie them all together, whichever seems best, or place an upright splint on it, as for a dislocation of the hip.
et pren warde en la restauration et en la disposition d’aposteme chaut, et secor ceu qui i vient, si com j’ai dit.	And beware in the restoration and arrangement of hot abscesses, and treat those who come there, as I have said.
de la cuixe brisie	Here is the text for "de la cuixe brisie" (for a fractured thighbone):
Li os de la cuixe est maintes fois brisiez, et bien le voit on quant elle torne devant et derrier;	The thighbone is often broken, which can be clearly seen when it turns forward or backward.
et li restauration si est c’on lie I liien desus la briseure, et I autre desoz.	And the restoration is done by tying something above and below the fracture.
Et li malaides gise sus sa faice, puis estende chescuns ministres son lien a sa part igalment;	And the patient lies on his face, then each attendant stretches out their bandage evenly on their side.
et c’est quant li brisure est emmi l’os.	And this is when the fracture is within the bone.
Et se li brisure est prochiene a la racine de la cuixe, si soit li uns des liiens devers lou poignil, et li autres liiens desoz la briseure.	And if the dislocation is close to the root of the thigh, then let one ligament be towards the point and the other ligament below the dislocation.
Et ausi s’elle est prochiene au genoil, et adonques soit li liens delez lou genoil, et soit li extension aval;	And also if it is close to the knee, then let the bandage be near the knee, and extend it downward;
puis mette li mires l’os igal a ses II mains, tant qu’il soit selonc sa figure natureil, et puis met l’emplaustre, et lou lie, se apostemes chaz n’i vient.	Then let the physician align the bone with both hands until it is in its natural position, and then apply the splint, and if an abscess does not form there.
Et s’il i a aposteme chaut, si le laisse apaisier puis revien a ton ovraige et a ta cure;	And if there is a hot abscess, let it cool first, then return to your work and treatment;
li lieure est faite en teil maniere.	The bandage is made in this manner.
Il covient que tu envoloupes sus la briseure I bendeil dur doublé en II ou III, et en demoure li superfluitez, puis torne la jambe tant que li talons veigne a la racine de la naige, et boute I fil lonc entre la cuixe et la jambe, delez lou genoil desoz, et veignent li chief dou fil au desus;	You must wrap the fracture with one or two hard bandages doubled, and remove any excess material. Then twist the leg so that the heel comes to the root of the thigh. Insert a long thread between the hip and the leg below the knee, bringing the ends of the thread upwards;
puis torne sus la jambe et sus la cuixe le bendeil, puis met sus la briseure esteles, et met une estele sus l’os de la jambe;	then wrap the leg and hip with the bandage again, place supports on both sides of the fracture, and put one support on the bone of the leg;
puis emple le leu vuit entre la jambe et la cuixe de drapelz souef por mettre igal l’estrignement, puis comence a liier forment III tors ou IIII sus la briseure;	Then fill the empty space between the leg and thigh with soft cloth to make the tension even; then begin binding tightly three or four turns above the break.
et quant plus vas en sus de la briseure, et moins l’estraint;	And as you go higher up from the break, decrease the tension gradually.
puis enten as II chiés dou fil que tu as bouteit entre la jambe et la cuixe, et en lie III esteles que sont desus, puis revai au desoz au chief dou fil, tant que tu veignes delez le piet;	Then take both ends of the thread you have placed between the leg and thigh, and tie three knots that are above; then return below to the top of the thread until you reach the foot.
et l’estraint, si qu’il ne se mueve de son leu, puis le laisse ensi, puis k’il n’i vient ne aposteme ne enfleure n’autre semblant.	And tighten it so that it does not move from its place; then leave it thus until there is no inflammation or swelling or other similar condition.
Et s’il i avient, si le deslie, et adresce ceu que i vient, si com nos avons dit maintes fois;	And if any of these occurs, untie it and address what has come as we have said many times before.
et se il i a pieces de l’os que poigne, si le covient ewer, s’om puet;	And if there are pieces of bone that prick out, they must be removed if possible.
et s’on ne puet, si covient fendre le leu, et traire fuer;	And if it is not possible, then the place should be split open and infection pulled out
et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant k’il soit sanez.	And the treatment, as we have said, until he is healed.
Et aucune fois est brisie li cuixe ensi c’on i met esteles, si com en l’ajutoire et ou bras;	And sometimes the hip is broken in this way when one places splints on it, such as in the shoulder or arm;
toutevoie, en la restauration ensi faite ne cloche mie li malaides.	However, the patient does not limp after restoration done in this manner.
Et saiches que li cuixe est restoree en .l. jors, ou poc moins ou poc plus, selonc les diversitez des complexions.	And know that the thighbone takes about one month to heal, give or take a few days depending on individual constitutions.
de la ruelle dou genoil	Regarding the kneecap
Saiches que en la ruelle dou genoil avient poc brisure, mais elle ploie maintes fois.	You know that in the cruciate ligament of the knee there is rarely a break, but it often stretches.
Et s’elle brise, si n’est mais c’une fendure, ou I pertus, et avient a tout plaie, et sens plaie, et ce sent om bien.	And if it breaks, it is only a fissure or hole, and this happens in all wounds, and even without wounds, which everyone knows.
Et li restauration si est c’on mette igal ceu qui est rons a ses dois, tant qu’il soit assemblez mues c’on puet;	And the restoration is when one places what is round on both sides, until it moves together as much as possible;
puis met l’emplaustre, et i met une estele reonde, se tu en as mestier, et l’estraint si com il covient, puis rewarde toutes les dispositions que nos avons dit ens autres briseures, si com aposteme chaut et autre semblant;	then place the splint, and if necessary, place a round bandage on it and tighten it as needed, then review all the arrangements we have said for other fractures, such as treating heat and similar injuries;
si met a chescun accident ceu k’il li covient, tant qu’il soit sanez.	then apply to each injury what is necessary until he is healed.
de la brisure de la jambe	Regarding bone fractures of the leg
Saiches que en la jambe ait II os, de coi li uns est apelez par droit non «mustelz», et li autres est apelez «foscile»;	Know that in the leg there are two bones, one of which is rightly called 'mustelz', and the other 'foscile';
et avient tout auteil briseure com il vient au bras, et por ceu est li restauracion si com celle dou bras igalment, et li ovraiges est tout i. Et se li dui os sont brisiet ensamble, si torne li jambe de toutes pars.	And all other fractures happen similarly to those in the arm, and therefore restoration is done similarly to that of the arm, and the work is all one. And if both bones are broken together, then the leg turns all around.
Et se li os subtilz est brisiez, si torne devant.	And if the delicate bone is broken, so turn [it] forward.
Et se li gros os est brisiez, si sent on grant dolor, et le voit on bien;	And if the large bone is broken, great pain is felt, and it is clearly seen.
et torne desoz.	And twisted underneath.
Adonques amenistre extension, et le met igal, et lie les esteles igalement;	Then apply traction, align it evenly, and bind the splints evenly.
mais toutevoie, il covient se li brisure est laide, et il i a plusors pieces, que li extension soit menor et plus legiere;	But nonetheless, if the break is ugly with many fragments, then traction should be lighter and gentler.
et l’alige selonc ta vertu.	And align it according to your ability.
Et quant tu as tout acomplit ton ovraige, si pren II faixes de fust chevees que porpreignent la jambe d’une part et d’autre, et soient dou lonc de la jambe des le genoil jusque desoz;	When you have completed your work, then take two smooth bands of wood that encircle the leg on both sides and are as long as the leg from below the knee down.
puis envoloupe en II leus I bendeil desus et desoz, et le lie em mileu ausi, et a ceste lieure ne pora li jambe decliner a destre ne a senestre, et ensi est bien;	Then wrap one bandage above and another below, tie them in the middle, so that the leg cannot bend to the right or left at this joint, which is good.
et aucun i aministrent I bers dou lonc de la jambe, et s’est de fust, et i met on la jambe por warder de movement, et proprement fait on ceu en la brisure ou il a plaie;	And some apply splints the length of the leg made of wood, and place the leg to prevent movement, particularly if there is a wound at the break.
et remue chescun jor la jambe, por veoir s’il i a aposteme chaut n’autre accident;	And move each day the leg to see if there is any heat or other accident.
si le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	If the treatment continues until he is healthy.
de la brisure des os dou piet	About the fracture of bones in the foot
A la cheville ne vient point de brisure, mais as os dou piet vient aucune fois brisure et as dois poc, et n’i avient fuer que quassure em plusor dispositions.	In the ankle there is no fracture, but sometimes a bone in the foot is broken and in two pieces, and there occurs only quassure in various positions.
Et s’il avient as os dou piet brisure, et tu vois ces os sormonter l’un l’autre, si mette si malaides som piet sus la terre, ausi com s’il voloit aler, et puis met maintenant ton piet sus lou sien, lai ou li os sont levez, puis le presse tant k’il reveignent en lor leus;	And if it happens that the bones of the foot are broken and you see these bones rising above each other, then place this patient's foot on the ground as if he wants to walk, and then put your foot on his where the bones are raised, and press down until they return to their places;
puis met l’emplaustre et estoupes sus, et met desoz lou ventre dou piet une petite tauble a II chiés plains, puis l’estraint au piet avenanment, puis que tu as envoloupez drapelz entor, et autres choses dont tu as mestier.	then place the splint and bandages on it, and put under the foot of the patient a small board with two legs, then bind the foot firmly, and wrap cloths around it, and other things that you may need.
Et quant .iij. jors ou .iiij. seront passez, si deslie lou liien, car tu troveras les os igalz, soient brisiez, soient desaluez.	And when three or four days have passed, then untie the bandage, for you will find the bones even, whether they are broken or dislocated.
Et s’il i a aucuns des dois brisiez, si les restoure, si com nos avons dit as dois de la main;	And if there are any bones of the hand broken, restore them, just as we have said for the bones of the hand;
puis met au doi brisiet une estele selonc la longesce dou doi, et soit un poc plus large, puis met desoz le piet celle tauble que j’ai dit, et l’estrain avenanment;	then place on the broken bone a splint according to the length of the bone, and a bit wider, then put under the foot that board which I mentioned earlier, and bind it firmly;
et s’il en i a II ou III, ou plus, brisiez, si met sus chescun doi une estele selonc sa quantiteit, envoloupee en I drapeil de lin, et estraint la tauble desoz lou piet;	And if there are two or three, or more [hairs] that need breaking, then place an adhesive bandage on each one according to its amount, wrapped in a piece of linen cloth, and secure the wound with a pad beneath the foot.
et soit estans sus lou chief de la tauble defuer lou ventre dou piet, si qu’il le teigne bien.	And let it be placed on top of the wound's head, away from the belly of the foot, so that it may adhere well.
Et covient que tu n’oblier mie les autres choses que j’ai dit as autres briseures, des que nos avons dit;	And remember not to forget the other things I have mentioned regarding other fractures.
et secor chescun accident si com il covient.	and treat each injury as it deserves.
de la brisure de l’os dou poignil	About the fracture of the bone of the thumb
Quant li os de la nature la femme est brisiez, si la fai seoir enlargie, puis l’encline a la partie dou dos, et soit tenue par derrier;	When a woman's hipbone is broken, have her sit down and lean towards the back part, being held there from behind.
puis emplisse li baile la nature de la malaide de couton, et en i mette ausi gros com I sto;	Then fill the woman's hip joint with cotton, adding as much as one stone's weight,
puis deboute la femme, et lieve lou dos poc et poc, et adonques saut li coton, tant qu’il vient a l’entree de la nature, et revient li os avec lou sto;	Then lower the woman and raise her back little by little until the cotton begins to rise towards the hip joint, causing the bone to return with the weight of one stone.
et quant elle vuet pissier, si oste lou coton, et quant elle a pissiet, se li remette, et ensi faice VII jors ou entor:	And when she wishes to urinate, remove the cotton, and when she has urinated, replace it, and do so for about seven days.
si sera restoree li brisure, et se tu vues, pren une vessie de berbis, et lie au pertus une cainne, et boute toute la vessie en la nature;	Then the fracture will be restored, and if you see that it is so, take a bladder of a sheep, tie a tube to its opening, and pour the entire contents into the wound.
puis soffle en la cainne forment, tant que li vessie soit enflee dedens:	Then blow forcefully into the tube until the bladder is fully inflated inside.
la nature si revenra li brisure;	The wound will then heal.
puis soit emplie de coton, et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then fill it with cotton, and leave it thus for several days until it is healed.
Et quant li os dou poignil de l’ome est brisiez, ou de la femme, si le restoure ensi com nos avons dit en l’os de la hainche;	And when the bone of the hand of a man or woman is broken, restore it as we have said for the thighbone.
et ne sont mie occultees ces briseures prochienes a celui qui i met son estude et son us, et entent mon livre.	But these nearby fractures are not hidden from those who study and practice this art, and may my book be understood.
Car li brisure li signifie em plusors dispositions la droite voie de la restauration:	For a fracture indicates many ways to correctly reset it:
enten le donques.	So listen to them now.
En la verge, quant elle est brisie, pren une gorge d’oie et i boute la verge;	In the thighbone, when it is broken, take a goose's feather and insert it into the bone.
puis envoloupe drapelz entor, et le laisse III jors ou enqui entor, et il sera sanez hastanment.	Then wrap bandages around it, and let it rest for three days or more, and it will heal quickly.
de brisure avec plaie	About fracture with wound
Il covient a celui qui a brisure avec plaie, meismement s’elle est grans, si com li os de la cuixe ou de l’ajutoire ou semblant, qu’il soit sainiez maintenant, si que les sainies que nos avons dit le tesmoignent.	He who has a fracture with a wound, even if it is large, such as the bone of the thigh or the arm or similar, must be healed now, so that the healing that we have mentioned proves it.
Et se li plaie saine, si la restainche de vitriole, se tu n’as autre chose, puis rencomence a restorer la briseure en cele meisme houre, ou celui jor, se apostemes chaus n’i vient.	And if the wound heals, then rinse it with vitriol, if you don't have anything else, then begin to restore the fracture in that same hour or day, if no inflammation occurs.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si laisse la restauration jusc’a nuevime jor, tant que li apostemes soit apaisiez, et n’i touchier ne au tier jor ne au quart, car tu i feroies venir malvais accident.	And if inflammation occurs, then leave the restoration until the ninth day, until the inflammation is appeased, and do not touch it on the third or fourth day, for you would bring bad accidents upon it.
Et se li os brisiez est aparans sus lou keur descovert, si covient que tu lou mettes a point legierement a tes mains, a extension petite.	And if the broken bone is appearing above the exposed heart, then it must be put in place lightly with your hands, with slight traction.
Et se li extensions ne t’est apareillie por mettre igal a tes mains, si le ramoine a cest estrument qui est de fer, qui a VII dois ou VIII de lonc, et li largesce est selonc la quantiteit de la plaie;	And if the extension is not suitable for placing evenly in your hands, then straighten it with this iron tool that is seven or eight fingers long, and its width should match the size of the wound.
et por ceu est mestier au mire qu’il empreigne III ou IIII, selonc ceu qu’il en ait mestier en chescune cure de briseure;	And so it is necessary for the physician to have three or four of them ready, depending on what he needs in each case of fracture treatment.
et soit rons et un poc gros, k’il ne ploie mie a la compression sus lou membre a ton ovraige, et soit agus devant, et gros des le mileu en avant, ensi:	And it should be round and slightly thick so that it does not bend under pressure during your procedure, and it should be pointed at the front and thickest in the middle, like this:
Et est apelez «palainche», por coi il covient que li chiés corbes soit mis sus lou chief de l’os apparent;	And it is called "palainche," for which reason the curved head of the bone must be placed on the visible end of the bone.
et le boute a une fois, tant k’il reviegne, et soit igalz l’un encontre l’autre.	And push it in once, until it returns, and let them lie evenly opposite each other.
Et se li brisure est subtilz, et li estrumens ne puet bien prendre l’os, si covient que tu copes lou chief de l’os, tant que li estrumens en ait possance.	And if the fracture is slight and tools cannot grasp the bone well, then you must cut off the head of the bone until tools can seize it.
Et se tu ne pues ramener l’os, si com nos avons dit, si lou cope d’un estrument covenable a ceu, ou incisoire ou soieure, a ton pooir;	And if you cannot reset the bone as we have said, then cut with an appropriate tool, such as a scalpel or knife, to your ability;
puis reis ceu qui est demorez en l’os d’aspreteit et de menues escorces.	Then remove that which remains on the bone roughly and in small shavings.
Et quant li os est ramenez, et li malaides sent grant dolor aprés, saiches qu’il n’est mie en son leu natureil.	And when the bone is reset but the patient feels great pain afterwards, know that it is not in its natural place.
Si fai tant qu’il soit en son leu, puis moille I drapeil en vin stiptique noir, et proprement se c’est en esteit;	Once it is back in its place, then wet a cloth with black staunching wine and cleanse it properly if it is inflamed;
et ne mettre mie sus la plaie cerote ne autre chose ou il ait oile, qu’il n’i faice venir porriture et corruption;	and do not apply any ointment or other substance containing oil to the wound, lest putrefaction and corruption arise therein.
puis aministre esteles quant tu as restoreit l’os, et laisse la plaie descoverte, et cope la coverture tout entor, selonc la quantiteit de la plaie, et te done bien en garde que li plaie ne soit estrainte avec la brisure;	Then apply dressings once the bone has been reset, leave the wound uncovered, and cut away the surrounding skin according to the size of the wound, taking care that the wound is not constricted by the dressing.
et maintes fois ont ce fait li fol mire, et ont fait venir sus le malaide ou mort ou corrodent aucune fois;	And many foolish physicians have done this and thereby brought death or corruption upon their patients.
et soit li estrignemens plus molz et plus souef des autres brisures.	And let the bandaging be softer and more gentle than other dressings.
Et se li plaie est male ou grans, et tu doutes que mavais accidens n’i veigne, si com nos avons dit, et tu trueves dolor au leu, si n’i covient mie mettre sus esteles;	And if the wound is bad or large, and you doubt that some misfortune will come of it, as we have said, and you find pain at its location, then do not put on bandages.
mais envoloupe entor, en leu d’esteles, drapelz durs, et les lie.	But wrap it around instead, with hard cloths, and tie them securely.
Et quant tu vois aprés I jor ou II enjanrer bowe a la plaie, si oste ceu que tu as mis sus a tout vin, et i met oignement sanant plaies, si com oignement tetrafarmaçon et semblans.	And when you see after one or two days an opening of the wound, then remove what you had put on it previously, and apply healing salve to it, such as tetrapharmaceutical salve and similar ones.
Et covient que tu deslies lou membre .ij. fois le jor, lou matin et au vespre, tant qu’il soit soudez et sanez.	You must wash the limb twice a day, in the morning and evening, until it is solid and healed.
Et covient que li membres soit aparilliez en teil maniere que li bowe corre aval legierement.	The limb should be placed in such a way that the wound drains easily.
Et se maint jor trespassent, et il ne puet souder mais rent adés bowe, saiches k’il i a petites pieces d’os, por coi il covient que tu quieres la plaie avec tente, et oste toutes ces pieces desevrees que font venir celle dolor.	And if many days pass and the wound does not heal but continues to suppurate, know that there are small bone fragments present, for which reason you should cleanse the wound with tincture and remove all these unwanted fragments that cause pain.
Et se fistule vient au leu, ou autre maniere de corruption, si covient que tu le cures, selonc ceu qu’il dist en son chapistre ci devant.	And if a fistula appears at the location, or another manner of corruption, then it is necessary that you treat it according to what is said in its chapter above.
Et quant li os est brisiez, et apert sus lou membre, si com li os de la cuixe ou de l’ajutoire, et autres semblans des grans membres, si ne le traire mie, car maintes fois en vient li mors, mais le laisse tant qu’il porrisse;	And when the bone is broken and exposed on the limb, such as the thighbone or shoulder blade, and other similar large limbs, do not pull it out, for many times death ensues, but let it be until it rots.
par aventure cherra par lui aprés XX jors ou XXX, puis cure la plaie, se tu pues;	Perhaps it will fall off by itself after 20 or 30 days, then treat the wound if you can.
et se tu ne pues, si la laisse.	And if you cannot, then leave it alone.
des brus qui vienent sor la sodure	about the burns that come on top of the scab
Nous vienent maintes fois aprés la santeit de la briseure, meismement quant c’est pres de la jointure, et laide chose est a veoir li figure dou membre;	Many times afterwards the health of the broken part is questioned, especially when it is near the joint, and it is unpleasant to see the deformity of the limb.
et par aventure ne puet faire li membres ses ovraiges naturelz.	And perhaps the limb cannot perform its natural tasks.
Pren warde donques se li nous est fres:	Take care then if the bone is fresh:
si li aministre medicines stiptiques, si com aloes, encens, et mirre, et sarcocolle, acaice, et semblans autres, ensi que tu preignes aucune de ces choses, ou toutes ensamble, et les confit avec vin stiptique ou avec abun d’uef ou avec aisil;	If the administrator applies medicines that are astringent, such as aloes, incense, and myrrh, and sarcocolle, acacia, and similar others, thus you should take any of these things, or all together, and mix them with an astringent wine or with egg white or with egg yolk;
et les met sus le nout en estoupes, et l’estraint bien, et ne la desliier en mains jors;	and apply it to the wound in bandages, pressing it down tightly, and do not remove it for many days;
et puis la desloie, et rencomence une autre, tant que li nodations soit ostee;	then remove it, and start again with another one until the dislocation has been reduced;
ou tu estrain sus une piece de plonc bien faite;	or you can press on a well-made splint;
car li proprietez dou plonc si est qu’il oste toutes les enfleures desus les membres;	for the property of wood is such that it draws out all the swellings from the limbs;
et se li nodation est ja convertie en durteit ausi com piere, et il est besoing de l’oster, si la cope desus, et fent la superfluiteit apparent;	and if the dislocation has already become hard like stone, and it is necessary to remove it, cut on top of it, and remove the excess;
ou tu la reis a aucun raseur, tant qu’ele soit ostee, et la cure tant qu’ele soit sanee.	or you can scrape it away with any sharp instrument until it is removed, and then treat it until it has healed.
dou membre qui est foibles aprés la garison	about the limb that is weak after healing
Quant li brisure de l’os est restoree, et demoure aprés li membres foibles et subtilz, si avient por mout de causes:	When bone fracture is restored, but afterwards the limb remains weak and slender, this occurs for many reasons:
de coi l’une est por ceu qu’il fut liiez trop estroit, et ne fut mie liiez si com il covenoit;	One reason is that it was bound too tightly, and was not bound as it should have been;
ou por ceu qu’il i ot trop de liiens, et ne pooit venir li norrissemens au membre;	Or because there were too many bindings, and the limb could not receive nourishment;
ou por multitude d’arosement;	Or due to excessive bandaging;
ou por trop grans movements, ne mie en son houre;	Or because of excessive movements, not at the right time.
ou por ceu qu’il a poc de sanc en son cors, si est foibles.	Or because it lacks blood in its body, so it is weak.
Et li cure si est que tu faices mengier le malaide, et faire le cors tendre, tant que li sans soit multipliiez en lui;	And the treatment for this is to feed the patient and make their body supple until their blood becomes abundant within them;
et li aministre bain, et li done joie et liesce;	and apply fomentations, give them joy and ease.
puis met poix sus le membre, si que li poix atraie a li grant norrissement, et l’arose sovent d’aigue tede, tant que li norrissement corre au membre;	Then place pitch on the limb so that the pitch attracts great nourishment to it, and apply warm water bandages often until the nourishment reaches the limb;
et reviegne a sa figure natureil.	and return it to its natural shape.
dou membre tort aprés la santeit	The limb twisted after recovery
Quant li membres est tors aprés la restauration, et li os brisiez apert, et li forme dou membre est laide, toutevoie ne pert mie son ovraige natureil:	When the limb is twisted after restoration, and the broken bone opens up, and the form of the limb is ugly, nevertheless it does not lose its natural function:
si ne croire mie les folz qui dient c’on doit brisier lou membre tout de noveil, et maint fol mire ont ce fait en nostre terre;	If you do not believe the foolish ones who say one must break the limb anew, and many foolish physicians have done this in our land
et cist ovraiges est blamez, et en vient grans malz, et par aventure li mors;	and these deeds are blameworthy, causing great harm, and sometimes death
toutevoie, se li nodations et li torture sont fres, si covient k’il soient arosez d’aigue chaude, ou herbes mollifians soient cuites, si com foilles de vismalve, et racines, et mellilote, et semblans choses;	Nevertheless, if the dislocations and contusions are fresh, they should be rinsed with hot water, or softening herbs should be cooked on them, such as vinca leaves, roots, and mallow
et li fai I emplaustre mollificatif, si com dyaquilon bien fait, et tu pren le muscillaige de vismalve, et la confit avec graisse de geline ou oile de sisament, et fai emplaustre sus;	And apply a softening poultice, such as well-made diacelion, and take the mollificating ointment of vinca, and mix it with goose grease or sesame oil, and apply the poultice on
ou tu pren figues graisses, et les broie avec fien de colon, et semblans medicines que amenuisent le soudement.	Or you take fat figs, crush them with fennel seeds, and similar remedies that soften bone setting.
Et aucune fois est ostee li nodacion por froter continuelment et longement a mains moistes.	And sometimes dislocation occurs due to continuous and prolonged rubbing with moist hands.
Et soit amenistrez movement au membre chescune houre.	And move the limb each hour.
Et se li tortuositez est enveillie et endurcie, ausi com piere, et besoins est de l’oster au fer, si la covient coper jusc’a l’os, a l’incisoire subtil legierement;	And if the distortions are old and hardened like stone, it is necessary to remove them with an iron instrument; they should be cut down to the bone with a fine, light scalpel
et mettre cusenson et estude en la cure.	And apply bandages and care to the treatment.
Ci encomence li livres des dislocations	Here begins the book of dislocations
Dislocations est issue d’aucune jointe de son leu, por coi il ne se puet muevre, et est li membres mal figurez, et sent li malaides grant dolor et grant lesion.	Dislocations are when a joint leaves its place, so that it cannot move, and the limb is misshapen, and the sufferer feels great pain and great injury.
Quant dislocation vient a aucun, si le covient maintenant ramener sens targier.	When dislocation comes to anyone, they should try to reduce it immediately.
Car s’on tarde, si enfle li leus, et par aventure si le remet on a poines au leu;	If one delays, the area swells, and if it is barely reset.
por ceu ne covient mie c’on le mueve a l’oure k’il est enflez:	Therefore, one should not move it until the swelling has subsided:
maintes fois fait venir spame et autres dolors;	Often brings about spasms and other pains;
toutevoie, quant ce avenra, si fai sainier lou malaide, puis le laisse, tant que li apostemes chas soit apaisiez;	However, when this happens, make the patient sweat, then leave him until the inflammation is reduced.
puis arose le membre d’aigue chaude et d’oile, puis le ramoinne legierement, et cure chescun membre si com li cure venra en son leu.	Then raise the limb with warm water and oil, then gently reset it, and treat each joint as they come into their proper place.
Et j’ai ordenez les chapistres des dislocations des lou chief jusc’a piez.	And I have ordered the chapters of the dislocations from head to foot.
des mandibules	of the jaws
Poc avient que les mandibules soient desaluees andous, et li dislocations d’ambedous est selonc II manieres:	It happens sometimes that the jaws are dislocated outward, and the dislocation of both is in two ways:
ou elles sont un poc ostees de lor leus, et mollifies un poc;	Either they are a little bony out of their place, or softened a little;
ou elles sont desaluees entierement, et pendent vers lou pis, et cort li salive de la bouche qu’il ne la puet tenir, ne ne puet clore sa bouche, et envoloupe sa langue avec la parole.	Or they are completely dislocated and hang down towards the chest, causing saliva to flow from the mouth so that he cannot hold it in nor close his mouth, and it envelops his tongue with speech.
Quant li dislocations est petite, si revient par li em plusors disposicions.	When dislocation is slight, it returns spontaneously in most cases.
Et s’elle est entiere et acomplie, si covient que tu la ramoinne hastanment, et ne targier mie;	And if it is whole and complete, then you must reset it quickly, and do not delay.
et en tel maniere que li ministres teigne le chief dou malaide, et boute li mires som pochet de l’une de ses mains en la racine de la dislocation de la mandibule dedens la bouche, se li dislocations est de II pars;	And in such a manner that the assistants hold the patient's head still, and the physician places his little finger of one hand at the root of the jaw dislocation within the mouth, if the dislocation is on the right side;
et li autre doi des mains soient defuer, por mettre igal;	and the other two fingers of the hands be spread apart to place it evenly;
et comande au malaide qu’il les amollisse, ses mandibules, et les mueve de toutes pars.	and instruct the patient to soften his jaws and move them in all directions.
Et li mires la mete igal, tant qu’elle reveigne en son leu.	And the physician places it back until it returns to its proper place
Et se li ramener est griés, meismement se ce sont les II mandibules ensamble, si les arose d’aigue chaude et d’oile, tant que les ramoinnes legierement;	And if resetting is difficult, especially if both jaws are dislocated together, then apply warm water and oil, until they reset easily;
ne ne targier mie dou ramener, si com nos avons dit.	do not delay in resetting them, as we have said.
Et quant elles sont ramenees igalment, et li bouche dou malaide clot bien sens mollifiier, si met sus drapelz moilliez en cerote fait d’oile roset et de cire, puis le lie legierement de molz liiens;	And when they are reset evenly, and the patient can close his mouth without difficulty, then apply warm, moist cloths made of oil, rose wax, and honey, and lightly bind it with soft linens.
et dorme li malaides sus son dos, et ses chiés soit estans entre II cussins, si qu’il ne lou mueve ne a destre ne a senestre, ne ne s’efforce mie de maixier, mais preigne legiere viande, tant que les dolors soient ostees, et soient noees les mandibules;	And let the patient sleep on their back, with their shoulders between two pillows so that they do not move to the right or left, nor try to mix things up, but instead take light food until the pain has subsided and the jawbones are healed.
et puis menjuce ce qu’il vuet legierement, et ne se travaille mie d’ovrir la bouche au mengier et au boivre, tant que li mandibule soit bien noee et sanee.	And then let them chew what they want lightly, and do not strain to open their mouth for eating and drinking, until the jawbone is completely healed and sound.
Et se les .ij. mandibules ne pueent estre remises a point a une houre, et ne sont mie converties a lor leus, si en vient fievres et sode acostumees, et par aventure solution de ventre, et par aventure vomist cole pure.	And if both jaws cannot be put back in place within an hour and are not returned to their proper positions, then fever and chills may occur, sometimes with diarrhea and occasionally vomiting of clear bile
Et quant tu verras ceu, adonc saiches que c’est perdicions;	And when you see these signs, know that it is a loss.
et maintes fois muert cil cui il avient, en VIIII jors.	and many times the person for whom this happens dies within nine days.
de la forcelle	of dislocation
Li forcele ne puet desaluer dou costeit dedens la continuation de li et dou pis, et est desaluee aucune fois au defuer, et bien le sent on.	The dislocation cannot be dislocated from the inner side of the cheekbone nor from the breastbone; sometimes it is dislocated backward and can be felt quite well
Et li restauration si est que li malaides gise sovin sor son dos, et estende ses bras;	And the treatment is that the patient should lie often on their back and extend their arms;
et puis presse le leu forment a ta palme, et elle revenra;	and then press firmly with your hand's palm on it, and it will return.
puis met sus l’emplaustre et lou bendeil, et l’estraint;	then place the bandage and tie it tightly
et li chiez qui est devers lou coute ne puet desaluer;	and the shoulder that is towards the back cannot dislocate
se poc non, et se il desalue aucune fois, si le ramoinne a son leu, si com nos avons dit;	If not, and if it dislocates any time, then reset it to its place, as we have said.
puis met sus l’emplaustre et le bendeil, et l’estraint, et coumande au malaide qu’il se repose tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then place the splint and bandage, and secure it, commanding the patient to rest until they are healed.
et ensi meisme est ramenez li chiés de l’espale, quant il est desevrez de son leu.	And thus similarly is the head of the shoulder reset when it is dislocated from its place.
de la dislocation de l’espaule	Chapter on the dislocation of the shoulder
Saiches que li espaule n’est desaluee fuer que selonc III manieres:	Know that the shoulder can be dislocated in only three ways:
de coi l’une est qu’ele desalue a la partie de l’assele au desoz;	one of which is that it dislocates at the part of the socket below;
et li seconde est a la partie dou pis;	and the second is at the part towards the arm;
et par aventure desalue a la partie desus, et ceu avient poc;	and sometimes it dislocates above, which happens rarely.
et ne desalue mie derrier por l’espaule, et ne desalue mie dedens por les ners;	and the shoulder does not dislocate behind or inside for the nerves.
et plusors fois desalue desoz vers l’assele, meismement a ces qui ont poc de char, car a ces saut ele fuer hastanment;	And often it dislocates below towards the socket, especially in those who have little flesh, as it moves suddenly.
a ces qui ont assez char, saut ele a poines, et rentre a poines.	In those who have enough flesh, it moves barely and returns barely.
Et par aventure avient a aucuns homes percussion ou casseure, et enfle li espaule d’un aposteme chaut, et cuide qu’elle est desaluee par ceu.	And sometimes there occurs a blow or fall which causes the shoulder to swell with a hot hematoma and the person believes that it is dislocated because of this
Il covient donques que tu l’esprueves, tant que tu en soies certains;	You must therefore test it until you are certain of it
et adonques encomence la cure.	and then begin the treatment.
Et est conue li dislocations quant il est aval vers l’assele, et met difference entre l’espaule malade et la saine, et tu troveras entre lor diversiteit manifeste;	And dislocation is recognized when it is down towards the thighbone, and there is a difference between the affected shoulder and the healthy one, which you will find clearly different.
et troveras au chief de l’espaule une fosse, et desoz l’assele au tochier le chief de l’espaule, ausi com se ce soit uns oes;	and you will find a hollow at the top of the shoulder and below the thighbone you will touch the top of the shoulder as if it were an egg.
et ne puet li malaides ramener sa main a son neis, ne movoir de nulz movemens;	and the patient cannot bring their hand to their neck nor move in any way
et ausi, s’elle est desaluee en haut, si n’est mie occultee, car tu le trueves manifestement au tochier;	Also, if it is dislocated upwards, it is not hidden, for you will find it clearly upon touching.
et ceste maniere de dislocation n’est mie fors a ramener, quant elle est novele, ou se li enfes est malaides.	This type of dislocation cannot be reduced except when it is new or if the child is the patient
Et li maniere est que li ministres lieve la main dou malaide en haut, puis met tes peuchas desoz l’assele, et lieve la jointure a force en haut au leu;	And the method is for the practitioner to lift the patient's hand upwards, then place their fingers beneath the thighbone and forcefully raise the joint upwards into its proper place
et li ministres lieve la main, et l’estende en haut, pues le mette desoz;	The servant raises the hand, extends it upwards, then places it beneath
si venra hastanment.	so that it comes quickly.
Et s’elle ne vient si com nos avons dit em mains jors aprés, si covient ke li malaides soit baigniez en aigue chaude;	And if it does not come as we have said within a few days afterward, then the patient must be bathed in warm water;
et li amenistre arosement mollifiant et assouajant, si com decoction de altee et de fenugrec et de mellilote en aigue, et soit amenistree;	and let the servant apply gently softening and soothing ointment, such as a decoction of celery, fennel, and melilot in water, and it should be applied;
puis soit sovinez li malaides sus son dos, et mette on desoz l’assele un sto de lainne igal, ne trop mol ne trop dur, puis mette li mires son talon sus le sto, et lieve le chief de l’espaule vertuousement, et traie la main dou malaide;	then have the patient lie on their back, and place underneath the armpit a cloth of even thickness, not too soft nor too hard; then let the physician put their heel upon the cloth, lift the virtuous shoulder gently, and draw out the hand of the patient.
et uns autres ministres teigne lou chief dou malaide, si qu’il ne se mueve aval;	And another servant should hold the head of the patient so that it does not move downwards;
celle espaule revient tout maintenant, et se tu vues si le ramoinne selonc ceste maniere:	When that shoulder returns perfectly aligned, then reset it according to this method:
et est que tu faices estre present I home qui soit plus grans que li malaides;	and ensure that a man larger than the patient is present;
et soit drois devers lou costeit, et boute s’espaule desoz l’assele dou malaide, et lieve l’assele en haut, si que li malaides pende en l’ar;	And let it be right across from the ribcage, and place your shoulder beneath the patient's elbow, then lift the elbow upwards so that the patient hangs down.
et uns autres ministres traie la main dou malaide aval devers lou ventre.	Another minister pulls the patient's hand down towards their belly.
Et se li malaides est trop legiers, si pent avec lui aucune chose pesant, et li dislocation revient maintenant.	And if the patient is too light, hang something heavy with him, and the dislocation will return now.
Et le ramoinne on ausi en autre maniere:	And it is reset in another manner as well:
et est c’on fiche I lonc tison en terre, dont li chiés soit ausi reons com I pistal, et ne soit ne trop gros ne trop graile;	And this one involves sticking a long, dry stick into the ground, onto which the head should be placed level with the fist, neither too thick nor too thin;
puis soit mis desoz lou malaide, mais k’il ait drapelz souef sus, et li malaides soit estans dou lonc dou fust;	then place it under the patient, but gently so they do not feel any pressure, and let them stand on the long stick.
puis soit estendue sa main aval d’autre part forment, et li jointure revenra en son leu hastanment;	Then extend their arm downwards on the other side, and the dislocation will quickly return to its place.
et s’elle ne vuet revenir por toutes ces choses que nos avons dit, si fai ceste cure:	But if it still does not want to return after all these things we have said, then perform this treatment:
pren I tison de II bras de grant et IIII dois de large, qui ait le chief reont por mues entrer em parfont desoz l’assele, selonc ceste forme:	Take a stick two arms long and four fingers wide, with a rounded end for easy insertion deep under the elbow.
puis lie sus le chief dou fust drapelz souez, que li fust ne blece lou malaide, puis le met desoz l’assele dou malaide;	Then place upon the head of the patient a cloth moistened with water so that the wood does not burn the patient; then place it under the pillow of the patient.
et estende som bras sus le fust dou lonc, et lie l’ajutoire sus le fust, et lou bras au chief de la main, puis met le bras sus I eschillon d’une eschiele dou large, et soit estendue li mains aval, et soit laissiez li cors pendans d’autre part:	And stretch his arm along the wood's length, and tie the joint to the wood, and bind the arm at the hand's head; then place the arm on the edge of a wide beam, with the hand hanging down below, and let the body hang freely on the other side.
li jointure reva ens maintenant.	The joint is ready now.
Et quant elle est ens, en quel maniere que ce soit, si covient que tu mettes desoz l’assele une spere de laine igal, puis met l’emplaustre aparilliet de poudre dou molin, avec encens et aubun d’uef, sus toute l’espaule et entor, puis l’estrain desoz l’assele avenanment, et torne le liien sus l’emplaustre, et embraice la main a son col, et soit li mains demorans ensi.	And when it has returned into its proper place, however this may have happened, then you must place a bandage of wool beneath the socket, sprinkle the whole shoulder and surrounding area with powdered mallow leaves mixed with incense and egg-white, then draw the bandage tight beneath the arm and tie the ends securely around the emplastrum; fasten the hand to its collarbone and let it remain in this position
Et covient qu’il menjuce poc, tant que li membres soit confortez, car il sanera plus tost;	And it is necessary that he consume little food, so that the limb may be rested; for it will heal more quickly.
et puis menjuce plus aprés V jors ou VII, et le mueve;	Then eat again after five or seven days, and move around.
et s’il est fermeis et il n’est mollifiez, si est sanez.	And if it is firm but not softened, then it is healed.
Et se li jointure est fuer de leu por moistor que i est venue, ou por autre cause, si covient que tu i aministres cauteres a III pertus, si com il est mis devant ou chapistre des cauteres.	And if the joint is out of place due to moisture that has come there, or for another reason, you must administer cauteries through three holes, as it is shown before in the chapter on cauteries.
Et se tu fais tout ceu, et il deslie aprés VII jors, et li jointure ne se tient, et ne puet lever som bras amont, adonc saiches que li nerf au chief de l’espaule sont copeit ou estendut ou amollis;	And if you do all this, and after seven days it still does not stay in place and the arm cannot be raised above, then know that the nerve at the head of the shoulder is cut or stretched or softened.
et saiches que li jointure n’iert jamais fichie en son leu.	And know that the joint will never again be fixed in its place.
Li dislocation qui est devers lou pis, et les mameles, ou derrier, si est faite par impulsion, et estendement de mains, et i aministre on autre lieure;	The dislocation which is towards the hip, and breasts, or behind, if it occurs due to forceful movement of hands, and another ligature should be administered;
et cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And treat until it is healed.
Et se aprés la sanation vient grietez au membre, et tardemens em movement, si use li malaides bain maintes fois, tant que celle grietez soit alegie, et reviegne a sa premiere nature.	And if after the healing there is stiffness in the limb and difficulty in movement, then let the patient exercise many times until that stiffness is alleviated and returns to its original condition.
de la dislocation dou coute	of dislocation of the neck
Saiches que li jointure dou coute est desaluee a poinnes, et a poinnes revient;	Know that the shoulder joint is easily dislocated and can readily become dislocated again;
et s’est desaluee de toutes pars, et meismement devant et derrier, et li dislocations n’est mie reponue, car on la voit bien et sent bien;	And if it has been dislocated from all sides, especially front and back, the dislocation is not hidden because it can be seen clearly and felt easily;
et desalue selonc chescune figure.	And it becomes dislocated according to each position.
Et quant tu joins le coute malaide avec lou sain, si le pues veoir apertement.	And when you join the sick limb with the sound one, you can then see it clearly.
Car li jointure est chevee, et ne puet ploier lou bras, ne touchier son espaule a tout.	For the joint is dislocated and cannot bend the arm nor touch the shoulder at all
Et covient que tu le ramoinnes ainsois que apostemes chaus i viegne, car se apostemes chaus i venoit, si seroit grief li ramener;	Therefore you must reset it before an abscess forms there, for if an abscess had already formed, it would be difficult to reset.
et par aventure ne puet estre ramenez dou tout en tout, meismement quant ele est au derrier;	And sometimes it cannot be fully reset altogether, especially when it is behind;
si vaut pis que les autres dislocations, et est de plus grant dolor, et par aventure i vient li mors.	So it is worse than other dislocations and causes greater pain, and sometimes death occurs.
Et li restauration si est, quant elle est telz c’on la puet ramener, que tu li estendes sa main a tes II mains;	And restoration occurs when it is such that one can reset it, by extending his hand with both of yours.
et ses bras soit espandus, et les mains dou mire selonc le coute entor, desor et desoz, et boute la jointure a ses peuchas ensamble, ou a la racine de sa palme, tant qu’ele reviegne a son leu.	And let his arms be extended, and the hands of the doctor according to the count be placed around, above and below, and push the joint towards his fingers together, or at the root of his palm, until it returns to its place.
Et se li dislocations est au devant, si revient quant il double sa main a sa main, et fier de la racine de la palme lou coute qui est desaluez.	And if the dislocation is on the front, it can be reduced by doubling the hand onto itself and pressing the root of the palm against the dislocated neck.
Et s’il ne vuet revenir au leu, si aministre fort extension;	And if it does not want to return to its place, then apply strong traction;
et est que dui ministre estendent le bras, et le teignent dui ministre, si qu’il ne se mueve a l’estension;	and two ministers should extend the arm, and two other ministers should hold it so that it does not move during the extension;
puis torne le bras de chescune part, puis que tu as envoloupeit un drapeil double lonc et large;	then twist the arm in both directions, then wrap a long and wide folded cloth around it;
et quant li mires a jointe la jointure a sa main, si l’oigne d’aucun oile por amolir la jointure, puis boute la jointure forment, tant qu’ele reviegne;	and when the doctor has joined the joint with his hand, then anoint it with some oil to soften the joint, then push the joint strongly until it returns;
et quant elle est au leu, si met sus emplaustre sec avec aubun d’uef, et l’estrain forment, et pent le bras au col dou malaide, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le deslie.	and when it is in place, then put dry compresses with egg yolk on it, press it strongly, and wrap the arm around the patient's neck, leaving it for a few days before removing it.
Et se li jointure est ferme en son leu, si deslie lou liien, et le laisse;	And if the joint is firm in its place, then loosen it, and let it be.
et se tu vois que li jointure n’estrigne bien, si rencomence l’emplaustre et lou lien, et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, tant qu’il soit fermement mis;	And if you see that the joint is not properly aligned, then recommence the emplacement and loosen the ligature, and leave it thus for several days until it is firmly in place.
puis le deslie.	Then loosen it.
Et se il sent grieteit aprés le ramenement de la jointe, et elle se muet, si le baigne et frote bellement, et presse tant qu’il soit assouagiez;	And if there is great heat after the resetting of the joint, and it moves, then bathe it and rub it gently, and press until it is soothed.
ou tu met sus la jointure une naige de mouton grasse, puis la laisse I jor et une nuit, puis l’oste, et lou fai entrer ou bain;	Or you put a greasy wool cloth on the joint, then leave it for a day and a night, then remove it, and let it enter into the bath.
et quant il sue, se li frote la jointure tempreement, puis remet la naige sus, et puis entre ou bain;	And when it sweats, rub the joint moderately, then put the wool cloth back on, and then enter the bath;
et ensi fai II fois ou III, tant qu’il soit sanez;	And thus do it two or three times until it is healed.
et se tu vues, si met sus fien de vaiche moiste chaufeit avec burre, et l’estrain sus;	And if you see [that the joint is still not healed], then put on a hot moist cloth made with butter, and bind it tightly.
si revenra a sa disposition.	If it returns to its state
li dislocation de la main	Dislocation of the hand
Li jointure de la main desalue, et li revenue est legiere, plus que les autres jointures.	The dislocated joint of the hand returns, and the return is easier than with other joints.
Toutevoie, il la covient ramener au leu hastanment, en l’oure meisme qu’ele est desaluee, ainsois que li leus soit enflez, ou qu’il i viegne aposteme chaut.	Nevertheless, it must be reset quickly to its place, in the very same opening that it was dislocated, before the place becomes inflamed or an abscess forms.
Et li ramenemens si est que tu mettes la main malaide sus une tauble, et estende li ministres la main, et li mires la mette igal, ensi que il mette sa paume sus l’aparance de la jointure, et la boute tant qu’elle reviegne.	And the resetting is done by placing the dislocated hand on a table, extending the hand of the assistant, and the physician pressing down evenly until it returns.
Toutevoie, il covient que vos regardez s’il est bien a leu;	Nevertheless, you must ensure that it is properly in place;
adonc mette li malaides lou dos de sa main sus une tauble a l’estension et au ramenement.	Then the patient places the back of their hand on a table at full extension and reset.
Et se li dislocations est au dos de la main, si mette li malaides son dos de sa main sus la tauble, et li mires mette sa main sus cele apparance de la jointure.	And if the dislocation is at the back of the hand, then the patient places the back of their hand on the table, and the physician places his hand upon that appearance of the joint.
S’elle revient maintenant, c’est bien.	If it returns now, that is good.
Se ce non, si l’estrain d’emplaustres apaisans apostemes chaus, et lou laisse ensi sens rencomencier.	If not, then apply soothing emplasters to alleviate heat and swelling, and leave it thus without restarting the procedure.
Et s’il ne le puet soffrir, et tu ne la pues mettre au leu aprés aucuns jors, si demore li jointure torte;	And if he cannot endure it, and you are unable to place it in its proper position even after several days, then the joint remains dislocated.
et ne nuist niant au malaide fuer que tant que li mains est amoillie, et ne puet estraindre aucune chose a tout:	And let no harm come to the patient from this cautery until the hand is weakened, and it can grasp nothing.
adonc saiches que li nerf sont copez, ou li artere;	Then know that the nerve is cut or the artery.
si n’i a autre engien fuer que d’estraindre par cautere delez le cas, et par aventure n’i vaut autre chose.	If there is no other means to burn by fire near the case, then perhaps nothing else will help.
Et quant li mains est au leu, si met sus l’emplaustre que nos avons dit, puis l’estrain et le laisse .v. jors, puis le deslie et laisse ensi.	"And when the hand is in its place, put on the dressing that we have said, then bind it and leave it for five days, then untie it and let it remain thus."
Et s’il ne la puet bien movoir, et il i a aucune grieteit, si la moille d’aigue chaude, et le frote tant qu’il soit sanez.	"And if he cannot move it well, and there is some stiffness, then make him warm water compresses, and rub him until he is free."
de la dislocation des dois de la main	"on the dislocation of the fingers of the hand"
Aucune fois sont desaluez li doi de la main a chescune part, aucune fois au dos de la palme ou au ventre;	Sometimes both sides of the hand are dislocated, sometimes at the back of the palm or the front.
adonques estent le doi, et boute la dislocation a tes pouchés tant qu’il reviegne, puis sostien lou chief dou doi, et le pent vers la partie ou il est desjoins;	Then straighten the hand and push the dislocation into your pouch until it returns, then hold the head of the hand and bend it towards the side where it was dislocated.
et le laisse II jors, et puis le met igal celui jor;	And leave it for two days, then put it even on that day;
et de nut le lie, si com nos avons dit, et lou deslie de jor, et lou fai movoir, et le relie la nut;	and bind it tightly as we have said, both during the day and night, and when moving it, and re-bind it tightly.
et fai ce sovent, tant qu’il soit estroit, et tout ausi fai, se il est desaluez au ventre de la main, et fai si com tu as fait ci devant, tant qu’il soit sanez;	And do this frequently until it is tight, and do the same if it is dislocated on the front of the hand, doing as you have done here until it is healed.
et tout ausi fai, quant il est desaluez d’autre part.	And likewise does he, when it is dislocated elsewhere.
dou desaluement de l’eschinee dou dos	"on the dislocation of the shoulder blade of the back"
Quant l’eschinee dou dos ou dou col est desaluee, ou il en i a plusors desaluees, si n’i a point de cure, car li mors haste le malaide.	When the sciatica of the back or neck is dislocated, or if there are many dislocations, there is no treatment, for the patient hastens his death.
Et li signes si est que li egestions saut fuer sens volunteit, ne ne la puet tenir, et maintes fois sont mollifiez aucun membre, ou les II cuixes ou li dui bras ou I.	And the sign is that evacuations happen involuntarily, and he cannot control them. Often some limb becomes limp, either both thighs or both arms.
Et maintes fois se muet li eschinee a IIII pars;	And often the backbone moves in four parts;
celle qui se muet au derrier si est apelee «gilbositez»:	That which moves at the back is called "gilbositez":
li cure si est que tu rewarde se li gilbositez est venue d’enfance:	The treatment for this is that you should examine whether the gilbositez came from childhood:
si n’i ait point de cure ne de sanation dou tot.	If there is no cure or healing of it at all.
Et celle que vient de cheoir ou de percussions ou de semblans choses, dirent li ancien manieres de cures par grans paroles, ou il n’a mie en toutes grant profit;	And that which comes from falls, blows, or similar things; the old masters describe various ways of treating it with grand words, but there is no great benefit in all of them.
mais je l’ai abregiet selonc mon entention, et ai formez estrumens en diverses manieres.	But I have abbreviated it according to my intention and made tools in various forms.
Je dis que en la gilbositeit que vient au pis devant, nen a engien ne santeit;	I say that in the gilbositez which comes at the front of the chest, there is no healing.
et ausi cele que vient droitement en II costez, et ne puet on curer fuers que celi proprement qui vient au dos, si com je dis;	And also that which comes directly into both sides; and one can only cure those properly that come to the back, as I say.
et est que li malaides soit estendus sus sa faice en I leu igal, et ait de l’estrain desoz lui, qu’il ne se blece;	And it is necessary for the patient to lie on their back evenly on a level surface, with restraint underneath them so they do not become bruised.
puis fiche I tison au chief en terre forment, et I autre as piez, et lie un liien pardesoz les asseles dou malaide, et I autre as hainches, et as genous, et as chevilles;	Then plant one stake firmly at the head of the bed and another at the feet, and tie a rope around the patient's thighs, another at the hips, knees, and ankles.
et dui ministre saichent les liiens, li uns au chief et li autres as piez, parmi les II tisons;	And two assistants hold the ropes, one at the head and the other at the feet, between the two stakes
et soient bien fermez, li tison si com nos avons dit, et li mires mette ses paumes sus l’espinee forment, tant qu’ele reviegne.	and let them be securely tied, with the stake firmly planted as we have said, and the physician place their palms firmly on the spine until it returns.
Et s’elle ne revient par ceste cure, si pren une tauble de III bras de lonc, et chevé desoz la paroit, et li malaides soit en costé, et boute le chief de la tauble desoz la paroit, puis met le mileu de la tauble sus l’espinee;	And if it does not return with this treatment, take a board three fingers wide and place it under the shoulder blade while the patient is lying on their side, then insert the end of the board under the shoulder blade and place the middle of the board on the spine.
et mette li mires ses piez sus l’autre chief de la tauble, et presse bien, tant qu’il reviegne au leu;	and the physician places their feet on the other end of the board and presses firmly until it returns to its proper place
et se tu vues, si le fai au tornet qui torne a la main.	And if you see one, do it to the joint that turns towards the hand.
Et est que tu fiches II tisons au chief dou malaide d’un bras de grant, et devers les piez II autres, et ait entre chescun tison, desoure et desoz, une paume d’espaice de lonc;	And you shall place two splints at the head of the patient's injured arm, and two others towards the feet; let there be a space of one palm length between each splint above and below.
et ait en chescun tison I pertus, ou li tornet corre, et soient li tison fermement en terre, si qu’il ne se muevent;	And let each splint have one hole where the joint is located, so that they are securely placed on the ground without moving.
et entre chescuns II tisons ait I tison tornant, sor coi li liien tornent, et ait en II tornans II petis tisons d’une paume de lonc, por torner le tornet;	And between each pair of splints there should be one turning splint on which the joint turns, and this turning splint should have two small splints, each a palm length long, to turn the joint.
et puis lie lou lien qui est parmi les asseles au tornet devers le chief, et l’autre liien devers les piez a l’autre tornet, et chescuns des ministres torne son tornet a tout le liien, et li maistres mette l’espinee igal si com nos avons dit.	And then tie the bandage that is among the splints around the joint towards the head, and the other bandage around the feet at the other joint; each assistant should turn their respective joint throughout the binding process, and the master shall keep the bandage even as we have described.
Et quant elle est igalz, si met sus emplaustre desiccatif avec abun d’uef, et puis les estoupes, et puis l’estele d’une tablete de III dois de lonc, que porpreigne lou leu de la gilbositeit et la partie de l’espondile sainne, puis le lie d’un liien, si com nos avons dit, et use li malaides de norrissement subtil, tant qu’il soit sanez;	And when it is aligned, then place a drying plaster with plenty of egg, and then the bandages, and then the hot iron of a tablet of three fingers in length, which should press on the location of the gibbosity and the healthy part of the spine, then tie it with a linen, as we have said, and let the patient use subtle nourishment until they are healed.
et s’aucune chose vient en la fin de la santez, si covient aministrer medicines amollissans et asouajans, avec l’estele que nos avons dit ci devant;	And if anything happens at the end of the healing process, then it is necessary to administer softening and soothing medicines along with the hot iron that we mentioned earlier;
et aucune fois i aministre on une piece de plonc, et aucune fois vient li apparance en la derriere spondile dou dos, et cuide on que ce soit dislocations;	And sometimes one administers a piece of lead, and sometimes the appearance comes in the lower spine of the back, and it is believed to be dislocation.
et c’est li os qui apert, por coi on n’i doit mie avoir presumption:	And it is the bone that appears, therefore one must not presume anything about it:
par aventure feroit venir la mort.	For fear of bringing death upon oneself.
des dislocations de la hainche	dislocations of the hip
Saiches que as jointures de la hainche et as jointures de l’espaule ne vient fuers que dislocacions soulement, ne n’i vient mie si com as autres jointures;	Know that in the joints of the hip and the joints of the shoulder only dislocation occurs, not like other joints;
et li jointure de la hainche est desaluee selonc IIII parties:	And the hip joint is dislocated according to four parts:
dedens et defuer ,et devant et derrier;	Within and without, and before and behind.
et plus dedens c’aillors, et poc desalue devant et derrier.	And further within others, and mostly dislocated before and behind.
Et li conoissance de sa dislocations dedens si est que quant on joint la jambe malaide avec la sainne, si est plus longe, et apert plus li malaides genous que li sains, et ne puet li malaides doubler son genoil au feu;	And the sign of its dislocation within is that when the sick leg is joined with the healthy one, it appears longer, and the sick knee opens wider than the healthy one, and the sick person cannot bend their knee by the fire;
et est li leus qui est delez enflez d’aposteme chaut, por ceu que li chiés de la cuixe vient lai.	And the place near it is swollen with a hot boil because the head of the thigh comes there.
Et li signe de celui cui il vient au defuer, si est que cist accident sont contraire a ces devant.	And the sign of one that comes on the outside is that it is opposite to those that have come before
Et li signes de celui cui avient au devant, si est qu’il estent bien sa jambe selonc l’acomplissement;	And the sign of that which occurs in front is that they stretch their leg well according to its length;
toutevoie, ne double mie le genoil sens dolor, et s’on le vuet faire aler, si ne puet avant, et retient son urine, et enfle li angre, et quant il vait, si passe sus le talon.	Nevertheless, they cannot bend the knee without pain; and if one tries to make them walk, they cannot go forward, and they retain their urine, and the anus swells, and when they walk, they limp on their heel.
Et li signes de celui cui il avient derrier, si est qu’il ne puet espandre son genoil, ne doubler, et est celle jambe plus torte de l’autre, et li angre est mollifié, et est li chiés de la cuixe au leu desoz les costes.	And the sign of one that happens behind is that he cannot straighten or bend his knee, and his leg is twisted compared to the other one, and the angle is softened, and the hip joint is located beneath the ribs.
Li ramenemens de ceste semblance de dislocation si est que tu rewarde se li dislocations est anciainne, et elle demore selonc sa disposition, si n’i a nule cure;	The treatment for this type of dislocation is that if the dislocation is ancient, and it remains in its position, there is no remedy;
et n’i covient mie qu’il ait presumption.	And presumption must not be there.
Et en celi dont li dislocation est fresche, et c’est des IIII manieres de dislocation, si te haste que tu tornes la jointe, et l’esten dedens et defuer, et la muef a destre et senestre;	And in the case where dislocation is fresh, and there are four types of dislocation, you should hasten to put the joint back in place, extend it inside and outside, and move it to the right and left.
par aventure si revenra, et n’a mestier d’autre cure.	Perhaps it will return, and no other treatment is needed.
Et s’il ne revient en ceste maniere, si covient que tu apareilles I ministre fort, et esten la jambe fort a II mains, ou a I liien que soit liiez sus lou genoil;	And if it does not return in this manner, you must then seize a strong assistant, and hold the leg firmly with both hands, or have one person tie it above the knee.
et uns autres ministres estende sa main desus en teil maniere qu’il boute ses mains desoz ses asseles, puis l’estrigne d’un souef liien sus la cuixe;	and another assistant extends their hand in such a way that they place their hands under the buttocks, then grasp it with a soft bandage on the hip.
et uns autres tigne lou chief dou liien;	And another ties the head of the bandage;
et estendent amont et aval tuit a une fois, tant que li malaide soit levez de terre a une fois, et demoure pendans.	and they both pull up and down at once, so that the patient is lifted off the ground all at once, and remains hanging.
Ceste maniere d’estension si est commune as .iiij. semblances, et se li dislocation est revenue, si com nos avons dit, c’est bien.	This method of stretching applies to all four types of hip dislocation, and if the dislocation has returned to its proper position as we have said, then that is good.
Se ceu non, si covient mettre cure a sa semblance.	If this does not happen, then treat it in the same way.
Quant li dislocations est au pardedens, si covient que tu sovines le malaide sus son costeit sain, puis met le liien sus la racine de la cuixe, et le leu qui est desoz l’angre, puis estent le liien en haut devers l’angre, et devers la forcele;	When dislocation is on the right side, you must place the patient on their sound cheek, then put a sling on the root of the thigh, and the spot that is below the angle, then stretch the sling upwards towards the angle, and towards the front.
puis preigne uns autres ministres ses bras, et embraice le gros leu de la cuixe malaide, et l’estende au defuer forment:	Then take other assistants by his arms, embrace the great length of the dislocated thigh, and extend it strongly forward:
si revenra a son leu maintenant;	And it will now return to its proper place;
et ceste maniere de dislocation est plus legiere des autres.	This method is easier than others for reduction.
Et se tu ne la pues serrer en ceste maniere que nos avons dit, si covient que tu lies les II piés dou malaide ensamble d’un fort liien souef sus les II talons, et sus les II genous, et soit li jambe malaide estendue II dois plus que li autres;	And if you cannot secure it in this way that we have described, then you must bind the two feet of the patient together with a soft strong rope on both heels and both knees, and let the dislocated leg extend about two fingers more than the other
puis soit pendus sus le chief d’un fust, et soit en sus de terre II bras de lonc;	Then hang it over the top of a stick, and let it hang freely from the ground for two arm-lengths
puis comande a I ministre qu’il embraice le chief de la cuixe, et soit uns autres ministres pendans avec le malaide, qui embraice forment la cuixe, car li jointure revient maintenant hastanment.
