Then command one minister to embrace the top of the thigh, and let another minister hang with the patient, embracing the thigh strongly for the joint will now return quickly.
Et quant li dislocations est au defuer, si gise li malaides, si com nos avons dit en celui qui a gilbositeit, et estraigne I liien sus la jambe malaide proprement, et sus le peis ausi;	And when dislocation occurs at the hip joint, let the patient lie down in the manner we described for those with gibbousness; then apply traction to the limb above the injured leg properly, and also above the foot.
puis met II tisons, I au chief et I autre as piez, puis fiche I tison entre les cuixes au malaide emmi la forme;	Then place two reeds: one at the head, another at the feet; then insert one reed between the thighs of the patient in this manner;
et ait plantei de drapelz moistes entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide, puis estende chescuns ministre devers lui, et li mires mette igal a sa main la dislocation.	And place moistened cloths around to prevent burning of the patient; then extend each assistant towards him, and the surgeon shall set his hand equally upon the dislocation.
S’elle revient, c’est boin.	If it returns, it is good.
Se ce non, met sus .ie. table, et le presse ensi com nos avons dit en la gilbositeit, et gise li malaides sus le sain costeit.	If not, place a board on top and press down as we have described in the case of gibosity; let the patient lie on their healthy side.
Et quant li dislocations est devant, si covient estendre la jambe malaide hastanment, et selonc ce que j’ai dit;	And when dislocation is anterior, the injured leg must be extended hastily, as I have said;
et mette li mires sa paine d’estre sus l’angre malaide, puis presse a l’autre main, et l’estent aval devers lou genoil.	Then let the surgeon place his foot on the outer side of the injured leg and press with the other hand, then extend it down towards the knee.
Et se li dislocations est au defuer, si ne covient pas estendre le malaide aval, ne lever sus la terre, ains covient qu’il soit ausi com se li hainche estoit desaluee au defuer, si com nos avons dit dou couchement sus les II hainches;	And if dislocation is at the hip joint, it is not necessary to extend the patient downwards or lift him up; rather, he should remain as if the hip were dislocated backwards, as we have described for childbirth on both hips.
et soit sus sa faice, et li lien estendut si com nos avons dit ci devant, et doit om presser sus la jointure a la table;	And it should be placed on its face, and the bandage extended as we have said before, and one should press upon the joint against the table;
et sera a point quant li malaides estendra ses jambes, et elles seront igalz;	And it will be set when the patient extends their legs, and they will be even;
adonques ajoste les cuixes, et met l’emplaustre, et l’estrain d’un bendeil, si que li hainche ne se mueve;	Then join the thighs together, place the splint, and bind it with a bandage so that the hip does not move;
et se repose III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie, et met l’emplaustre sus;	And let him rest for three or four days, then remove it, and place the splint on top;
et se tu vois qu’elles soient igalz, si l’estrain, si com devant, et le laisse III jors;	If you see that they are even, then bind it again as before, and leave it for three days;
puis le deslie, et lou fai aler belement, tant que li membres soit confortez.	Then remove it, and let the patient go gently until the limb is comfortable.
de la dislocation dou genoil	"Of dislocation of the knee"
Li genous est desaluez selonc III manieres:	The knee is dislocated in three ways:
c’est a savoir, dedens et defuer, et derrier;	That is to say, inward, outward, and backward;
et ne desalue point devant.	And it does not dislocate forward.
Et li signes si est que tu comande au malaide qu’il plie sa jambe a sa cuixe, et s’ele ne s’aert a sa cuixe, saiches qu’il est desaluez;	And the sign is that you tell the patient to bend their leg towards their thigh, and if it does not bend easily, know that it is dislocated;
et li restauration de toutes si est que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et estende sa jambe s’il puet, et li met ton dos sus sa faice, et met son piet sus tes piez;	And the restoration of all these is that you make the patient sit up straight, and extend his leg if possible, and place your back against his face, and put his foot on your feet.
puis pren son genoil a tes paumes, et retrai entre tes dois, puis plie les II costez dou genoil forment;	Then grasp his knee with your palms, draw it between your thighs, then bend both sides of the knee forcefully;
et uns autres ministres estende son piet, tant que li genous reviegne a son leu, et li signes est qu’il aert bien sa jambe a sa cuixe legierement;	And another assistant extends his foot until the knee returns to its place; and the sign that it is correctly reset is that he can move his leg easily against his thigh.
et met l’emplastre sus, et fai aerdre la jambe a la cuixe, et les loie ensamble fort III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie;	Then apply the plaster and bind the leg to the thigh tightly with bandages for three or four days, then release.
et ne se travaille mie li malaides d’aler, tant que li membres soit confortez.	And do not let the patient walk until the limb is strengthened.
Et se li membres n’est a point, si aministre estendement fort, si com nos avons dit en la cure de la hainche, tant qu’il soit sanez	And if the limb isn't straight, then extend it firmly as we have said in the treatment of the thigh until it is aligned
de la dislocation dou talon	"Of dislocation of the heel"
Li talons est aucune fois esmeus, et aucune fois desaluez plenement, et dedens et defuer.	"The heel can sometimes be dislocated and sometimes completely dislocated, both inward and outward."
Et li signes si est que li cheville est enflee, et tent avant a la partie ou elle est desaluee:	And the sign of this is that the ankle is swollen and sticks out on the side where it was dislocated:
li ramenemens si est legier, et le doit on estendre legierement a ses mains quant il est esmeus soulement.	The reset will be easy, and one should easily extend the arm at its hands when it is only shaken.
Et quant il est desaluez dou tot, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et le tigne I ministres fors par la jambe, desus la cheville;	And when it is dislocated entirely, then you must make the patient sit up straight, and tie one leg of the attendants firmly above the ankle.
puis trai le piet a toi a ta main destre, et puis a la senestre II fois, puis l’estent en haut, et boute bellement lou piet en haut;	Then pull the foot towards you with your right hand, then with your left twice, then lift it up and gently place the foot back in its original position.
et fai ce II fois, si com nos avons dit, em boutant et en traiant lou piet;	Do this twice, as we have said, pulling and pushing the foot.
s’elle revient, c’est bien;	If it returns to its proper place, that is good.
se ce non, si rencomence l’ovraige, car il revient;	But if not, start again, for it will dislocate again.
et s’il ne puet revenir ensi, si fai gesir lou malaide sor son dos sus terre, et fiche I passeil fermement en terre entre ses cuixes, et lie drapelz entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide;	And if it cannot be returned in this way, then make the patient lie on their back on the ground, and firmly plant a pole in the earth between their thighs, tying cloths around so that the patient is not injured.
puis teigne li ministres la cuixe, et uns autres ministres estende lou piet a ses mains ou a I liien, k’il lie sus le col dou piet;	Then have the attendants hold the thigh, and another attendant stretch out the foot at the patient's hands or feet so that it is held in place.
puis estende chescuns ministres igalment, et li passelz soit adés entre les cuixes dou malaide por retenir le malaide quant on l’estent;	Then each attendant stretches out equally, and the pole should always be between the patient's thighs to hold the patient steady when lifting them.
puis mette li mires igal la dislocation a ses mains, et uns autres ministres teigne la jambe sainne au desoz, et li dislocation revenra hastanment.	Then let the physician set the dislocation evenly with his hands, and another assistant grasp the healthy leg below, and the dislocation will return quickly.
Et quant elle iert a point, si met l’emplastre et estoupes sus, et l’estrain forment, et lie lou piet a la jambe, et warde les ners qui sont sus la cheville derrier, que li liiens ne soit trop estrois;	And when it is in place, apply the plaster and dressings, press firmly, and bind the foot to the leg; beware the nerves that are above the ankle behind, so the bandage is not too tight.
puis le laisse II jors ou III, et se li liiens amolist, si l’estrain;	Then let it rest for two or three days, and if the binding loosens, then press harder;
puis le deslie au tier jor ou au quart, et deffent a aler lou malaide par IIII jors;	Then untie on the third or fourth day, and forbid the patient from walking for four days.
et s’il va devant cel termine, ce n’est mie seurtez qu’il ne desalue encor.	And if they walk before this time, it is not certain that it will not dislocate again.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si covient que tu l’apaises, si com nos avons dit autre part, tant qu’il soit sanez.	"And if inflammation occurs afterwards, you must calm it as we have said elsewhere until it is healed."
des dois	"of the fingers"
Quant li doi sont desaluez, si les covient bellement estendre sens travail, et c’est legiere chose.	"When the fingers are dislocated, they should be gently extended without force, and this is an easy matter."
Et se li dislocations est en aucun nout dou dos dou piet, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide sus I leu plain ou sus .ie. table tot droit, et met ton piet sus ce qui apert de ces jointures, puis presse a ton piet forment, tant qu’il reviegne;	And if the dislocation is in any of the joints at the back of the foot, then make the patient sit on a flat surface or on two boards laid straight, and place your foot over what opens from these joints; then press firmly with your foot until it returns.
et quant il est igalz, et il n’i apert nient, si met desoz la plante dou piet une table a II chiés, puis l’estrain forment, et le laisse III jors, puis le deslie;	And when it is aligned, and there appears nothing, then place under the sole of the foot a board at two inches, then press firmly, and leave for three days, then release.
et le fai reposer, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And let him rest until he is healed.
de plaie et de dislocation ensamble	"of wound and dislocation together"
Quant plaie vient avec la dislocation, et on la vuet restorer, maintes fois avient que li malaides muert:	When wound comes with dislocation, and one wishes to restore it, often the patient dies:
si ne soies mie presumptuous en la cure, se tu n’es saiges en l’art et tu ne l’as useit longement, et se tu n’es pitous et misericors et tardis, ne mie hardis;	Do not be overly confident in treating it if you are not skilled in the art and have not practiced it for a long time, nor should you be hasty rather than merciful.
et use au comencement de choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et laisse le malaide en la main Deu, se tu n’i vois esperance de santeit;	Use cooling remedies at the beginning to calm heat, and leave the patient in God's hands if you see no hope of recovery.
et quant tu i vois esperance, si ramoinne maintenant le membre au leu, ainsois que li apostemes chaus i viegne;	And when you see hope, reset the limb now before the hot abscess arrives.
et quant li membres est a leu, si aministre choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et cure la plaie, si com il covient, d’oignemens desiccatis;	When the limb is in place, apply cooling remedies for the hot abscess, and dress the wound with drying ointments as necessary.
et se avec la dislocation a brisure, et os menus desevrez, si les oste, et fai ce que nos avons dit en maladies simples;	And if with the dislocation there is fracture, and small bones dislocated, then set them, and do as we have said in simple diseases;
et te garde d’entrer en voie de paour, selonc ce que j’ai dit, car ce te vaut mues selonc ton Creator, et por la saveteit de t’arme et de ton cors.	And keep yourself from the path of fear, as I have said, for you will move according to your Creator, and for the sake of your knowledge and body.
